Chapter_Header: 1
Verse_Ch: 1:1 起初神创造诸天与地， ###EN### In the beginning God created the heavens and the earth.
Verse_Ch: 1:2 而地变为荒废空虚，渊面黑暗。神的灵覆罩在水面上。 ###EN### But the earth became waste and emptiness, and darkness was on the surface of the deep, and the Spirit of God was brooding upon the surface of the waters.
Verse_Ch: 1:3 神说，要有光，就有了光。 ###EN### And God said, Let there be light; and there was light.
Verse_Ch: 1:4 神看光是好的，就把光暗分开了。 ###EN### And God saw that the light was good, and God separated the light from the darkness.
Verse_Ch: 1:5 神称光为昼，称暗为夜；有晚上，有早晨，这是第一日。 ###EN### And God called the light Day, and the darkness He called Night. And there was evening and there was morning, one day.
Verse_Ch: 1:6 神说，诸水之间要有广阔的空间，将水与水分开。 ###EN### And God said, Let there be an expanse in the midst of the waters, and let it separate the waters from the waters.
Verse_Ch: 1:7 神就造出天空，将天空以下的水，与天空以上的水分开；事就这样成了。 ###EN### And God made the expanse and separated the waters which were under the expanse from the waters which were above the expanse, and it was so.
Verse_Ch: 1:8 神称天空为天；有晚上，有早晨，是第二日。 ###EN### And God called the expanse Heaven. And there was evening and there was morning, a second day.
Verse_Ch: 1:9 神说，天以下的水要聚在一处，使旱地露出来；事就这样成了。 ###EN### And God said, Let the waters under the heavens be gathered together into one place, and let the dry land appear; and it was so.
Verse_Ch: 1:10 神称旱地为地，称水的聚处为海；神看是好的。 ###EN### And God called the dry land Earth, and the gathering together of the waters He called Seas; and God saw that it was good.
Verse_Ch: 1:11 神说，地要长出青草，和结种子的菜蔬，并结果子的树木，各从其类，果子都包着核；事就这样成了。 ###EN### And God said, Let the earth sprout grass, herbs yielding seed, and fruit trees bearing fruit according to their kind with their seed in them upon the earth; and it
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: was so.
Verse_Ch: 1:12 于是地生出青草，和结种子的菜蔬，各从其类，并结果子的树木，各从其类，果子都包着核；神看是好的。 ###EN### And the earth brought forth grass, herbs yielding seed according to their kind, and trees bearing fruit with their seed in them according to their kind; and God saw
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: that it was good.
Verse_Ch: 1:13 有晚上，有早晨，是第三日。 ###EN### And there was evening and there was morning, a third day.
Verse_Ch: 1:14 神说，天上穹苍之中要有光体，可以分昼夜，作记号，定节令、日子、年岁； ###EN### And God said, Let there be light-bearers in the expanse of heaven to separate the day from the night, and let them be for signs and for seasons and for days
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: and years;
Verse_Ch: 1:15 并要发光在天上穹苍之中，普照在地上；事就这样成了。 ###EN### And let them be light-bearers in the expanse of heaven to give light on the earth; and it was so.
Verse_Ch: 1:16 于是神造了两个大的光体，大的管昼，小的管夜；又造众星。 ###EN### And God made the two great light-bearers, the greater light-bearer to rule the day and the lesser light-bearer to rule the night, and the stars.
Verse_Ch: 1:17 就把这些光体摆设在天上穹苍之中，普照在地上， ###EN### And God set them in the expanse of heaven to give light on the earth
Verse_Ch: 1:18 管理昼夜，分别光暗；神看是好的。 ###EN### And to rule over the day and over the night and to separate the light from the darkness, and God saw that it was good.
Verse_Ch: 1:19 有晚上，有早晨，是第四日。 ###EN### And there was evening and there was morning, a fourth day.
Verse_Ch: 1:20 神说，水要多多滋生有生命的物；要有禽鸟飞在地面以上，天空之中。 ###EN### And God said, Let the waters swarm with swarms of living animals, and let birds fly above the earth in the open expanse of heaven.
Verse_Ch: 1:21 神就创造大鱼，和水中所滋生各样有生命的动物，各从其类；又创造各样飞鸟，各从其类；神看是好的。 ###EN### And God created the great sea creatures and every living animal that moves, with which the waters swarmed, according to their kind, and every winged bird
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: according to its kind; and God saw that it was good.
Verse_Ch: 1:22 神就赐福给这一切，说，要繁衍增多，充满海中的水；禽鸟也要增多在地上。 ###EN### And God blessed them, saying, Be fruitful and multiply, and fill the waters in the seas, and let the birds multiply on the earth.
Verse_Ch: 1:23 有晚上，有早晨，是第五日。 ###EN### And there was evening and there was morning, a fifth day.
Verse_Ch: 1:24 神说，地要生出有生命的物，各从其类；牲畜、爬物、走兽，各从其类；事就这样成了。 ###EN### And God said, Let the earth bring forth living animals according to their kind, cattle and creeping things and animals of the earth according to their kind; and it
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: was so.
Verse_Ch: 1:25 于是神造出走兽，各从其类；牲畜各从其类；地上一切爬物，各从其类；神看是好的。 ###EN### And God made the animals of the earth according to their kind and the cattle according to their kind and everything that creeps on the ground according to its
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: kind, and God saw that it was good.
Verse_Ch: 1:26 神说，我们要按着我们的形像，照着我们的样式造人，使他们管理海里的鱼、空中的鸟、地上的牲畜、和全地、并地上所爬的一切爬物。 ###EN### And God said, Let Us make man in Our image, according to Our likeness; and let them have dominion over the fish of the sea and over the birds of heaven and
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: over the cattle and over all the earth and over every creeping thing that creeps upon the earth.
Verse_Ch: 1:27 神就按着自己的形像创造人，乃是按着神的形像创造他；创造他们有男有女。 ###EN### And God created man in His own image; in the image of God He created him; male and female He created them.
Verse_Ch: 1:28 神就赐福给他们；又对他们说，要繁衍增多，遍满地面，并制伏这地，也要管理海里的鱼、空中的鸟、和地上各样行动的活物。 ###EN### And God blessed them; and God said to them, Be fruitful and multiply, and fill the earth and subdue it, and have dominion over the fish of the sea and over the
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: birds of heaven and over every living thing that moves upon the earth.
Verse_Ch: 1:29 神说，看哪，我将遍地上各样结种子的菜蔬，和各样结有核果子的树，赐给你们作食物。 ###EN### And God said, Behold, I have given you every herb yielding seed that is on the surface of all the earth and every tree which has fruit yielding seed; it shall be for
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: you as food.
Verse_Ch: 1:30 至于地上各样的走兽和空中各样的飞鸟，并各样爬在地上有生命的物，我将青草赐给它们作食物；事就这样成了。 ###EN### And to every animal of the earth and to every bird of heaven and to everything that creeps upon the earth, in which is a living soul, I have given every green herb
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: for food; and it was so.
Verse_Ch: 1:31 神看一切所造的都甚好；有晚上，有早晨，是第六日。 ###EN### And God saw everything that He had made, and indeed, it was very good. And there was evening and there was morning, the sixth day.
Chapter_Header: 2
Verse_Ch: 2:1 天地万物都造齐了。 ###EN### Thus the heavens and the earth and all their host were finished.
Verse_Ch: 2:2 到第七日，神造作的工已经完毕，就在第七日歇了祂一切造作的工，安息了。 ###EN### And on the seventh day God finished His work which He had done, and He rested on the seventh day from all His work which He had done.
Verse_Ch: 2:3 神赐福给第七日，将其分别为圣，因为在这日神歇了祂一切创造和造作的工，就安息了。 ###EN### And God blessed the seventh day and sanctified it because in it He rested from all His work which God had created and made.
Verse_Ch: 2:4 诸天与地创造的来历，乃是这样。在耶和华神造地造天的日子， ###EN### These are the generations of the heavens and of the earth when they were created. When Jehovah God made earth and heaven,
Verse_Ch: 2:5 地上还没有草木，田间的菜蔬还没有长起来，因为耶和华神还没有降雨在地上，也没有人耕地。 ###EN### And no plant of the field was yet in the earth, and no herb of the field had yet sprung up-for Jehovah God had not caused it to rain upon the earth, and there
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: was not a man to work the ground,
Verse_Ch: 2:6 只有雾气从地上腾，滋润遍地。 ###EN### But a mist went up from the earth and watered the whole surface of the ground -
Verse_Ch: 2:7 耶和华神用地上的尘土塑造人，将生命之气吹在他鼻孔里，人就成了活的魂。 ###EN### Jehovah God formed man with the dust of the ground and breathed into his nostrils the breath of life, and man became a living soul.
Verse_Ch: 2:8 耶和华神在东方的伊甸栽植了一个园子，把所塑造的人安放在那里。 ###EN### And Jehovah God planted a garden in Eden, in the east; and there He put the man whom He had formed.
Verse_Ch: 2:9 耶和华神使各样的树从地里长出来，可以悦人的眼目，也好作食物；园子当中有生命树，还有善恶知识树。 ###EN### And out of the ground Jehovah God caused to grow every tree that is pleasant to the sight and good for food, as well as the tree of life in the middle of the
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: garden and the tree of the knowledge of good and evil.
Verse_Ch: 2:10 有一道河从伊甸流出来滋润那园子，从那里分为四道。 ###EN### And a river went forth from Eden to water the garden, and from there it divided and became four branches.
Verse_Ch: 2:11 第一道名叫比逊，就是环绕哈腓拉全地的，在那里有金子。 ###EN### The name of the first is Pishon; it is the one that goes around the whole land of Havilah, where there is gold.
Verse_Ch: 2:12 并且那地的金子是好的；在那里又有珍珠和红玛瑙。 ###EN### And the gold of that land is good; bdellium and onyx stone are there.
Verse_Ch: 2:13 第二道河名叫基训，就是环绕古实全地的。 ###EN### And the name of the second river is Gihon; it is the one that goes around the whole land of Cush.
Verse_Ch: 2:14 第三道河名叫希底结，流在亚述的东边。第四道河就是伯拉河。 ###EN### And the name of the third river is Hiddekel; it is the one that goes east of Assyria. And the fourth river is the Euphrates.
Verse_Ch: 2:15 耶和华神将那人安置在伊甸园，使他耕种看守。 ###EN### And Jehovah God took the man and put him in the garden of Eden to work it and to keep it.
Verse_Ch: 2:16 耶和华神吩咐那人说，园中各样树上的果子，你可以随意吃， ###EN### And Jehovah God commanded the man, saying, Of every tree of the garden you may eat freely,
Verse_Ch: 2:17 只是善恶知识树上的果子，你不可吃，因为你吃的日子必定死。 ###EN### But of the tree of the knowledge of good and evil, of it you shall not eat; for in the day that you eat of it you shall surely die.
Verse_Ch: 2:18 耶和华神说，那人独居不好，我要为他造一个帮助者作他的配偶。 ###EN### And Jehovah God said, It is not good for the man to be alone; I will make him a helper as his counterpart.
Verse_Ch: 2:19 耶和华神把祂用土所造的野地各样走兽，和空中各样飞鸟，都带到那人面前，看他叫什么；那人怎样叫各样的活物，那就是它的名。 ###EN### And Jehovah God formed from the ground every animal of the field and every bird of heaven, and brought them to the man to see what he would call them; and
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: whatever the man called any living animal, that was its name.
Verse_Ch: 2:20 那人便给一切的牲畜、空中的飞鸟、和野地各样的走兽都起了名，只是亚当没有找到一个帮助者作他的配偶。 ###EN### And the man gave names to all cattle and to the birds of heaven and to every animal of the field, but for Adam there was not found a helper as his counterpart.
Verse_Ch: 2:21 耶和华神使那人沉睡，他就睡了，于是取了他的一条肋骨，又把肉在原处合起来。 ###EN### And Jehovah God caused a deep sleep to fall upon the man, and he slept; and He took one of his ribs and closed up the flesh in its place.
Verse_Ch: 2:22 耶和华神就用那人身上所取的肋骨，建造成一个女人，领她到那人跟前。 ###EN### And Jehovah God built the rib, which He had taken from the man, into a woman and brought her to the man.
Verse_Ch: 2:23 那人说，这一次这是我骨中的骨，肉中的肉，可以称这为女人，因为这是从男人身上取出来的。 ###EN### And the man said, This time this is bone of my bones And flesh of my flesh; This one shall be called Woman Because out of Man this one was taken.
Verse_Ch: 2:24 因此，人要离开父母，与妻子联合，二人成为一体。 ###EN### Therefore a man shall leave his father and his mother and shall cleave to his wife, and they shall become one flesh.
Verse_Ch: 2:25 当时那人和他妻子，二人赤身露体，彼此并不觉得羞耻。 ###EN### And both the man and his wife were naked and were not ashamed before each other.
Chapter_Header: 3
Verse_Ch: 3:1 耶和华神所造的，惟有蛇比田野一切的活物更狡猾。蛇对女人说，神岂是真说，你们不可吃园中所有树上的果子么？ ###EN### Now the serpent was more crafty than every other animal of the field which Jehovah God had made. And he said to the woman, Did God really say, You shall not
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: eat of any tree of the garden?
Verse_Ch: 3:2 女人对蛇说，园中树上的果子，我们可以吃， ###EN### And the woman said to the serpent, Of the fruit of the trees of the garden we may eat;
Verse_Ch: 3:3 惟有园当中那棵树上的果子，神曾说，你们不可吃，也不可摸，免得你们死。 ###EN### But of the fruit of the tree which is in the middle of the garden, God has said, You shall not eat of it, nor shall you touch it, lest you die.
Verse_Ch: 3:4 蛇对女人说，你们不一定死； ###EN### And the serpent said to the woman, You shall not surely die!
Verse_Ch: 3:5 因为神知道，你们吃的日子眼睛就开了，你们便如神知道善恶。 ###EN### For God knows that in the day you eat of it your eyes will be opened, and you will become like God, knowing good and evil.
Verse_Ch: 3:6 于是女人见那棵树的果子好作食物，也悦人的眼目，且是可喜爱的，能使人有智慧，就摘下果子来吃了，又给与她一起的丈夫，她丈夫也吃了。 ###EN### And when the woman saw that the tree was good for food and that it was a delight to the eyes, and that the tree was to be desired to make oneself wise, she
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: took of its fruit and ate; and she also gave some to her husband with her, and he ate.
Verse_Ch: 3:7 他们二人的眼睛就开了，才知道自己是赤身露体的；他们便拿无花果树的叶子，为自己编作裙子。 ###EN### And the eyes of both of them were opened, and they knew that they were naked; and they sewed fig leaves together and made loincloths for themselves.
Verse_Ch: 3:8 天凉的时候，耶和华神在园中行走，那人和他妻子听见神的声音，就藏在园里的树木中，躲避耶和华神的面。 ###EN### And they heard the sound of Jehovah God walking about in the garden in the cool of the day, and the man and his wife hid themselves from the presence of
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: Jehovah God among the trees of the garden.
Verse_Ch: 3:9 耶和华神呼唤那人，对他说，你在那里？ ###EN### And Jehovah God called to the man and said to him, Where are you?
Verse_Ch: 3:10 他说，我在园中听见你的声音，我就害怕，因为我是赤身露体的；所以我藏了起来。 ###EN### And he said, I heard the sound of You in the garden, and I was afraid because I am naked; so I hid myself.
Verse_Ch: 3:11 耶和华神说，谁告诉你，你是赤身露体的呢？莫非你吃了我吩咐你不可吃的那树上的果子么？ ###EN### And He said, Who told you that you are naked? Have you eaten of the tree of which I commanded you not to eat?
Verse_Ch: 3:12 那人说，你所赐给我，与我一起的女人，她把那树上的果子给我，我就吃了。 ###EN### And the man said, The woman whom You gave to be with me, she gave me fruit from the tree, and I ate.
Verse_Ch: 3:13 耶和华神对女人说，你作的是什么事？女人说，那蛇诱骗我，我就吃了。 ###EN### And Jehovah God said to the woman, What is this that you have done? And the woman said, The serpent deceived me, and I ate.
Verse_Ch: 3:14 耶和华神对蛇说，你既作了这事，就必受咒诅，比一切的牲畜和田野的活物更甚。你必用肚子行走，终身吃土。 ###EN### And Jehovah God said to the serpent, Because you have done this, You are cursed more than all the cattle And more than all the animals of the field: Upon your
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: stomach you will go, And dust you will eat All the days of your life.
Verse_Ch: 3:15 我又要叫你和女人彼此为仇，你的后裔和女人的后裔也彼此为仇；女人的后裔要伤你的头，你要伤他的脚跟。 ###EN### And I will put enmity Between you and the woman And between your seed and her seed; He will bruise you on the head, But you will bruise him on the heel.
Verse_Ch: 3:16 又对女人说，我必多多加增你怀胎的苦楚，你生产儿女必受苦楚；你必恋慕你丈夫，你丈夫必管辖你。 ###EN### To the woman He said, I will greatly multiply Your pain in your childbearing; In pain you will bring forth children. And your desire will be to your husband, And he
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: will rule over you.
Verse_Ch: 3:17 又对亚当说，你既听妻子的话，吃了我所吩咐你不可吃的那树上的果子，地必因你的缘故受咒诅；你必终身劳苦，才能从地里得吃的。 ###EN### And to Adam He said, Because you listened to the voice of your wife and have eaten of the tree concerning which I commanded you, saying, You shall not eat of
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: it; Cursed is the ground because of you; In toil will you eat of it All the days of your life.
Verse_Ch: 3:18 地必给你长出荆棘和蒺藜来，你也要吃田间的菜蔬。 ###EN### And thorns and thistles it will bring forth for you, And you will eat the herb of the field;
Verse_Ch: 3:19 你必汗流满面才得糊口，直到你归了土，因为你是从土取出的；你本是尘土，仍要归于尘土。 ###EN### By the sweat of your face You will eat bread Until you return to the ground, Because from it you were taken; For dust you are, And to dust you shall return.
Verse_Ch: 3:20 亚当给他妻子起名叫夏娃，因为她是众生之母。 ###EN### And the man called his wife's name Eve, because she was the mother of all living.
Verse_Ch: 3:21 耶和华神为亚当和他妻子用皮子作衣服给他们穿。 ###EN### And Jehovah God made for Adam and for his wife coats of skins and clothed them.
Verse_Ch: 3:22 耶和华神说，那人已经与我们相似，知道善恶；现在恐怕他伸手又摘生命树的果子吃，就永远活着。 ###EN### And Jehovah God said, Behold, the man has become like one of Us, knowing good and evil; and now, lest he put forth his hand and take also from the tree of life
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: and eat and live forever -
Verse_Ch: 3:23 耶和华神便打发他出伊甸园去，耕种他所出自之土。 ###EN### Therefore Jehovah God sent him forth from the garden of Eden, to work the ground from which he was taken.
Verse_Ch: 3:24 于是把那人赶出去了；又在伊甸园的东边，安设基路伯和四面转动发火焰的剑，把守生命树的道路。 ###EN### So He drove the man out, and at the east of the garden of Eden He placed the cherubim and a flaming sword which turned in every direction to guard the way to
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: the tree of life.
Chapter_Header: 4
Verse_Ch: 4:1 那人和他妻子夏娃同房，夏娃就怀孕，生了该隐；便说，我得了一个男子，耶和华。 ###EN### And the man knew Eve his wife, and she conceived and gave birth to Cain and said, I have acquired a man, Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 4:2 又生了该隐的弟弟亚伯。亚伯是牧羊的，该隐是耕地的。 ###EN### And again she gave birth to his brother Abel. And Abel was a tender of sheep, but Cain was a tiller of the ground.
Verse_Ch: 4:3 有一日，该隐拿地里的出产为供物献给耶和华； ###EN### And in the course of time Cain brought an offering to Jehovah from the fruit of the ground.
Verse_Ch: 4:4 亚伯也将他羊群中头生的，特别是羊的脂油献上。耶和华看中了亚伯和他的供物， ###EN### And Abel also brought an offering from the firstlings of his flock, that is, from their fat portions. And Jehovah had regard for Abel and for his offering.
Verse_Ch: 4:5 只是看不中该隐和他的供物。该隐就大大发怒，垂下脸来。 ###EN### But for Cain and for his offering He had no regard. And Cain became very angry, and his countenance fell.
Verse_Ch: 4:6 耶和华对该隐说，你为什么发怒？你为什么垂下脸来？ ###EN### And Jehovah said to Cain, Why are you angry, and why has your countenance fallen?
Verse_Ch: 4:7 你若行得好，岂不扬起脸来么？你若行得不好，罪就伏在门前；他要恋慕你，但你必须管辖他。 ###EN### If you do well, will not your countenance be lifted up? And if you do not do well, sin is crouching at the door; and his desire is for you, but you must rule over him.
Verse_Ch: 4:8 该隐对他弟弟亚伯说，我们往田间去罢。二人正在田间，该隐起来打他弟弟亚伯，把他杀了。 ###EN### And Cain said to Abel his brother, Let us go into the field. And when they were in the field, Cain rose up against Abel his brother and slew him.
Verse_Ch: 4:9 耶和华对该隐说，你弟弟亚伯在那里？他说，我不知道。我岂是看守我弟弟的么？ ###EN### Then Jehovah said to Cain, Where is Abel your brother? And he said, I do not know. Am I my brother's keeper?
Verse_Ch: 4:10 耶和华说，你作了什么事？你弟弟的血有声音从地里向我哀告。 ###EN### And He said, What have you done? The voice of your brother's blood is crying out to Me from the ground.
Verse_Ch: 4:11 地开了口，从你手里接受你弟弟的血；现在你必从这地受咒诅。 ###EN### And now you are cursed from the ground, which has opened its mouth to receive your brother's blood from your hand.
Verse_Ch: 4:12 你耕地，地不再给你效力；你必流离飘荡在地上。 ###EN### When you till the ground, it will no longer yield its strength to you. You will be a fugitive and a wanderer on the earth.
Verse_Ch: 4:13 该隐对耶和华说，我的刑罚太重，过于我所能承担的。 ###EN### And Cain said to Jehovah, My punishment is greater than I can bear.
Verse_Ch: 4:14 你今日赶逐我离开这地的面，以致我不得见你的面；我必流离飘荡在地上，凡遇见我的必杀我。 ###EN### Now You have driven me out this day from the face of the ground, and from Your face I will be hidden; and I will be a fugitive and a wanderer on the earth, and
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: whoever finds me will kill me.
Verse_Ch: 4:15 耶和华对他说，既是这样，凡杀该隐的，必遭报七倍。耶和华就在该隐身上作一个记号，免得人遇见就击杀他。 ###EN### And Jehovah said to him, Therefore whoever kills Cain, vengeance will be taken on him sevenfold. And Jehovah put a mark on Cain, so that anyone who found
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: him would not strike him.
Verse_Ch: 4:16 于是该隐离开耶和华的面，去住在伊甸东边挪得之地。 ###EN### And Cain went forth from the presence of Jehovah and dwelt in the land of Nod, east of Eden.
Verse_Ch: 4:17 该隐与妻子同房，他妻子就怀孕，生了以诺。该隐建造了一座城，并按着他儿子的名，将那城叫作以诺。 ###EN### And Cain knew his wife, and she conceived and gave birth to Enoch; and he built a city and called the name of the city after the name of his son Enoch.
Verse_Ch: 4:18 以诺生以拿，以拿生米户雅利，米户雅利生玛土撒利，玛土撒利生拉麦。 ###EN### And Irad was born to Enoch, and Irad begot Mehujael, and Mehujael begot Methushael, and Methushael begot Lamech.
Verse_Ch: 4:19 拉麦娶了两个妻子，一个名叫亚大，另一个名叫洗拉。 ###EN### And Lamech took two wives for himself: The name of the first was Adah, and the name of the second Zillah.
Verse_Ch: 4:20 亚大生雅八；雅八是居住帐棚、牧养牲畜之人的始祖。 ###EN### And Adah gave birth to Jabal; he was the father of those who dwell in tents and raise cattle.
Verse_Ch: 4:21 雅八的兄弟名叫犹八；他是一切弹琴吹箫之人的始祖。 ###EN### And his brother's name was Jubal; he was the father of all those who play the lyre and pipe.
Verse_Ch: 4:22 洗拉也生了土八该隐；他是打造各样铜铁利器的。土八该隐的妹妹是拿玛。 ###EN### And Zillah also gave birth to Tubal-cain, the forger of every cutting instrument of bronze and iron; and the sister of Tubal-cain was Naamah.
Verse_Ch: 4:23 拉麦对他的两个妻子说，亚大和洗拉，听我的声音；拉麦的妻子，听我的言语：壮年人伤我，我把他杀了；少年人打我，我把他害了。 ###EN### And Lamech said to his wives, Adah and Zillah, listen to my voice; O wives of Lamech, hearken to my speech; For I have slain a man for wounding me, Even a
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: young man for striking me.
Verse_Ch: 4:24 若杀该隐遭报七倍，杀拉麦必遭报七十七倍。 ###EN### If Cain is avenged sevenfold, Then Lamech seventy-sevenfold.
Verse_Ch: 4:25 亚当又与妻子同房；她就生了一个儿子，给他起名叫塞特，说，神给我另立了一个后裔代替亚伯，因为该隐杀了他。 ###EN### And Adam knew his wife again; and she gave birth to a son and called his name Seth; for, she said, God has appointed me another seed instead of Abel,
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: because Cain slew him.
Verse_Ch: 4:26 塞特也生了一个儿子，起名叫以挪士。在那时候，人开始呼求耶和华的名。 ###EN### And to Seth also a son was born, and he called his name Enosh. At that time men began to call upon the name of Jehovah.
Chapter_Header: 5
Verse_Ch: 5:1 亚当的后代记在下面。当神创造亚当的日子，乃是按着祂的样式造的。 ###EN### This is the book of the generations of Adam. When God created Adam, He made him in the likeness of God.
Verse_Ch: 5:2 神创造他们有男有女；在他们被创造的日子，神赐福给他们，称他们的名为亚当。 ###EN### Male and female He created them, and He blessed them and called their name Adam, on the day when they were created.
Verse_Ch: 5:3 亚当活到一百三十岁，生了一个儿子，样式和形像与自己相似，就给他起名叫塞特。 ###EN### And Adam lived one hundred thirty years and begot a son in his likeness according to his image, and he called his name Seth.
Verse_Ch: 5:4 亚当生塞特之后，又在世八百年，并且生儿生女。 ###EN### And the days of Adam after he had begotten Seth were eight hundred years, and he begot more sons and daughters.
Verse_Ch: 5:5 亚当共活了九百三十岁就死了。 ###EN### And all the days that Adam lived were nine hundred thirty years, and he died.
Verse_Ch: 5:6 塞特活到一百零五岁，生了以挪士。 ###EN### And Seth lived one hundred five years and begot Enosh.
Verse_Ch: 5:7 塞特生以挪士之后，又活了八百零七年，并且生儿生女。 ###EN### And Seth lived after he had begotten Enosh eight hundred seven years, and he begot more sons and daughters.
Verse_Ch: 5:8 塞特共活了九百一十二岁就死了。 ###EN### And all the days of Seth were nine hundred twelve years, and he died.
Verse_Ch: 5:9 以挪士活到九十岁，生了该南。 ###EN### And Enosh lived ninety years and begot Kenan.
Verse_Ch: 5:10 以挪士生该南之后，又活了八百一十五年，并且生儿生女。 ###EN### And Enosh lived after he had begotten Kenan eight hundred fifteen years, and he begot more sons and daughters.
Verse_Ch: 5:11 以挪士共活了九百零五岁就死了。 ###EN### And all the days of Enosh were nine hundred five years, and he died.
Verse_Ch: 5:12 该南活到七十岁，生了玛勒列。 ###EN### And Kenan lived seventy years and begot Mahalalel.
Verse_Ch: 5:13 该南生玛勒列之后，又活了八百四十年，并且生儿生女。 ###EN### And Kenan lived after he had begotten Mahalalel eight hundred forty years, and he begot more sons and daughters.
Verse_Ch: 5:14 该南共活了九百一十岁就死了。 ###EN### And all the days of Kenan were nine hundred ten years, and he died.
Verse_Ch: 5:15 玛勒列活到六十五岁，生了雅列。 ###EN### And Mahalalel lived sixty-five years and begot Jared.
Verse_Ch: 5:16 玛勒列生雅列之后，又活了八百三十年，并且生儿生女。 ###EN### And Mahalalel lived after he had begotten Jared eight hundred thirty years, and he begot more sons and daughters.
Verse_Ch: 5:17 玛勒列共活了八百九十五岁就死了。 ###EN### And all the days of Mahalalel were eight hundred ninety-five years, and he died.
Verse_Ch: 5:18 雅列活到一百六十二岁，生了以诺。 ###EN### And Jared lived a hundred sixty-two years and begot Enoch.
Verse_Ch: 5:19 雅列生以诺之后，又活了八百年，并且生儿生女。 ###EN### And Jared lived after he had begotten Enoch eight hundred years, and he begot more sons and daughters.
Verse_Ch: 5:20 雅列共活了九百六十二岁就死了。 ###EN### And all the days of Jared were nine hundred sixty-two years, and he died.
Verse_Ch: 5:21 以诺活到六十五岁，生了玛土撒拉。 ###EN### And Enoch lived sixty-five years and begot Methuselah.
Verse_Ch: 5:22 以诺生玛土撒拉之后，与神同行三百年，并且生儿生女。 ###EN### And Enoch walked with God after he had begotten Methuselah three hundred years, and he begot more sons and daughters.
Verse_Ch: 5:23 以诺共活了三百六十五岁。 ###EN### And all the days of Enoch were three hundred sixty-five years.
Verse_Ch: 5:24 以诺与神同行，神将他取去，他就不在世了。 ###EN### And Enoch walked with God, and he was not, for God took him.
Verse_Ch: 5:25 玛土撒拉活到一百八十七岁，生了拉麦。 ###EN### And Methuselah lived one hundred eighty-seven years and begot Lamech.
Verse_Ch: 5:26 玛土撒拉生拉麦之后，又活了七百八十二年，并且生儿生女。 ###EN### And Methuselah lived after he had begotten Lamech seven hundred eighty-two years, and he begot more sons and daughters.
Verse_Ch: 5:27 玛土撒拉共活了九百六十九岁就死了。 ###EN### And all the days of Methuselah were nine hundred sixty-nine years, and he died.
Verse_Ch: 5:28 拉麦活到一百八十二岁，生了一个儿子， ###EN### And Lamech lived a hundred eighty-two years and begot a son.
Verse_Ch: 5:29 给他起名叫挪亚，说，这个儿子必为我们的操作和手中的劳苦安慰我们；这操作与劳苦是因为地受了耶和华的咒诅。 ###EN### And he called his name Noah, saying, This one will give us rest from our work and from the toil of our hands, which come because of the ground which Jehovah
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: has cursed.
Verse_Ch: 5:30 拉麦生挪亚之后，又活了五百九十五年，并且生儿生女。 ###EN### And Lamech lived after he had begotten Noah five hundred ninety-five years, and he begot more sons and daughters.
Verse_Ch: 5:31 拉麦共活了七百七十七岁就死了。 ###EN### And all the days of Lamech were seven hundred seventy-seven years, and he died.
Verse_Ch: 5:32 挪亚五百岁生了闪、含、雅弗。 ###EN### And Noah was five hundred years old. And Noah begot Shem, Ham, and Japheth.
Chapter_Header: 6
Verse_Ch: 6:1 当人在地上多起来，又生女儿的时候， ###EN### And when men began to multiply on the surface of the ground, and daughters were born to them,
Verse_Ch: 6:2 神的儿子们看见人的女子美貌，就随意挑选，娶来为妻。 ###EN### The sons of God saw that the daughters of men were fair; and they took wives for themselves from all whom they chose.
Verse_Ch: 6:3 耶和华说，人既是肉体，我的灵就不永远与他相争；然而他的日子还有一百二十年。 ###EN### And Jehovah said, My Spirit will not strive with man forever, for he indeed is flesh; so his days will be one hundred twenty years.
Verse_Ch: 6:4 神的儿子们和人的女子交合生子，从那时起地上就有了拿非利人；他们就是上古英武有名的人。 ###EN### The Nephilim were on the earth in those days-and also afterward-when the sons of God came in to the daughters of men, and they gave birth to children to
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: them; these were the mighty men who were of old the men of renown.
Verse_Ch: 6:5 耶和华见人在地上罪恶甚大，心中终日所思念的尽都是恶； ###EN### And Jehovah saw that the wickedness of man was great in the earth, and that every imagination of the thoughts of his heart was only evil continually.
Verse_Ch: 6:6 耶和华就后悔造人在地上，心中忧伤。 ###EN### And Jehovah repented that He had made man on the earth, and it grieved Him in His heart.
Verse_Ch: 6:7 耶和华说，我要将所创造的人，连人带走兽、爬物、以及空中的飞鸟，都从地上除灭，因为我后悔造了他们。 ###EN### And Jehovah said, I will blot out the man whom I have created from the surface of the ground, from man to beast to creeping things to the birds of heaven; for I
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: repent that I have made them.
Verse_Ch: 6:8 但挪亚在耶和华眼前蒙恩。 ###EN### But Noah found favor in the sight of Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 6:9 挪亚的后代记在下面。挪亚是个义人，在当时的世代是个完全人；挪亚与神同行。 ###EN### These are the generations of Noah. Noah was a righteous man, blameless in his generations; and Noah walked with God.
Verse_Ch: 6:10 挪亚生了三个儿子，就是闪、含、雅弗。 ###EN### And Noah begot three sons: Shem, Ham, and Japheth.
Verse_Ch: 6:11 全地在神面前败坏，地上满了强暴。 ###EN### And the earth was corrupt before God, and the earth was filled with violence.
Verse_Ch: 6:12 神观看全地，见是败坏了；凡属肉体的人，在地上的行径都败坏了。 ###EN### And God looked on the earth, and behold, it was corrupt; for all flesh had corrupted its way upon the earth.
Verse_Ch: 6:13 神就对挪亚说，凡属肉体之人的结局，已经来到我面前；因为地上满了他们的强暴，我要把他们和地一并毁灭。 ###EN### And God said to Noah, The end of all flesh has come before Me, for the earth is filled with violence because of them; and now I am about to destroy them with
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: the earth.
Verse_Ch: 6:14 你要用歌斐木造一只方舟，里面要有隔间，方舟内外要涂上松香。 ###EN### Make yourself an ark of gopher wood; you shall make rooms in the ark and shall cover it within and without with pitch.
Verse_Ch: 6:15 方舟的造法乃是这样：要长三百肘，宽五十肘，高三十肘。 ###EN### And this is how you shall make it: The length of the ark shall be three hundred cubits, its width fifty cubits, and its height thirty cubits.
Verse_Ch: 6:16 方舟顶上要造一个透光处，高一肘；方舟的门要开在旁边；方舟要分上、中、下三层。 ###EN### You shall make an opening for light for the ark, and you shall finish it up to a cubit from the top; and you shall put the entrance of the ark in its side; you shall
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: make it with lower, second, and third stories.
Verse_Ch: 6:17 看哪，我要使洪水泛滥在地上，毁灭天下一切有血肉、有气息的；凡在地上的无一不死。 ###EN### And now I am about to bring a flood of water upon the earth to destroy from under heaven all flesh in which is the breath of life; everything that is on the earth
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: shall die.
Verse_Ch: 6:18 我却要与你立约；你同你的儿子、妻子与儿媳，都要进入方舟。 ###EN### But I will establish My covenant with you, and you shall come into the ark, you and your sons and your wife and your sons' wives with you.
Verse_Ch: 6:19 凡有血肉的活物，每样两个，有公有母，你要带进方舟，好与你一同保全生命。 ###EN### And of every living thing, of all flesh, two of every kind you shall bring into the ark to preserve them alive with you; they shall be male and female.
Verse_Ch: 6:20 飞鸟各从其类，牲畜各从其类，地上的爬物各从其类，每样两个，要到你那里，好保全生命。 ###EN### Of the birds according to their kind and of the cattle according to their kind, of every creeping thing of the ground according to its kind, two of every kind will come
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: to you in order to preserve them alive.
Verse_Ch: 6:21 至于你，要拿各样可吃的食物，积聚起来，好作你和它们的食物。 ###EN### And for your part, take some of every kind of food that is edible, and gather it to yourself, and it will be for food for you and for them.
Verse_Ch: 6:22 挪亚就这样行；凡神所吩咐的，他都照样行了。 ###EN### And Noah did this; according to all that God commanded him, so he did.
Chapter_Header: 7
Verse_Ch: 7:1 耶和华对挪亚说，你和你全家都要进入方舟；因为在这世代中，我见只有你在我面前是义的。 ###EN### Then Jehovah said to Noah, Come into the ark, you and all your household, for you alone I have seen to be righteous before Me in this generation.
Verse_Ch: 7:2 凡洁净的畜类，你要带七对公母；不洁净的畜类，你要带一对公母； ###EN### Of every clean animal you shall take with you seven pairs, a male and its female; and of the animals that are not clean two, a male and its female;
Verse_Ch: 7:3 空中的飞鸟，也要带七对公母；可以留种，活在全地上， ###EN### Also of the birds of heaven, seven pairs, male and female; to preserve their offspring alive on the surface of all the earth.
Verse_Ch: 7:4 因为再过七天，我要降雨在地上四十昼四十夜，把我所造的各种活物都从地上除灭。 ###EN### For in seven more days I will cause it to rain on the earth forty days and forty nights, and every living being that I have made I will blot out from the surface of the
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: ground.
Verse_Ch: 7:5 挪亚就遵着耶和华所吩咐的一切行了。 ###EN### And Noah did according to all that Jehovah commanded him.
Verse_Ch: 7:6 当洪水泛滥在地上的时候，挪亚正六百岁。 ###EN### And Noah was six hundred years old when the flood of waters came upon the earth.
Verse_Ch: 7:7 挪亚就同他的儿子、妻子和儿媳，都进入方舟，躲避洪水。 ###EN### And Noah and his sons and his wife and his sons' wives with him went into the ark because of the waters of the flood.
Verse_Ch: 7:8 洁净的畜类和不洁净的畜类，飞鸟并地上一切的爬物， ###EN### Of clean animals and of animals that are not clean and of birds and of everything that creeps upon the ground,
Verse_Ch: 7:9 都是一对一对的，有公有母，到挪亚那里进入方舟，正如神所吩咐挪亚的。 ###EN### Two by two they came into the ark to Noah, male and female, as God had commanded Noah.
Verse_Ch: 7:10 过了那七天，洪水泛滥在地上。 ###EN### And after the seven days the waters of the flood came upon the earth.
Verse_Ch: 7:11 当挪亚六百岁，二月十七日那一天，大渊的一切泉源都裂开了，天上的窗户也敞开了， ###EN### In the six hundredth year of Noah's life, in the second month, on the seventeenth day of the month, on that very day all the springs of the great deep burst open,
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: and the windows of heaven were opened.
Verse_Ch: 7:12 四十昼四十夜降雨在地上。 ###EN### And the rain fell upon the earth forty days and forty nights.
Verse_Ch: 7:13 正当那日，挪亚和他三个儿子闪、含、雅弗，并挪亚的妻子和三个儿媳，都进入方舟。 ###EN### On that very same day Noah and Shem and Ham and Japheth, the sons of Noah, and Noah's wife and the three wives of his sons with them entered the ark,
Verse_Ch: 7:14 他们一家，和一切走兽，各从其类，一切牲畜，各从其类，一切爬在地上的爬物，各从其类，一切禽鸟，各从其类，都进入方舟。 ###EN### They and every animal according to its kind and all the cattle according to their kind and every creeping thing that creeps upon the earth according to its kind and
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: every bird according to its kind-every bird, every winged creature.
Verse_Ch: 7:15 凡有血肉、有生命气息的，都一对一对的到挪亚那里，进入方舟。 ###EN### And they went into the ark to Noah, two by two of all flesh in which was the breath of life.
Verse_Ch: 7:16 凡有血肉进入方舟的，都是有公有母，正如神所吩咐挪亚的；耶和华就把他关在方舟里头。 ###EN### And those who went in, male and female of all flesh, went in as God had commanded him; and Jehovah shut the door behind him.
Verse_Ch: 7:17 洪水泛滥在地上四十天，水往上涨，把方舟浮起，方舟就离地升高。 ###EN### And the flood was on the earth forty days; and the waters increased and lifted up the ark, and it rose high above the earth.
Verse_Ch: 7:18 水势浩大，在地上大大上涨，方舟在水面上漂来漂去。 ###EN### And the waters prevailed and increased greatly upon the earth, and the ark went about on the surface of the waters.
Verse_Ch: 7:19 水势在地上极其浩大，普天下一切高山都淹没了。 ###EN### And when the waters had prevailed exceedingly upon the earth, all the high mountains that were under the entire heaven were covered.
Verse_Ch: 7:20 水势浩大，比山高过十五肘，山岭都淹没了。 ###EN### The waters prevailed fifteen cubits higher once the mountains were covered.
Verse_Ch: 7:21 凡在地上有血肉的动物，就是飞鸟、牲畜、走兽，和爬在地上的爬物，以及所有的人，都死了。 ###EN### And all flesh that moved upon the earth expired: birds and cattle and animals and every swarming thing that swarms upon the earth and all mankind.
Verse_Ch: 7:22 凡在旱地上，鼻孔有生命气息的，都死了。 ###EN### Everything in whose nostrils was the breath of the spirit of life, of all that was on the dry land, died.
Verse_Ch: 7:23 这样，神把地上一切的活物，连人带走兽、爬物、以及空中的飞鸟，都除灭了。这些都从地上除灭了，只留下挪亚和那些与他同在方舟里的。 ###EN### Thus He blotted out every living being that was upon the surface of the ground, from man to beast to creeping things to the birds of heaven. And they were
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: blotted out from the earth, and only Noah was left, and those who were with him in the ark.
Verse_Ch: 7:24 水势浩大，在地上共一百五十天。 ###EN### And the waters prevailed upon the earth one hundred fifty days.
Chapter_Header: 8
Verse_Ch: 8:1 神记念挪亚和方舟里同挪亚一起的一切走兽牲畜；神叫风吹地，水就渐落。 ###EN### And God remembered Noah and all the animals and all the cattle that were with him in the ark; and God made a wind pass over the earth, and the waters
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: subsided.
Verse_Ch: 8:2 深渊的泉源和天上的窗户都闭塞了，天上的雨也止住了。 ###EN### The springs of the deep and the windows of heaven were also stopped, and the rain from the heavens was restrained;
Verse_Ch: 8:3 水从地上渐退。过了一百五十天，水就渐消。 ###EN### And the waters receded steadily from upon the earth. So at the end of one hundred fifty days the waters began to diminish.
Verse_Ch: 8:4 七月十七日，方舟停在亚拉腊山上。 ###EN### And the ark came to rest in the seventh month, on the seventeenth day of the month, upon the mountains of Ararat.
Verse_Ch: 8:5 水又渐消，到十月初一日，山顶都现出来了。 ###EN### And the waters diminished steadily until the tenth month. In the tenth month, on the first day of the month, the tops of the mountains were seen.
Verse_Ch: 8:6 过了四十天，挪亚开了他所造方舟的窗户， ###EN### And at the end of forty days Noah opened the window of the ark which he had made.
Verse_Ch: 8:7 放出一只乌鸦；那乌鸦飞来飞去，直到地上的水都干了。 ###EN### And he sent out the raven; and it went out, going to and fro until the waters had dried up from the earth.
Verse_Ch: 8:8 他又放出一只鸽子，要看看水从地上退了没有。 ###EN### And he sent out the dove from him to see if the waters had abated from the surface of the ground.
Verse_Ch: 8:9 但遍地上都是水，鸽子找不着落脚之地，就回到方舟挪亚那里，挪亚伸手把鸽子接进方舟。 ###EN### But the dove found no resting place for the sole of her foot, so she returned to him to the ark; for the waters were on the surface of the whole earth. And he put
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: out his hand and took her and brought her to himself into the ark.
Verse_Ch: 8:10 他又等了七天，再把鸽子从方舟放出去。 ###EN### And he waited yet another seven days, and again he sent out the dove from the ark.
Verse_Ch: 8:11 到了晚上，鸽子回到他那里，嘴里叼着一片新拧下来的橄榄叶子，挪亚就知道地上的水退了。 ###EN### And the dove came to him toward evening time, and there in her beak was a freshly plucked olive leaf. So Noah knew that the waters had abated from the earth.
Verse_Ch: 8:12 他又等了七天，再放出鸽子，鸽子就不再回来了。 ###EN### And he waited yet another seven days and sent out the dove, and she did not return to him again.
Verse_Ch: 8:13 到挪亚六百零一岁，正月初一日，地上的水都干了。挪亚撤去方舟的盖观看，便见地面上干了。 ###EN### And in the six hundred first year, in the first month, the first day of the month, the water was dried up from the earth; and Noah removed the covering of the ark
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: and saw that now the surface of the ground was dry.
Verse_Ch: 8:14 到了二月二十七日，地就都干了。 ###EN### And in the second month, on the twenty-seventh day of the month, the earth was dry.
Verse_Ch: 8:15 神对挪亚说， ###EN### And God spoke to Noah, saying,
Verse_Ch: 8:16 你和你的妻子、儿子、儿媳都可以出方舟。 ###EN### Go forth from the ark, you and your wife and your sons and your sons' wives with you;
Verse_Ch: 8:17 在你那里凡有血肉的活物，就是飞鸟、牲畜、和一切爬在地上的爬物，都要带出来，叫它们在地上孳生，繁衍增多。 ###EN### Bring out with you every living thing that is with you of all flesh-birds and cattle and every creeping thing that creeps upon the earth-that they may swarm on the
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: earth and be fruitful and multiply upon the earth.
Verse_Ch: 8:18 于是挪亚和他的儿子、妻子、儿媳都出来了。 ###EN### So Noah went forth, as well as his sons and his wife and his sons' wives with him.
Verse_Ch: 8:19 一切走兽、爬物、飞鸟、和地上所有的动物，各从其类，也都出了方舟。 ###EN### Every animal, every creeping thing, and every bird, everything that moves upon the earth, went forth from the ark according to their families.
Verse_Ch: 8:20 挪亚为耶和华筑了一座坛，拿各类洁净的牲畜、飞鸟，献在坛上为燔祭。 ###EN### And Noah built an altar to Jehovah and took of every clean beast and of every clean bird and offered burnt offerings on the altar.
Verse_Ch: 8:21 耶和华闻了那怡爽的香气，就心里说，我不再因人的缘故咒诅地，(人从小时心里怀着恶念，)也不再按着我才行的，灭各种的活物了。 ###EN### And Jehovah smelled the satisfying fragrance; and Jehovah said in His heart, I will never again curse the ground on account of man, for the imagination of man's
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: heart is evil from his youth; nor will I ever again smite everything living as I have done.
Verse_Ch: 8:22 地还存留的时候，稼穑、寒暑、冬夏、昼夜，就永不停息了。 ###EN### Throughout all the days that earth remains, Seed time and harvest, and cold and heat, And summer and winter, and day and night Shall not cease.
Chapter_Header: 9
Verse_Ch: 9:1 神赐福给挪亚和他的儿子，对他们说，你们要繁衍增多，遍满了地。 ###EN### And God blessed Noah and his sons and said to them, Be fruitful and multiply and fill the earth.
Verse_Ch: 9:2 地上的各样走兽和空中的各样飞鸟，以及地上一切的爬物并海里一切的鱼，都必畏惧、惊怕你们；这一切都交在你们手中了。 ###EN### And the fear of you and the terror of you shall be upon every animal of the earth and upon every bird of heaven, on everything that creeps on the ground and on
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: all the fish of the sea; into your hand they are delivered.
Verse_Ch: 9:3 凡活着的动物都可以作你们的食物；这一切我都赐给你们，如同我将菜蔬赐给你们一样。 ###EN### Every moving thing that lives shall be food for you; just as I gave you the green herb, so I have given you everything.
Verse_Ch: 9:4 惟独肉带着生命，就是带着血，你们不可吃。 ###EN### But flesh with its life, that is, its blood, you shall not eat.
Verse_Ch: 9:5 你们生命的血，我必追讨。向兽，我必追讨；向人，向各人的弟兄，我也必追讨人的命。 ###EN### And indeed your lifeblood I will require; from every animal I will require it. And from every man, from every man's brother, I will require the life of man.
Verse_Ch: 9:6 凡流人血的，他的血也必被人所流，因为神造人是按自己的形像造的。 ###EN### Whoever sheds man's blood, By man shall his blood be shed, For in the image of God He made man.
Verse_Ch: 9:7 你们要繁衍增多，在地上孳生繁增。 ###EN### And you, be fruitful and multiply, Abound on the earth and multiply in it.
Verse_Ch: 9:8 神对挪亚和同他一起的儿子说， ###EN### Then God spoke to Noah and to his sons with him, saying,
Verse_Ch: 9:9 看哪，我与你们和你们的后裔立约， ###EN### And I Myself now establish My covenant with you and with your seed after you
Verse_Ch: 9:10 并与你们这里的一切活物，就是飞鸟、牲畜、走兽，凡从方舟出来地上的活物立约。 ###EN### And with every living animal that is with you: the birds, the cattle, and every animal of the earth with you, of all that came out of the ark, every animal of the earth.
Verse_Ch: 9:11 我与你们立约，凡有血肉的，不再被洪水灭绝，也不再有洪水毁坏地了。 ###EN### And I establish My covenant with you, that never again will all flesh be cut off by the waters of the flood, and never again will there be a flood to destroy the earth.
Verse_Ch: 9:12 神说，这是我与你们，并你们这里各样活物所立之约的记号，直到万代： ###EN### And God said, This is the sign of the covenant which I am making between Me and you and every living animal that is with you, for perpetual generations:
Verse_Ch: 9:13 我把虹放在云彩中，这就作我与地立约的记号。 ###EN### I set My bow in the clouds, and it shall be for a sign of a covenant between Me and the earth.
Verse_Ch: 9:14 我使云彩遮地的时候，必有虹现在云彩中； ###EN### And when I bring clouds over the earth, and the bow is seen in the clouds,
Verse_Ch: 9:15 我便记念我与你们，和各样有血肉的活物所立的约，水就再不泛滥，毁灭一切有血肉的物了。 ###EN### I will remember My covenant which is between Me and you and every living animal of all flesh, and never again will the waters become a flood to destroy all
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: flesh.
Verse_Ch: 9:16 虹必现在云彩中，我必观看，记念我与地上各样有血肉的活物所立的永约。 ###EN### And the bow will be in the clouds, and I will look upon it to remember the everlasting covenant between God and every living animal of all flesh that is upon the
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: earth.
Verse_Ch: 9:17 神对挪亚说，这就是我与地上一切有血肉之物立约的记号。 ###EN### And God said to Noah, This is the sign of the covenant which I have established between Me and all flesh that is upon the earth.
Verse_Ch: 9:18 出方舟挪亚的儿子是闪、含、雅弗；含是迦南的父亲。 ###EN### Now the sons of Noah who came forth from the ark were Shem and Ham and Japheth. And Ham was the father of Canaan.
Verse_Ch: 9:19 这是挪亚的三个儿子，他们的后裔散布在全地。 ###EN### These three were the sons of Noah, and from these the whole earth was spread over.
Verse_Ch: 9:20 挪亚作起农夫来，栽了一个葡萄园。 ###EN### And Noah began to be a farmer, and he planted a vineyard.
Verse_Ch: 9:21 他喝了园中的酒便醉了，在帐棚里赤着身子。 ###EN### And he drank of the wine and became drunk. And he uncovered himself inside his tent.
Verse_Ch: 9:22 迦南的父亲含看见他父亲赤身，就到外边告诉他的两个弟兄。 ###EN### And Ham, the father of Canaan, saw the nakedness of his father and told his two brothers outside.
Verse_Ch: 9:23 于是闪和雅弗拿件衣服搭在肩上，倒退着进去，遮盖他们父亲的赤身；他们背着脸，就没有看见父亲的赤身。 ###EN### And Shem and Japheth took a garment and laid it upon both their shoulders, and they walked backward and covered the nakedness of their father. And their
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: faces were turned backward, so that they did not see their father's nakedness.
Verse_Ch: 9:24 挪亚醒了酒，知道小儿子向他所作的事， ###EN### And Noah awoke from his wine and learned what his youngest son had done to him.
Verse_Ch: 9:25 就说，迦南当受咒诅，必给他弟兄作奴仆的奴仆。 ###EN### And he said, Cursed be Canaan: A servant of servants Shall he be to his brothers.
Verse_Ch: 9:26 又说，耶和华闪的神，是当受颂赞的；愿迦南作闪的奴仆。 ###EN### And he said, Blessed be Jehovah, The God of Shem; And let Canaan be his servant.
Verse_Ch: 9:27 愿神使雅弗扩张，使他住在闪的帐棚里；又愿迦南作他的奴仆。 ###EN### May God enlarge Japheth, And let him dwell in the tents of Shem, And let Canaan be his servant.
Verse_Ch: 9:28 洪水以后，挪亚又活了三百五十年。 ###EN### And Noah lived after the flood three hundred fifty years.
Verse_Ch: 9:29 挪亚共活了九百五十岁就死了。 ###EN### And all the days of Noah were nine hundred fifty years, and he died.
Chapter_Header: 10
Verse_Ch: 10:1 挪亚的儿子闪、含、雅弗的后代记在下面。洪水以后，他们都生了儿子。 ###EN### Now these are the generations of the sons of Noah, of Shem, Ham, and Japheth; and sons were born to them after the flood.
Verse_Ch: 10:2 雅弗的儿子是歌篾、玛各、玛代、雅完、土巴、米设、提拉。 ###EN### The sons of Japheth: Gomer and Magog and Madai and Javan and Tubal and Meshech and Tiras.
Verse_Ch: 10:3 歌篾的儿子是亚实基拿、利法、陀迦玛。 ###EN### And the sons of Gomer: Ashkenaz and Riphath and Togarmah.
Verse_Ch: 10:4 雅完的子孙是以利沙、他施、基提人、罗单人。 ###EN### And the sons of Javan: Elishah and Tarshish, Kittim and Rodanim.
Verse_Ch: 10:5 这些人的后裔，在列国的岛屿和沿海一带分地居住，各按各的方言、家族、邦国。 ###EN### From these the islands and coastal regions of the nations were separated into their lands, every one according to his tongue, according to their families, in their
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: nations.
Verse_Ch: 10:6 含的儿子是古实、麦西、弗、迦南。 ###EN### And the sons of Ham: Cush and Mizraim and Put and Canaan.
Verse_Ch: 10:7 古实的儿子是西巴、哈腓拉、撒弗他、拉玛、撒弗提迦。拉玛的儿子是示巴、底但。 ###EN### And the sons of Cush: Seba and Havilah and Sabtah and Raamah and Sabtecha. And the sons of Raamah: Sheba and Dedan.
Verse_Ch: 10:8 古实又生宁录，他是地上最早的勇士。 ###EN### And Cush begot Nimrod: He began to be a mighty one on the earth.
Verse_Ch: 10:9 他在耶和华面前是个英勇的猎户，所以有话说，像宁录在耶和华面前是个英勇的猎户。 ###EN### He was a mighty hunter before Jehovah; therefore it is said, Like Nimrod a mighty hunter before Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 10:10 他国的起头是巴别、以力、亚甲、甲尼，都在示拿地。 ###EN### And the beginning of his kingdom was Babel and Erech and Accad and Calneh, in the land of Shinar.
Verse_Ch: 10:11 他从那地出来往亚述去，建造尼尼微、利河伯、迦拉， ###EN### From that land he went into Assyria and built Nineveh and Rehoboth-ir and Calah
Verse_Ch: 10:12 和尼尼微、迦拉中间的利鲜，就是那大城。 ###EN### And Resen between Nineveh and Calah, that is, the great city.
Verse_Ch: 10:13 麦西生路低人、亚拿米人、利哈比人、拿弗土希人、 ###EN### And Mizraim begot the Ludim and the Anamim and the Lehabim and the Naphtuhim
Verse_Ch: 10:14 帕斯鲁细人、迦斯路希人、迦斐托人；从迦斯路希人出来的有非利士人。 ###EN### And the Pathrusim and the Casluhim, from which came the Philistines, and the Caphtorim.
Verse_Ch: 10:15 迦南生长子西顿，又生赫、 ###EN### And Canaan begot Sidon his firstborn and Heth
Verse_Ch: 10:16 和耶布斯人、亚摩利人、革迦撒人、 ###EN### And the Jebusites and the Amorites and the Girgashites
Verse_Ch: 10:17 希未人、亚基人、西尼人、 ###EN### And the Hivites and the Arkites and the Sinites
Verse_Ch: 10:18 亚瓦底人、洗玛利人、哈马人，后来迦南的诸族散布出去了。 ###EN### And the Arvadites and the Zemarites and the Hamathites, and afterward the families of the Canaanites were spread out.
Verse_Ch: 10:19 迦南的境界是从西顿向基拉耳的路上，直到迦萨，又向所多玛、蛾摩拉、押玛、洗扁的路上，直到拉沙。 ###EN### And the territory of the Canaanites was from Sidon, as you go toward Gerar, as far as Gaza, and as you go toward Sodom and Gomorrah and Admah and
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: Zeboiim, as far as Lasha.
Verse_Ch: 10:20 这些就是含的子孙，各按他们的家族、方言、地土、邦国。 ###EN### These are the sons of Ham, according to their families, according to their tongues, in their lands, in their nations.
Verse_Ch: 10:21 雅弗的哥哥闪，是希伯所有子孙之祖，他也生了儿子。 ###EN### And also to Shem, the father of all the children of Eber, the eldest brother of Japheth, children were born.
Verse_Ch: 10:22 闪的儿子是以拦、亚述、亚法撒、路德、亚兰。 ###EN### The sons of Shem: Elam and Asshur and Arpachshad and Lud and Aram.
Verse_Ch: 10:23 亚兰的儿子是乌斯、户勒、基帖、玛施。 ###EN### And the sons of Aram: Uz and Hul and Gether and Mash.
Verse_Ch: 10:24 亚法撒生沙拉；沙拉生希伯。 ###EN### And Arpachshad begot Shelah, and Shelah begot Eber.
Verse_Ch: 10:25 希伯生了两个儿子，一个名叫法勒，因为那时人才分地居住，法勒的兄弟名叫约坍。 ###EN### And to Eber were born two sons: The name of the one was Peleg, for in his days the earth was divided; and his brother's name was Joktan.
Verse_Ch: 10:26 约坍生亚摩答、沙列、哈萨玛非、耶拉、 ###EN### And Joktan begot Almodad and Sheleph and Hazarmaveth and Jerah
Verse_Ch: 10:27 哈多兰、乌萨、德拉、 ###EN### And Hadoram and Uzal and Diklah
Verse_Ch: 10:28 俄巴路、亚比玛利、示巴、 ###EN### And Obal and Abimael and Sheba
Verse_Ch: 10:29 阿斐、哈腓拉、约巴，这些都是约坍的儿子。 ###EN### And Ophir and Havilah and Jobab; all these were the sons of Joktan.
Verse_Ch: 10:30 他们所住的地方是从米沙直到西发，东边的山地。 ###EN### And their dwelling was from Mesha, as you go toward Sephar, the hill country of the east.
Verse_Ch: 10:31 这些就是闪的子孙，各按他们的家族、方言、地土、邦国。 ###EN### These are the sons of Shem, according to their families, according to their tongues, in their lands, according to their nations.
Verse_Ch: 10:32 这些都是挪亚三个儿子的家族，各按他们的族系、邦国。洪水以后他们在地上分为邦国。 ###EN### These are the families of the sons of Noah, according to their generations, in their nations; and from these the nations were separated on the earth after the flood.
Chapter_Header: 11
Verse_Ch: 11:1 那时，全地的人只有一种语言，都说同样的话语。 ###EN### And the whole earth had one language and the same speech.
Verse_Ch: 11:2 他们往东边迁移的时候，在示拿地遇见一片平原，就住在那里。 ###EN### And as they journeyed east, they found a plain in the land of Shinar; and they dwelt there.
Verse_Ch: 11:3 他们彼此商量说，来罢，我们作砖，把砖烧透。他们就拿砖当石头，又拿石漆当灰泥。 ###EN### And they said to one another, Come, let us make bricks and burn them thoroughly. And they had brick for stone, and they had tar for mortar.
Verse_Ch: 11:4 他们说，来罢，我们建造一座城和一座塔，塔顶通天；我们要宣扬我们的名，免得我们分散在全地上。 ###EN### And they said, Come, let us build ourselves a city and a tower whose top is in the heavens; and let us make a name for ourselves, lest we be scattered over the
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: surface of the whole earth.
Verse_Ch: 11:5 耶和华降临，要看看世人所建造的城和塔。 ###EN### And Jehovah came down to see the city and the tower which the children of men had built.
Verse_Ch: 11:6 耶和华说，看哪，他们是一样的人民，都说一样的语言；这不过是他们开头要作的事，以后他们所图谋要作的，就没有能阻挡的了。 ###EN### And Jehovah said, Behold, they are one people, and they all have one language; and this is only the beginning of what they will do; and now nothing which they
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: purpose to do will be kept from them.
Verse_Ch: 11:7 来罢，我们下去，在那里变乱他们的语言，使他们的言语彼此不通。 ###EN### Come, let Us go down and there confound their language, that they may not understand one another's speech.
Verse_Ch: 11:8 于是耶和华使他们从那里分散在全地上；他们就停工，不造那城了。 ###EN### So Jehovah scattered them from there over the surface of all the earth, and they ceased building the city.
Verse_Ch: 11:9 因为耶和华在那里变乱全地人的语言，使众人分散在全地上，所以那城名叫巴别。 ###EN### Therefore its name was called Babel, because there Jehovah confounded the language of all the earth, and from there Jehovah scattered them over the surface
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: of all the earth.
Verse_Ch: 11:10 闪的后代记在下面：洪水以后二年，闪一百岁生了亚法撒。 ###EN### These are the generations of Shem. Shem was one hundred years old when he begot Arpachshad, two years after the flood.
Verse_Ch: 11:11 闪生亚法撒之后，又活了五百年，并且生儿生女。 ###EN### And Shem lived after he had begotten Arpachshad five hundred years, and he begot more sons and daughters.
Verse_Ch: 11:12 亚法撒活到三十五岁，生了沙拉。 ###EN### And Arpachshad lived thirty-five years and begot Shelah.
Verse_Ch: 11:13 亚法撒生沙拉之后，又活了四百零三年，并且生儿生女。 ###EN### And Arpachshad lived after he had begotten Shelah four hundred three years, and he begot more sons and daughters.
Verse_Ch: 11:14 沙拉活到三十岁，生了希伯。 ###EN### And Shelah lived thirty years and begot Eber.
Verse_Ch: 11:15 沙拉生希伯之后，又活了四百零三年，并且生儿生女。 ###EN### And Shelah lived after he had begotten Eber four hundred three years, and he begot more sons and daughters.
Verse_Ch: 11:16 希伯活到三十四岁，生了法勒。 ###EN### And Eber lived thirty-four years and begot Peleg.
Verse_Ch: 11:17 希伯生法勒之后，又活了四百三十年，并且生儿生女。 ###EN### And Eber lived after he had begotten Peleg four hundred thirty years, and he begot more sons and daughters.
Verse_Ch: 11:18 法勒活到三十岁，生了拉吴。 ###EN### And Peleg lived thirty years and begot Reu.
Verse_Ch: 11:19 法勒生拉吴之后，又活了二百零九年，并且生儿生女。 ###EN### And Peleg lived after he had begotten Reu two hundred nine years, and he begot more sons and daughters.
Verse_Ch: 11:20 拉吴活到三十二岁，生了西鹿。 ###EN### And Reu lived thirty-two years and begot Serug.
Verse_Ch: 11:21 拉吴生西鹿之后，又活了二百零七年，并且生儿生女。 ###EN### And Reu lived after he had begotten Serug two hundred seven years, and he begot more sons and daughters.
Verse_Ch: 11:22 西鹿活到三十岁，生了拿鹤。 ###EN### And Serug lived thirty years and begot Nahor.
Verse_Ch: 11:23 西鹿生拿鹤之后，又活了二百年，并且生儿生女。 ###EN### And Serug lived after he had begotten Nahor two hundred years, and he begot more sons and daughters.
Verse_Ch: 11:24 拿鹤活到二十九岁，生了他拉。 ###EN### And Nahor lived twenty-nine years and begot Terah.
Verse_Ch: 11:25 拿鹤生他拉之后，又活了一百一十九年，并且生儿生女。 ###EN### And Nahor lived after he had begotten Terah one hundred nineteen years, and he begot more sons and daughters.
Verse_Ch: 11:26 他拉活到七十岁，生了亚伯兰、拿鹤、哈兰。 ###EN### And Terah lived seventy years and begot Abram, Nahor, and Haran.
Verse_Ch: 11:27 他拉的后代记在下面：他拉生亚伯兰、拿鹤、哈兰；哈兰生罗得。 ###EN### Now these are the generations of Terah. Terah begot Abram, Nahor, and Haran. And Haran begot Lot.
Verse_Ch: 11:28 哈兰死在他的出生地迦勒底的吾珥，在他父亲他拉之先。 ###EN### And Haran died before his father Terah in the land of his birth, in Ur of the Chaldeans.
Verse_Ch: 11:29 亚伯兰、拿鹤各娶了妻子：亚伯兰的妻子名叫撒莱；拿鹤的妻子名叫密迦，是哈兰的女儿；哈兰是密迦和亦迦的父亲。 ###EN### And Abram and Nahor took wives for themselves: The name of Abram's wife was Sarai, and the name of Nahor's wife was Milcah, the daughter of Haran, the
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: father of Milcah and the father of Iscah.
Verse_Ch: 11:30 撒莱不生育，没有孩子。 ###EN### And Sarai was barren; she had no child.
Verse_Ch: 11:31 他拉带着他儿子亚伯兰和他孙子哈兰的儿子罗得，并他儿媳亚伯兰的妻子撒莱，一起出了迦勒底的吾珥，要往迦南地去；他们走到哈兰，就住在那里。 ###EN### And Terah took Abram his son and Lot the son of Haran, his son's son, and Sarai his daughter-in-law, his son Abram's wife; and they went out together from Ur
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: of the Chaldeans to go to the land of Canaan, but when they came to Haran they settled there.
Verse_Ch: 11:32 他拉共活了二百零五岁，就死在哈兰。 ###EN### And the days of Terah were two hundred five years, and Terah died in Haran.
Chapter_Header: 12
Verse_Ch: 12:1 耶和华对亚伯兰说，你要离开本地、亲族、父家，往我所要指示你的地去。 ###EN### Now Jehovah said to Abram, Go from your land And from your relatives And from your father's house To the land that I will show you;
Verse_Ch: 12:2 我必使你成为大国；我必赐福给你，使你的名为大；你也要使别人得福。 ###EN### And I will make of you a great nation, And I will bless you And make your name great; And you shall be a blessing.
Verse_Ch: 12:3 那为你祝福的，我必赐福与他；那咒诅你的，我必咒诅他。地上的万族都必因你得福。 ###EN### And I will bless those who bless you, And he who curses you I will curse; And in you all the families of the earth will be blessed.
Verse_Ch: 12:4 亚伯兰就照着耶和华的吩咐去了；罗得也和他同去。亚伯兰出哈兰的时候，年七十五岁。 ###EN### So Abram went as Jehovah had spoken to him, and Lot went with him. Now Abram was seventy-five years old when he went out of Haran.
Verse_Ch: 12:5 亚伯兰将他妻子撒莱和侄儿罗得，连他们在哈兰所积聚的家产、所得的人口，都带出来，往迦南地去。他们就到了迦南地。 ###EN### And Abram took Sarai his wife and Lot his brother's son and all their possessions that they had gathered, and the souls that they had acquired in Haran, and they
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: went out to go to the land of Canaan. And they came to the land of Canaan.
Verse_Ch: 12:6 亚伯兰经过那地，到了示剑地方、摩利橡树那里。当时迦南人住在那地。 ###EN### And Abram passed through the land to the place of Shechem, to the oak of Moreh. And at that time the Canaanites were in the land.
Verse_Ch: 12:7 耶和华向亚伯兰显现，说，我要把这地赐给你的后裔。亚伯兰就在那里为向他显现的耶和华筑了一座坛。 ###EN### And Jehovah appeared to Abram and said, To your seed I will give this land. And there he built an altar to Jehovah who had appeared to him.
Verse_Ch: 12:8 从那里他又迁到伯特利东边的山，支搭帐棚；西边是伯特利，东边是艾；他在那里又为耶和华筑了一座坛，并且呼求耶和华的名。 ###EN### And he proceeded from there to the mountain on the east of Bethel and pitched his tent, with Bethel on the west and Ai on the east; and there he built an altar to
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: Jehovah and called upon the name of Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 12:9 后来亚伯兰渐渐迁往南地去。 ###EN### And Abram journeyed onward, journeying toward the Negev.
Verse_Ch: 12:10 那地遭遇饥荒；因饥荒甚重，亚伯兰就下埃及去，要在那里寄居。 ###EN### And there was a famine in the land; and Abram went down to Egypt to sojourn there, for the famine was severe in the land.
Verse_Ch: 12:11 他将近埃及，就对妻子撒莱说，我知道你是容貌美丽的妇人。 ###EN### And when he was about to enter into Egypt, he said to Sarai his wife, I know indeed that you are a beautiful woman to look at;
Verse_Ch: 12:12 埃及人看见你，必说，这是他的妻子，他们就会杀我，却叫你活着。 ###EN### And when the Egyptians see you, they will say, This is his wife, and they will kill me; but they will keep you alive.
Verse_Ch: 12:13 求你说，你是我的妹妹，使我因你得善待，我的命也因你存活。 ###EN### Now say you are my sister, that it may be well with me on account of you and I may live because of you.
Verse_Ch: 12:14 及至亚伯兰到了埃及，埃及人看见那妇人极其美丽。 ###EN### And it came about when Abram came to Egypt, the Egyptians saw that the woman was very beautiful.
Verse_Ch: 12:15 法老的大臣看见了她，就在法老面前称赞她；那妇人就被带进法老的宫里去。 ###EN### And Pharaoh's officials saw her and praised her before Pharaoh, and the woman was taken into Pharaoh's house.
Verse_Ch: 12:16 法老因这妇人就善待亚伯兰，亚伯兰得了许多牛、羊、骆驼、公驴、母驴、仆人、婢女。 ###EN### And he treated Abram well on account of her, and he had sheep and oxen and donkeys and male servants and female servants and female donkeys and
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: camels.
Verse_Ch: 12:17 耶和华因亚伯兰妻子撒莱的缘故，以大灾病击打法老和他全家。 ###EN### And Jehovah struck Pharaoh and his house with great plagues because of Sarai, Abram's wife.
Verse_Ch: 12:18 法老就召了亚伯兰来，说，你这向我作的是什么事？为什么没有告诉我，她是你的妻子？ ###EN### And Pharaoh called Abram and said, What is this you have done to me? Why did you not tell me that she was your wife?
Verse_Ch: 12:19 为什么说她是你的妹妹，以致我把她取来要作我的妻子？现在你的妻子在这里，把她带走罢。 ###EN### Why did you say, She is my sister, so that I took her to be my wife? Now then here is your wife; take her and go.
Verse_Ch: 12:20 于是法老吩咐人将亚伯兰和他妻子，并他所有的都送走了。 ###EN### And Pharaoh commanded his men concerning him; and they sent him away with his wife and all that he had.
Chapter_Header: 13
Verse_Ch: 13:1 亚伯兰带着他的妻子和一切所有的，以及罗得，都从埃及上南地去。 ###EN### And Abram went up out of Egypt, he and his wife and all that he had, and Lot with him, into the Negev.
Verse_Ch: 13:2 亚伯兰的金、银、牲畜极多。 ###EN### And Abram was very rich in livestock, in silver and in gold.
Verse_Ch: 13:3 他从南地渐渐往伯特利去，到了伯特利和艾的中间，就是他起初支搭帐棚的地方， ###EN### And he continued on his journey from the Negev as far as Bethel, to the place where his tent had been at the beginning, between Bethel and Ai,
Verse_Ch: 13:4 也是他先前筑坛的地方；他又在那里呼求耶和华的名。 ###EN### To the place of the altar, which he had made there formerly; and there Abram called on the name of Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 13:5 与亚伯兰同行的罗得，也有牛群、羊群、帐棚。 ###EN### And Lot also, who went with Abram, had flocks and herds and tents.
Verse_Ch: 13:6 那地容纳不下他们；因为他们的家产甚多，使他们不能同住一起。 ###EN### And the land could not support them that they might dwell together, for their possessions were so great that they could not dwell together.
Verse_Ch: 13:7 当时，迦南人与比利洗人在那地居住。牧养亚伯兰牲畜的人和牧养罗得牲畜的人起了争执。 ###EN### And there was strife between the herdsmen of Abram's livestock and the herdsmen of Lot's livestock. And at that time the Canaanites and the Perizzites dwelt in
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: the land.
Verse_Ch: 13:8 亚伯兰就对罗得说，你我不可相争，你的牧人和我的牧人也不可相争，因为我们是弟兄。 ###EN### And Abram said to Lot, Let there please be no strife between me and you and between my herdsmen and your herdsmen, for we are brothers.
Verse_Ch: 13:9 遍地不都在你面前么？请你离开我；你向左，我就向右；你向右，我就向左。 ###EN### Is not the whole land before you? Please separate yourself from me. If you go to the left, then I will go to the right. Or if you go to the right, then I will go to the left.
Verse_Ch: 13:10 罗得举目看见约但河的全平原，直到琐珥，都是滋润的；那地在耶和华毁灭所多玛、蛾摩拉以前，如同耶和华的园子，也像埃及地。 ###EN### And Lot lifted up his eyes and saw the entire plain of the Jordan, that it was well watered everywhere-this was before Jehovah had destroyed Sodom and
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: Gomorrah-like the garden of Jehovah, like the land of Egypt, as you go to Zoar.
Verse_Ch: 13:11 于是罗得为自己选择约但河的全平原，往东迁移；他们就彼此分离了。 ###EN### So Lot chose for himself the entire plain of the Jordan, and Lot journeyed east; and they separated themselves from each other.
Verse_Ch: 13:12 亚伯兰住在迦南地；罗得住在平原的城邑，并且渐渐挪移帐棚，直到所多玛。 ###EN### Abram dwelt in the land of Canaan, and Lot dwelt in the cities of the plain and moved his tent as far as Sodom.
Verse_Ch: 13:13 所多玛人在耶和华面前罪大恶极。 ###EN### Now the men of Sodom were very wicked and sinful toward Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 13:14 罗得离别亚伯兰以后，耶和华对亚伯兰说，从你所在的地方，举目向东西南北观看； ###EN### And Jehovah said to Abram, after Lot had separated from him, Now lift up your eyes, and look from the place where you are, northward and southward and
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: eastward and westward;
Verse_Ch: 13:15 凡你所看见的一切地，我都要赐给你和你的后裔，直到永远。 ###EN### For all the land that you see I will give to you and to your seed forever.
Verse_Ch: 13:16 我也要使你的后裔如同地上的尘沙那样多，人若能数算地上的尘沙，才能数算你的后裔。 ###EN### And I will make your seed as the dust of the earth, so that if a man can number the dust of the earth, then your seed can also be numbered.
Verse_Ch: 13:17 你起来，纵横走遍这地，因为我必把这地赐给你。 ###EN### Rise up; walk through the land according to its length and its breadth, for I will give it to you.
Verse_Ch: 13:18 亚伯兰就搬了帐棚，来到希伯仑幔利的橡树那里居住，在那里为耶和华筑了一座坛。 ###EN### And Abram moved his tent and came and dwelt by the oaks of Mamre, which are in Hebron, and there he built an altar to Jehovah.
Chapter_Header: 14
Verse_Ch: 14:1 当暗拉非作示拿王，亚略作以拉撒王，基大老玛作以拦王，提达作戈印王的时候， ###EN### And in the days of Amraphel the king of Shinar, Arioch the king of Ellasar, Chedorlaomer the king of Elam, and Tidal the king of Goiim,
Verse_Ch: 14:2 他们都攻打所多玛王比锐、蛾摩拉王比沙、押玛王示纳、洗扁王善以别、和比拉王；比拉就是琐珥。 ###EN### These kings made war with Bera the king of Sodom and with Birsha the king of Gomorrah, Shinab the king of Admah, and Shemeber the king of Zeboiim, and the
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: king of Bela (that is, Zoar).
Verse_Ch: 14:3 这五王都在西订谷会合；西订谷就是盐海。 ###EN### All these joined together in the valley of Siddim (that is, the Salt Sea).
Verse_Ch: 14:4 他们已经服事基大老玛十二年，到第十三年就背叛了。 ###EN### Twelve years they had served Chedorlaomer, and in the thirteenth year they rebelled.
Verse_Ch: 14:5 第十四年，基大老玛和同盟的王都来在亚特律加宁，击败了利乏音人；在哈麦击败了苏西人，在沙微基列亭击败了以米人， ###EN### And in the fourteenth year Chedorlaomer and the kings who were with him came and struck the Rephaim in Ashteroth-karnaim and the Zuzim in Ham and the
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: Emim in Shaveh-kiriathaim
Verse_Ch: 14:6 在西珥山击败了何利人，一直追击到靠近旷野的伊勒巴兰。 ###EN### And the Horites in Mount Seir as far as El-paran, which is by the wilderness.
Verse_Ch: 14:7 他们回到安密巴，就是加低斯，击败了亚玛力全地的人，以及住在哈洗逊他玛的亚摩利人。 ###EN### And they turned back and came to En-mishpat (that is, Kadesh), and struck all the country of the Amalekites and also the Amorites who dwelt in Hazazon-tamar.
Verse_Ch: 14:8 于是所多玛王、蛾摩拉王、押玛王、洗扁王、和比拉王(比拉就是琐珥)都出来，在西订谷摆阵，与他们交战， ###EN### And the king of Sodom and the king of Gomorrah and the king of Admah and the king of Zeboiim and the king of Bela (that is, Zoar) went forth and set the battle
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: in array against them in the valley of Siddim,
Verse_Ch: 14:9 就是与以拦王基大老玛、戈印王提达、示拿王暗拉非、以拉撒王亚略交战；乃是四王与五王交战。 ###EN### Against Chedorlaomer the king of Elam and Tidal the king of Goiim and Amraphel the king of Shinar and Arioch the king of Ellasar, four kings against the five.
Verse_Ch: 14:10 西订谷有许多石漆坑；所多玛王和蛾摩拉王逃跑，掉在坑里，其余的人都往山地逃跑。 ###EN### Now the valley of Siddim was full of tar pits, and the kings of Sodom and Gomorrah fled; and they fell there, but those who survived fled to the hill country.
Verse_Ch: 14:11 四王就把所多玛和蛾摩拉所有的财物，并一切的粮食，都掳掠去了； ###EN### And they took all the possessions of Sodom and Gomorrah and all their food and went away.
Verse_Ch: 14:12 又把亚伯兰的侄儿罗得和罗得的财物掳掠去了，当时罗得正住在所多玛。 ###EN### And they took Lot, Abram's brother's son, and his possessions and departed, for he was dwelling in Sodom.
Verse_Ch: 14:13 有一个逃出来的人，来告诉希伯来人亚伯兰；亚伯兰正住在亚摩利人幔利的橡树那里。幔利和以实各并亚乃都是弟兄，曾与亚伯兰联盟。 ###EN### And one who had escaped came and told Abram the Hebrew. Now he was dwelling by the oaks of Mamre the Amorite, the brother of Eshcol and brother of
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: Aner; and these were allies of Abram.
Verse_Ch: 14:14 亚伯兰听见他侄儿被掳去，就率领他家里生养的精练壮丁三百一十八人，直追到但， ###EN### And when Abram heard that his brother had been taken captive, he led out his trained men, born in his house, three hundred eighteen of them, and pursued as
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: far as Dan.
Verse_Ch: 14:15 便在夜间，自己同仆人分队击败敌人，又追到大马色北边的何把， ###EN### And he divided his forces against them by night, he and his servants, and struck them and pursued them to Hobah, which is north of Damascus.
Verse_Ch: 14:16 将一切财物夺回来，连他侄儿罗得和他的财物，以及妇女、人民也都夺回来。 ###EN### And he brought back all the possessions and also brought back Lot his brother and his possessions as well as the women and the people.
Verse_Ch: 14:17 亚伯兰击败基大老玛和与他同盟的王回来的时候，所多玛王出来，在沙微谷迎接他；沙微谷就是王谷。 ###EN### And after his return from the slaughter of Chedorlaomer and the kings who were with him, the king of Sodom went out to meet him at the valley of Shaveh (that is,
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: the King's Valley).
Verse_Ch: 14:18 又有撒冷王麦基洗德带着饼和酒出来迎接；他是至高神的祭司。 ###EN### And Melchizedek the king of Salem brought out bread and wine. Now he was priest of God the Most High.
Verse_Ch: 14:19 他为亚伯兰祝福，说，愿天地的主、至高的神赐福与亚伯兰； ###EN### And he blessed him and said, Blessed be Abram of God the Most High, Possessor of heaven and earth;
Verse_Ch: 14:20 至高的神把敌人交在你手里，是当受颂赞的。亚伯兰就将所得的一切，拿了十分之一给他。 ###EN### And blessed be God the Most High, Who has delivered your enemies into your hand. And Abram gave him a tenth of all.
Verse_Ch: 14:21 所多玛王对亚伯兰说，你把人口给我，财物你自己拿去罢。 ###EN### And the king of Sodom said to Abram, Give me the people, and take the possessions for yourself.
Verse_Ch: 14:22 但亚伯兰对所多玛王说，我已经向天地的主，至高的神耶和华举手起誓； ###EN### But Abram said to the king of Sodom, I have lifted up my hand to Jehovah, God the Most High, Possessor of heaven and earth,
Verse_Ch: 14:23 凡是你的东西，就是一根线、一根鞋带，我都不拿，免得你说，我使亚伯兰富足。 ###EN### That I will not take a thread or a sandal thong or anything that is yours, lest you say, I have made Abram rich;
Verse_Ch: 14:24 只有仆人们所吃的，并与我同行的亚乃、以实各、幔利所应得的分，可以任凭他们拿去。 ###EN### Except only that which the young men have eaten and the portion of the men who went with me-Aner, Eshcol, and Mamre; let them take their portion.
Chapter_Header: 15
Verse_Ch: 15:1 这些事以后，耶和华的话在异象中临到亚伯兰，说，亚伯兰，你不要惧怕；我是你的盾牌，是你极大的赏赐。 ###EN### After these things the word of Jehovah came to Abram in a vision, saying, Do not be afraid, Abram; I am your shield and your exceedingly great reward.
Verse_Ch: 15:2 亚伯兰说，主耶和华阿，我快要去世了还没有儿子，你还赐我什么呢？那要承受我家业的，是大马色人以利以谢。 ###EN### And Abram said, O Lord Jehovah, what will You give me, for I go childless, and the heir of my house is Eliezer of Damascus?
Verse_Ch: 15:3 亚伯兰又说，你没有给我后裔；那在我家中的仆人，就是我的后嗣。 ###EN### And Abram said, Since You have given me no seed, therefore, a servant in my house is my heir.
Verse_Ch: 15:4 但耶和华的话临到他说，这人必不成为你的后嗣；你本身将要生的，才是你的后嗣。 ###EN### But then the word of Jehovah came to him, saying, This man shall not be your heir, but he who will come out from your own body shall be your heir.
Verse_Ch: 15:5 于是领他走到外边，说，你向天观看，数算众星，能数得过来么？又对他说，你的后裔将要如此。 ###EN### And He brought him outside and said, Look now toward the heavens, and count the stars, if you are able to count them. And He said to him, So shall your seed
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: be.
Verse_Ch: 15:6 亚伯兰信耶和华，耶和华就以此算为他的义。 ###EN### And he believed Jehovah, and He accounted it to him as righteousness.
Verse_Ch: 15:7 耶和华又对他说，我是耶和华，曾领你出了迦勒底的吾珥，为要将这地赐你为业。 ###EN### Then He said to him, I am Jehovah who brought you out of Ur of the Chaldeans to give you this land to inherit it.
Verse_Ch: 15:8 亚伯兰说，主耶和华阿，我怎能知道必得这地为业呢？ ###EN### And he said, O Lord Jehovah, how will I know that I will inherit it?
Verse_Ch: 15:9 祂说，你为我取一只三岁的母牛、一只三岁的母山羊、一只三岁的公绵羊、一只斑鸠、一只雏鸽。 ###EN### And He said to him, Bring Me a three-year-old heifer and a three-year-old female goat and a three-year-old ram and a turtledove and a young pigeon.
Verse_Ch: 15:10 亚伯兰就取了这些来，每样从中剖开，分成两半，一半对着一半的摆列，只有鸟没有剖开。 ###EN### And he brought Him all these and cut them in two in the middle and laid the half of each opposite the other, but the birds he did not cut in two.
Verse_Ch: 15:11 有鸷鸟下来，落在死畜的肉上，亚伯兰就把它们吓飞了。 ###EN### And the birds of prey came down upon the carcasses, and Abram drove them away.
Verse_Ch: 15:12 日头正落的时候，亚伯兰沉沉的睡了；忽然有惊人的大黑暗落在他身上。 ###EN### And when the sun was going down, a deep sleep fell upon Abram; and, behold, a terror and great darkness fell upon him.
Verse_Ch: 15:13 耶和华对亚伯兰说，你要确实知道，你的后裔必寄居别人的地，又服事那地的人；那地的人要苦待他们四百年。 ###EN### And He said to Abram, Know assuredly that your seed will be sojourners in a land that is not theirs, and they will serve them; and they will afflict them four
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: hundred years.
Verse_Ch: 15:14 但他们所要服事的那国，我要惩罚，后来他们必带着许多财物从那里出来。 ###EN### But I will also judge that nation, whom they will serve, and afterward they will come out with great possessions.
Verse_Ch: 15:15 至于你，你要享大寿数，被人埋葬，平平安安的归到你列祖那里。 ###EN### But as for you, you will go to your fathers in peace; you will be buried in a good old age.
Verse_Ch: 15:16 到了第四代，他们必回到此地，因为亚摩利人的罪孽还没有满盈。 ###EN### And in the fourth generation they will come here again, for the iniquity of the Amorites is not yet complete.
Verse_Ch: 15:17 日落天黑，不料有冒烟的炉并烧着的火把，从那些肉块中经过。 ###EN### And when the sun went down and it was dark, there came a smoking furnace and a torch of fire which passed between these pieces.
Verse_Ch: 15:18 当那日，耶和华与亚伯兰立约，说，我已赐给你的后裔，从埃及河直到伯拉大河之地， ###EN### On that day Jehovah made a covenant with Abram, saying, To your seed do I give this land, From the river of Egypt to the great river, the river Euphrates:
Verse_Ch: 15:19 就是基尼人、基尼洗人、甲摩尼人、 ###EN### The land of the Kenites and the Kenizzites and the Kadmonites
Verse_Ch: 15:20 赫人、比利洗人、利乏音人、 ###EN### And the Hittites and the Perizzites and the Rephaim
Verse_Ch: 15:21 亚摩利人、迦南人、革迦撒人、耶布斯人之地。 ###EN### And the Amorites and the Canaanites and the Girgashites and the Jebusites.
Chapter_Header: 16
Verse_Ch: 16:1 亚伯兰的妻子撒莱没有给他生儿女。撒莱有一个使女，名叫夏甲，是埃及人。 ###EN### Now Sarai, Abram's wife, bore him no children; and she had an Egyptian female servant, whose name was Hagar.
Verse_Ch: 16:2 撒莱对亚伯兰说，耶和华使我不能生育，求你和我的使女同房，或者我可以因她得孩子。亚伯兰听了撒莱的话。 ###EN### And Sarai said to Abram, Because Jehovah has prevented me from bearing, please go in to my female servant; perhaps I will obtain children by her. And Abram
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: listened to the voice of Sarai.
Verse_Ch: 16:3 于是亚伯兰的妻子撒莱，将使女埃及人夏甲给了她丈夫为妻；那时亚伯兰在迦南地已经住了十年。 ###EN### So after Abram had dwelt ten years in the land of Canaan, Sarai, Abram's wife, took Hagar the Egyptian, her female servant, and gave her to Abram her
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: husband to be a wife.
Verse_Ch: 16:4 亚伯兰与夏甲同房，夏甲就怀了孕；她见自己有孕，就轻看她的主母。 ###EN### And he went in to Hagar, and she conceived; and when she saw that she had conceived, her mistress was despised in her eyes.
Verse_Ch: 16:5 撒莱对亚伯兰说，愿我受的屈辱归到你身上。我将我的使女放在你怀中，她见自己有了孕，竟轻看我。愿耶和华在你我中间行判断。 ###EN### And Sarai said to Abram, May the wrong done to me be upon you. I gave my female servant into your bosom, and when she saw that she had conceived, I was
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: despised in her eyes. May Jehovah judge between me and you.
Verse_Ch: 16:6 亚伯兰对撒莱说，使女在你手下，你看怎样好，就怎样待她罢。于是撒莱苦待她，她就从撒莱面前逃走了。 ###EN### And Abram said to Sarai, Your female servant is now in your hand; do to her what is good in your eyes. So Sarai dealt harshly with her, and she fled from before
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: her.
Verse_Ch: 16:7 耶和华的使者在旷野往书珥路上的水泉旁遇见她， ###EN### And the Angel of Jehovah found her by a spring of water in the wilderness, by the spring on the way to Shur.
Verse_Ch: 16:8 对她说，撒莱的使女夏甲，你从那里来？要往那里去？夏甲说，我从我的主母撒莱面前逃出来。 ###EN### And He said, Hagar, Sarai's female servant, where did you come from and where are you going? And she said, I am fleeing from before my mistress Sarai.
Verse_Ch: 16:9 耶和华的使者对她说，你回到你主母那里，服在她手下； ###EN### And the Angel of Jehovah said to her, Return to your mistress, and submit yourself under her hands.
Verse_Ch: 16:10 又说，我必使你的后裔极其繁多，甚至不可胜数； ###EN### And the Angel of Jehovah said to her, I will greatly multiply your seed so that it will not be counted for multitude.
Verse_Ch: 16:11 并说，你如今怀孕要生一个儿子，可以给他起名叫以实玛利，因为耶和华听见了你的苦情。 ###EN### And the Angel of Jehovah said to her, You have now conceived And will bear a son, And you shall call his name Ishmael, Because Jehovah has heard of your
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: affliction.
Verse_Ch: 16:12 他为人必像野驴；他的手要攻打人，人的手也要攻打他；他必住在众弟兄的东边。 ###EN### And he will be a wild ass of a man; His hand will be against everyone, And everyone's hand, against him; And he will settle down opposite all his brothers.
Verse_Ch: 16:13 夏甲就称那对她说话之耶和华的名为：你是启示自己的神；因为她说，祂向我启示了祂自己，我在这里居然还存活么？ ###EN### And she called the name of Jehovah who spoke to her, You are a God who reveals Himself, for she said, Do I even remain here after He has revealed Himself to
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: me?
Verse_Ch: 16:14 所以这井名叫庇耳拉海莱；这井在加低斯和巴列之间。 ###EN### Therefore the well was called Beer-lahai-roi; there it is, between Kadesh and Bered.
Verse_Ch: 16:15 后来夏甲给亚伯兰生了一个儿子；亚伯兰给他起名叫以实玛利。 ###EN### And Hagar bore Abram a son, and Abram called the name of his son, whom Hagar bore, Ishmael.
Verse_Ch: 16:16 夏甲给亚伯兰生以实玛利的时候，亚伯兰年八十六岁。 ###EN### And Abram was eighty-six years old when Hagar bore Ishmael to Abram.
Chapter_Header: 17
Verse_Ch: 17:1 亚伯兰年九十九岁的时候，耶和华向他显现，对他说，我是全足的神；你要行在我面前，并且要完全； ###EN### And when Abram was ninety-nine years old, Jehovah appeared to Abram and said to him, I am the All-sufficient God; Walk before Me, and be perfect.
Verse_Ch: 17:2 我要与你立约，使你的后裔极其增多。 ###EN### And I will make My covenant between Me and you, And I will multiply you exceedingly.
Verse_Ch: 17:3 亚伯兰面伏于地；神又与他谈话，说， ###EN### And Abram fell on his face, and God talked with him, saying,
Verse_Ch: 17:4 我与你立的约是这样：你要成为多国的父。 ###EN### As for Me, this is My covenant with you, And you shall become the father of a multitude of nations.
Verse_Ch: 17:5 你的名不要再叫亚伯兰，要叫亚伯拉罕，因为我已立你作多国的父。 ###EN### Your name shall no longer be called Abram, But your name shall be Abraham; For I have made you the father of a multitude of nations.
Verse_Ch: 17:6 我必使你的后裔极其繁多；我必使多国从你而立，多王从你而出。 ###EN### And I will make you exceedingly fruitful; and I will make nations of you, and kings will come forth from you.
Verse_Ch: 17:7 我必与你并你世世代代的后裔坚立我的约，作永远的约，为要作你和你后裔的神。 ###EN### And I will establish My covenant between Me and you and your seed after you throughout their generations for an everlasting covenant, to be God to you and to
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: your seed after you.
Verse_Ch: 17:8 我要将你寄居的地，就是迦南全地，赐给你和你的后裔永远为业，我也必作他们的神。 ###EN### And I will give to you and to your seed after you the land of your sojournings, all the land of Canaan, for an everlasting possession; and I will be their God.
Verse_Ch: 17:9 神又对亚伯拉罕说，至于你，你和你的后裔当世世代代遵守我的约。 ###EN### And God said to Abraham, And as for you, you shall keep My covenant, you and your seed after you throughout their generations.
Verse_Ch: 17:10 你们所有的男子都要受割礼；这就是我与你并你的后裔所立的约，是你们所当遵守的。 ###EN### This is My covenant, which you shall keep, between Me and you and your seed after you: Every male among you shall be circumcised.
Verse_Ch: 17:11 你们都要受割礼，这是我与你们立约的记号。 ###EN### And you shall be circumcised in the flesh of your foreskin, and it shall be a sign of a covenant between Me and you.
Verse_Ch: 17:12 你们世世代代的男子，无论是家里生的，或是在你后裔之外用银子从外人买的，生下来第八日，都要受割礼。 ###EN### And he who is eight days old shall be circumcised among you, every male throughout your generations, he who is born in the house or bought with money from
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: any foreigner who is not of your seed.
Verse_Ch: 17:13 你家里生的和你用银子买的，都必须受割礼。这样，我的约就立在你们肉体上作永远的约。 ###EN### He who is born in your house and he who is bought with your money must be circumcised; thus My covenant shall be in your flesh for an everlasting covenant.
Verse_Ch: 17:14 但不受割礼的男子必从民中剪除，因他背了我的约。 ###EN### But as for the uncircumcised male who is not circumcised in the flesh of his foreskin, that person shall be cut off from his people; he has broken My covenant.
Verse_Ch: 17:15 神又对亚伯拉罕说，至于你的妻子撒莱，不可再叫撒莱，她的名要叫撒拉。 ###EN### And God said to Abraham, As for Sarai your wife, you shall not call her name Sarai, but her name shall be Sarah.
Verse_Ch: 17:16 我必赐福给她，也要使你从她得一个儿子。我必赐福给她，她也要作多国之母，必有多民的君王从她而出。 ###EN### And I will bless her, and I will also give you a son by her. Indeed, I will bless her, and she will be a mother of nations; kings of peoples will come forth from her.
Verse_Ch: 17:17 亚伯拉罕就面伏于地笑了，心里说，一百岁的人还能得孩子么？撒拉已经九十岁了，还能生孩子么？ ###EN### Then Abraham fell upon his face and laughed and said in his heart, Will a child be born to a man who is a hundred years old? And will Sarah, who is ninety years
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: old, bear a child?
Verse_Ch: 17:18 亚伯拉罕对神说，但愿以实玛利活在你面前。 ###EN### And Abraham said to God, Oh that Ishmael might live before You!
Verse_Ch: 17:19 神说，不然，你妻子撒拉必给你生一个儿子，你要给他起名叫以撒。我要与他坚定所立的约，作他后裔永远的约。 ###EN### But God said, No, but Sarah your wife will bear you a son, and you shall call his name Isaac; and I will establish My covenant with him for an everlasting covenant
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: for his seed after him.
Verse_Ch: 17:20 至于以实玛利，我也应允你；我已赐福给他，使他繁衍，极其增多。他必生十二个首领；我也要使他成为大国。 ###EN### And as for Ishmael, I have heard you; indeed, I have blessed him and will make him fruitful and will multiply him exceedingly: twelve princes will he beget, and I
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: will make him a great nation.
Verse_Ch: 17:21 到明年这约定的日期，撒拉必给你生以撒，我要与他坚定所立的约。 ###EN### But My covenant I will establish with Isaac, whom Sarah will bear to you at this appointed time next year.
Verse_Ch: 17:22 神和亚伯拉罕谈完了话，就离开他升上去了。 ###EN### And when He finished talking with him, God went up from Abraham.
Verse_Ch: 17:23 正当那日，亚伯拉罕遵着神对他所说的，给他的儿子以实玛利和家里的一切男子，无论是在家里生的，是用银子买的，都行了割礼。 ###EN### And Abraham took Ishmael his son and all who were born in his house and all who were bought with his money, every male among the men of Abraham's
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: house, and circumcised the flesh of their foreskin on the very same day, as God had said to him.
Verse_Ch: 17:24 亚伯拉罕受割礼的时候年九十九岁。 ###EN### And Abraham was ninety-nine years old when he was circumcised in the flesh of his foreskin.
Verse_Ch: 17:25 他儿子以实玛利受割礼的时候年十三岁。 ###EN### And Ishmael his son was thirteen years old when he was circumcised in the flesh of his foreskin.
Verse_Ch: 17:26 正当那日，亚伯拉罕和他儿子以实玛利一同受了割礼。 ###EN### On the very same day Abraham was circumcised as well as Ishmael his son.
Verse_Ch: 17:27 家里所有的男人，无论是在家里生的，是用银子从外人买的，也都与他一同受了割礼。 ###EN### And all the men of his house, those born in the house and those bought with money from a foreigner, were circumcised with him.
Chapter_Header: 18
Verse_Ch: 18:1 耶和华在幔利橡树那里向亚伯拉罕显现。那时天正热，亚伯拉罕坐在帐棚口。 ###EN### And Jehovah appeared to him by the oaks of Mamre as he was sitting at the entrance of his tent in the heat of the day.
Verse_Ch: 18:2 他举目观看，见有三个人在对面站着。他一看见，就从帐棚口跑去迎接他们，俯伏在地， ###EN### And he lifted up his eyes and looked, and there were three men standing opposite him. And when he saw them, he ran from the entrance of the tent to meet
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: them. And he bowed down to the earth
Verse_Ch: 18:3 说，我主，我若在你眼前蒙恩，求你不要离开仆人往前去。 ###EN### And said, My Lord, if I have found favor in Your sight, please do not pass on from Your servant.
Verse_Ch: 18:4 让我拿点水来，你们洗洗脚，在树下歇息歇息。 ###EN### Please let a little water be fetched, and do wash your feet, and rest yourselves under the tree.
Verse_Ch: 18:5 我再拿一点饼来，你们可以加添心力，然后往前去。你们既到仆人这里来，理当如此。他们说，就照你说的行罢。 ###EN### And let me fetch a morsel of bread that you may sustain yourselves. After that you may pass on, since you have come to your servant. So they said, Do as you
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: have said.
Verse_Ch: 18:6 亚伯拉罕急忙进帐棚见撒拉，说，你快快拿三细亚细面调和作饼。 ###EN### And Abraham hurried into the tent to Sarah and said, Quickly prepare three measures of fine flour, knead it, and make cakes.
Verse_Ch: 18:7 亚伯拉罕又跑到牛群里，牵了一只又嫩又好的牛犊来，交给仆人，仆人急忙预备好了。 ###EN### And Abraham ran to the herd and took a calf, tender and good, and gave it to the servant, and he hurried to prepare it.
Verse_Ch: 18:8 亚伯拉罕又取了奶酪和奶，并预备好的牛犊来，摆在他们面前，自己在树下站在旁边，他们就吃了。 ###EN### And he took curds and milk and the calf which he had prepared, and set them before them; and he stood by them under the tree while they ate.
Verse_Ch: 18:9 他们问亚伯拉罕说，你妻子撒拉在那里？他说，在帐棚里。 ###EN### And they said to him, Where is Sarah your wife? And he said, There, in the tent.
Verse_Ch: 18:10 其中一位说，到明年这时候，我必回到你这里；你的妻子撒拉必生一个儿子。撒拉在那位后边的帐棚口也听见了这话。 ###EN### And He said, I will certainly return to you according to the time of life, and then Sarah your wife shall have a son. And Sarah was listening at the entrance of the
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: tent, which was behind Him.
Verse_Ch: 18:11 亚伯拉罕和撒拉年纪老迈，撒拉的月经已经停了。 ###EN### Now Abraham and Sarah were old and advanced in age; it had ceased to be with Sarah according to the manner of women.
Verse_Ch: 18:12 撒拉心里暗笑，说，我既已衰败，我主也老迈，岂能有这乐趣呢？ ###EN### And Sarah laughed within herself, saying, After I have become old, shall I have pleasure, my lord being old also?
Verse_Ch: 18:13 耶和华对亚伯拉罕说，撒拉为什么笑，说，我既年迈，果真能生孩子么？ ###EN### And Jehovah said to Abraham, Why did Sarah laugh, saying, Shall I indeed bear a child, when I am old?
Verse_Ch: 18:14 耶和华岂有难成的事么？到了约定的日期，明年这时候，我必回到你这里，撒拉必生一个儿子。 ###EN### Is anything too marvelous for Jehovah? At the appointed time I will return to you, according to the time of life, and Sarah shall have a son.
Verse_Ch: 18:15 撒拉就害怕，不承认，说，我没有笑；那位说，不然，你实在笑了。 ###EN### Then Sarah denied it, saying, I did not laugh; for she was afraid. And He said, No, but you did laugh.
Verse_Ch: 18:16 三人就从那里起身，向所多玛观望；亚伯拉罕也与他们同行，要送他们一程。 ###EN### And the men rose up from there and looked down upon Sodom; and Abraham walked with them to send them away.
Verse_Ch: 18:17 耶和华说，我所要作的事，岂可瞒着亚伯拉罕么？ ###EN### And Jehovah said, Shall I hide from Abraham what I am about to do,
Verse_Ch: 18:18 亚伯拉罕必要成为又大又强的国，并且地上的万国都必因他得福。 ###EN### Since Abraham will indeed become a great and mighty nation, and all the nations of the earth will be blessed in him?
Verse_Ch: 18:19 我眷顾他，为要叫他吩咐他的子孙和他以后的家属，遵守我耶和华的道，秉行公义和公理，使我论到亚伯拉罕的话，都成就在他身上。 ###EN### For I know him, that he will command his children and his household after him to keep the way of Jehovah by doing righteousness and justice, that Jehovah may
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: bring upon Abraham what He has spoken concerning him.
