Verse_Ch: 18:20 耶和华说，所多玛和蛾摩拉的罪甚重，声闻于我。 ###EN### And Jehovah said, The cry of Sodom and Gomorrah, how great it is; and their sin, how very heavy it is!
Verse_Ch: 18:21 我现在要下去，察看他们所行的，果然尽像那达到我耳中的声音么？若是不然，我也会知道。 ###EN### I shall go down and see whether they have done altogether according to its outcry, which has come to Me; and if not, I will know.
Verse_Ch: 18:22 二人转身离开那里，向所多玛走去；但亚伯拉罕仍旧站在耶和华面前。 ###EN### And the men turned from there and went toward Sodom, while Abraham remained standing before Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 18:23 亚伯拉罕近前来，说，你真的要将义人与恶人一并剿灭么？ ###EN### And Abraham came near and said, Will You indeed destroy the righteous with the wicked?
Verse_Ch: 18:24 假若那城里有五十个义人，你还剿灭么？不为城里这五十个义人宽容那地方么？ ###EN### Suppose there are fifty righteous within the city; will You indeed destroy and not spare the place for the sake of the fifty righteous who are in it?
Verse_Ch: 18:25 你断不至将义人与恶人同杀，将义人与恶人一样看待；这断不是你所行的。审判全地的主岂不公平行事么？ ###EN### Far be it from You to do such a thing, to put to death the righteous with the wicked, so that the righteous should be as the wicked. Far be it from You! Shall the
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: Judge of all the earth not do justly?
Verse_Ch: 18:26 耶和华说，我若在所多玛城里见有五十个义人，我就要为他们的缘故宽容那地方。 ###EN### And Jehovah said, If I find in Sodom fifty righteous within the city, then I will spare the whole place for their sake.
Verse_Ch: 18:27 亚伯拉罕回答说，我虽然是尘土炉灰，还敢对主说话。 ###EN### And Abraham answered and said, Now behold, I have taken it upon myself to speak to the Lord, though I am but dust and ashes.
Verse_Ch: 18:28 假若这五十个义人缺了五个，你就因为缺了五个毁灭全城么？祂说，我在那里若见有四十五个，也不毁灭那城。 ###EN### Suppose the fifty righteous are lacking five, will You destroy the whole city because of five? And He said, I will not destroy it if I find forty-five there.
Verse_Ch: 18:29 亚伯拉罕又对祂说，假若在那里见有四十个怎么样？祂说，为这四十个的缘故，我也不作这事。 ###EN### And he spoke to Him yet again and said, Suppose forty are found there? And He said, I will not do it because of forty.
Verse_Ch: 18:30 亚伯拉罕说，求主不要动怒，容我说，假若在那里见有三十个怎么样？祂说，我在那里若见有三十个，我也不作这事。 ###EN### And he said, Oh may the Lord not be angry if I speak. Suppose thirty are found there? And He said, I will not do it if I find thirty there.
Verse_Ch: 18:31 亚伯拉罕说，我还敢对主说话，假若在那里见有二十个怎么样？祂说，为这二十个的缘故，我也不毁灭那城。 ###EN### And he said, Now behold, I have taken it upon myself to speak to the Lord. Suppose twenty are found there? And He said, I will not destroy it because of twenty.
Verse_Ch: 18:32 亚伯拉罕说，求主不要动怒，容我再说这一次，假若在那里见有十个呢？祂说，为这十个的缘故，我也不毁灭那城。 ###EN### And he said, Oh let the Lord not be angry if I speak yet once more. Suppose ten are found there? And He said, I will not destroy it because of ten.
Verse_Ch: 18:33 耶和华与亚伯拉罕说完了话就走了；亚伯拉罕也回到自己的地方去了。 ###EN### And Jehovah went away as soon as He had finished speaking with Abraham, and Abraham returned to his place.
Chapter_Header: 19
Verse_Ch: 19:1 那两个天使傍晚到了所多玛；罗得正坐在所多玛城门口，看见他们，就起来迎接，面伏于地下拜， ###EN### And the two angels came to Sodom in the evening, and Lot was sitting in the gate of Sodom. And when Lot saw them, he rose up to meet them and bowed with
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: his face to the ground.
Verse_Ch: 19:2 说，我主阿，请你们转来仆人家里洗洗脚，过一夜，清早起来再上路。他们说，不，我们要在大街上过夜。 ###EN### And he said, Now, my lords, please turn aside here to your servant's house, and spend the night, and wash your feet; then you can rise up early and go on your
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: way. But they said, No; we will spend the night in the square.
Verse_Ch: 19:3 罗得切切的请他们，他们才转身进到他屋里。罗得为他们预备筵席，烤无酵饼，他们就吃了。 ###EN### But he urged them strongly, and they turned aside to him and entered his house. And he made them a feast and baked unleavened bread, and they ate.
Verse_Ch: 19:4 他们还没有躺下，所多玛城里各处的人，连老带少，都来围住那房子， ###EN### But before they lay down, the men of the city, the men of Sodom, surrounded the house, both young and old, all the people from every quarter;
Verse_Ch: 19:5 呼叫罗得说，今晚到你这里来的人在那里？把他们带出来给我们，任我们所为。 ###EN### And they called to Lot and said to him, Where are the men who came to you tonight? Bring them out to us that we may know them.
Verse_Ch: 19:6 罗得出到门口，把门关上，到众人那里， ###EN### And Lot went out to them at the entrance and shut the door behind him.
Verse_Ch: 19:7 说，我的弟兄们，请你们不要作这恶事。 ###EN### And he said, Please, my brothers, do not act so wickedly.
Verse_Ch: 19:8 我有两个女儿，还是处女，让我领出来，照你们看为好的而行；只是这两个人既然到我舍下，不要向他们作什么。 ###EN### I have here two daughters who have not known a man. Please, let me bring them out to you, and do to them as is fitting in your eyes; only do not do anything to
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: these men, inasmuch as they have come under the shelter of my roof.
Verse_Ch: 19:9 但众人说，走开罢！又说，这个人来寄居，还作起审判官了！现在我们要害你比害他们更甚。众人就极力拥挤罗得，向前要攻破房门。 ###EN### But they said, Stand aside. Then they said, This one came here to sojourn, and already he is acting like a judge. Now we will treat you worse than we would have
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: them. And they pressed hard against the man, against Lot, and came near in order to break down the door.
Verse_Ch: 19:10 但那两个人伸出手来，将罗得拉进屋里，把门关上， ###EN### But the men stretched out their hand and brought Lot into the house to them and shut the door.
Verse_Ch: 19:11 并且使门外的人，无论老少，眼都昏迷；他们耗尽了力气，也寻不着房门。 ###EN### And they struck the men who were at the entrance of the house with blindness, both small and great, so that they wearied themselves trying to find the entrance.
Verse_Ch: 19:12 那两个人对罗得说，你这里还有什么人？无论是女婿，是儿女，还是这城中一切属你的人，你都将他们从这地方带出去。 ###EN### And the men said to Lot, Whom else do you have here? A son-in-law or your sons and your daughters or anyone you have in the city-bring them out of the
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: place.
Verse_Ch: 19:13 我们就要毁灭这地方；因为他们罪恶的声音在耶和华面前甚大，耶和华差我们来，要毁灭这地方。 ###EN### For we are about to destroy this place, because their outcry has become so great before Jehovah that Jehovah has sent us to destroy it.
Verse_Ch: 19:14 罗得就出去，告诉要娶他女儿的女婿们说，你们起来离开这地方，因为耶和华要毁灭这城。他女婿们却以为他在说戏言。 ###EN### And Lot went out and spoke to his sons-in-law, who were to marry his daughters, and said, Rise up; go forth from this place, for Jehovah will destroy the city. But
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: it seemed to his sons-in-law as though he were joking.
Verse_Ch: 19:15 天明了，天使催逼罗得说，起来，带着你的妻子和你在这里的两个女儿出去，免得你因这城里的罪孽同被剿灭。 ###EN### And when the morning dawned, the angels urged Lot, saying, Rise up; take your wife and your two daughters who are here, lest you be destroyed in the iniquity
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: of the city.
Verse_Ch: 19:16 但罗得迟延不走。那两个人因为耶和华怜悯罗得，就抓着他的手和他妻子的手，并他两个女儿的手，把他们领出来，安置在城外； ###EN### But he lingered; so the men seized his hand and the hand of his wife and the hand of his two daughters, Jehovah being merciful to him, and they brought him
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: out and set him outside the city.
Verse_Ch: 19:17 领他们出来以后，就说，逃命罢！不可回头看，也不可在平原上任何一处站住。要往山上逃跑，免得你被剿灭。 ###EN### And when they had brought them outside, He said, Escape for your life. Do not look behind you, neither stay anywhere in the plain. Escape to the hills, lest you be
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: destroyed.
Verse_Ch: 19:18 罗得对他们说，主阿，但愿不要如此。 ###EN### And Lot said to them, May it not be so, Lord;
Verse_Ch: 19:19 你仆人已经在你眼前蒙恩，你又向我显出莫大的慈爱，保全我的性命；我没有力量逃到山上，恐怕这灾祸追上我，我便死了。 ###EN### Even though Your servant has found favor in Your sight, and You have magnified Your lovingkindness, which You have showed to me in preserving my life; I
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: cannot escape to the mountain, lest the disaster overtake me and I die.
Verse_Ch: 19:20 看哪，这座小城很近，容易逃到。这不是一座小城么？求你让我逃到那里，我的性命就得存活。 ###EN### Here, this city is nearby to flee to, and it is a little one. Please let me escape there-is it not a little one?-and I shall live.
Verse_Ch: 19:21 天使对他说，这事我也应允你；我不倾覆你所说的这城。 ###EN### And He said to him, I now grant you this request also, that I will not overthrow the city concerning which you have spoken.
Verse_Ch: 19:22 你要快快逃到那里；因为你还没有到那里，我不能作什么。因此那城名叫琐珥。 ###EN### Hurry, escape there; for I cannot do anything until you arrive there. Therefore the name of the city was called Zoar.
Verse_Ch: 19:23 罗得到了琐珥，日头已经升起，照在地上。 ###EN### The sun had risen over the earth when Lot came to Zoar.
Verse_Ch: 19:24 当时，耶和华将硫磺与火从天上耶和华那里，降与所多玛和蛾摩拉， ###EN### Then Jehovah rained upon Sodom and upon Gomorrah brimstone and fire from Jehovah out of heaven.
Verse_Ch: 19:25 倾覆了那些城和全平原，并城里所有的居民，以及地上生长的一切。 ###EN### And He overthrew those cities and all the plain and all the inhabitants of the cities and what grew on the ground.
Verse_Ch: 19:26 罗得的妻子在后边回头一看，就变成了一根盐柱。 ###EN### But his wife looked back from behind him, and she became a pillar of salt.
Verse_Ch: 19:27 亚伯拉罕清早起来，到了他从前站在耶和华面前的地方， ###EN### And Abraham rose up early in the morning and went to the place where he had stood before Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 19:28 向所多玛和蛾摩拉与平原的全地观望，不料，那地方烟气上腾，如同烧窑的烟气一般。 ###EN### And he looked down upon Sodom and Gomorrah and upon all the land of the plain. And as he looked, there it was: the smoke of the land was going up like the
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: smoke of a furnace.
Verse_Ch: 19:29 当神毁灭平原诸城的时候，祂记念亚伯拉罕，正在倾覆罗得所住之诸城的时候，就打发罗得从倾覆之中出来。 ###EN### And when God destroyed the cities of the plain, God remembered Abraham and sent Lot out from the middle of the overthrow, when He overthrew the cities
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: among which Lot dwelt.
Verse_Ch: 19:30 罗得因为怕住在琐珥，就同他两个女儿从琐珥上去，住在山里；他和两个女儿住在一个洞里。 ###EN### Then Lot went up out of Zoar and dwelt in the mountains, and his two daughters with him, for he was afraid to dwell in Zoar. And he and his two daughters dwelt
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: in a cave.
Verse_Ch: 19:31 大女儿对小女儿说，我们的父亲老了，地上又无人按着世上的常规，来亲近我们。 ###EN### And the firstborn said to the younger, Our father is old, and there is not a man on the earth to come in to us after the manner of all the earth.
Verse_Ch: 19:32 来，我们可以叫父亲喝酒，与他同寝。这样，我们就可从他存留后裔。 ###EN### Come, let us make our father drink wine; and let us lie with him, that we may preserve alive seed from our father.
Verse_Ch: 19:33 于是，那夜她们叫父亲喝酒，大女儿就进去和她父亲同寝；她几时躺下，几时起来，父亲都不知道。 ###EN### And they made their father drink wine that night. And the firstborn went in and lay with her father, and he did not know when she lay down or when she arose.
Verse_Ch: 19:34 第二天，大女儿对小女儿说，我昨夜与父亲同寝。今夜我们再叫他喝酒，你可以进去与他同寝。这样，我们就可从父亲存留后裔。 ###EN### And the next day the firstborn said to the younger, I have now lain with my father last night. Let us make him drink wine tonight also; and you go in, and lie with
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: him, that we may preserve alive seed from our father.
Verse_Ch: 19:35 于是，那夜她们又叫父亲喝酒，小女儿起来与她父亲同寝；她几时躺下，几时起来，父亲都不知道。 ###EN### And they made their father drink wine that night also. And the younger one arose and lay with him, and he did not know when she lay down or when she arose.
Verse_Ch: 19:36 这样，罗得的两个女儿，都从她们父亲怀了孕。 ###EN### Thus both the daughters of Lot became pregnant by their father.
Verse_Ch: 19:37 大女儿生了儿子，给他起名叫摩押，他是现今摩押人的始祖。 ###EN### And the firstborn bore a son and called his name Moab; he is the father of the Moabites to this day.
Verse_Ch: 19:38 小女儿也生了儿子，给他起名叫便亚米，他是现今亚扪人的始祖。 ###EN### And the younger, she also bore a son and called his name Ben-ammi; he is the father of the children of Ammon to this day.
Chapter_Header: 20
Verse_Ch: 20:1 亚伯拉罕从那里向南地迁去，住在加低斯和书珥之间，寄居在基拉耳。 ###EN### And Abraham journeyed from there toward the region of the Negev and dwelt between Kadesh and Shur; then he sojourned in Gerar.
Verse_Ch: 20:2 亚伯拉罕提到他的妻子撒拉，说，她是我的妹妹。基拉耳王亚比米勒差人把撒拉取了去。 ###EN### And Abraham said of Sarah his wife, She is my sister. And Abimelech the king of Gerar sent and took Sarah.
Verse_Ch: 20:3 但夜间神来在梦中对亚比米勒说，你要死啦！因为你取了那女人来；她原是别人的妻子。 ###EN### But God came to Abimelech in a dream by night and said to him, You are now about to die because of the woman whom you have taken, for she is a man's wife.
Verse_Ch: 20:4 亚比米勒却还没有亲近撒拉；他说，主阿，连公义的国，你也要杀灭么？ ###EN### But Abimelech had not come near her, so he said, Lord, will You slay even a righteous nation?
Verse_Ch: 20:5 那人岂不是自己对我说，她是我的妹妹么？就是女人自己也说，他是我的哥哥。我作这事是心正手洁的。 ###EN### Did he himself not say to me, She is my sister? And even she herself said, He is my brother. In the integrity of my heart and the innocence of my hands I have
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: done this.
Verse_Ch: 20:6 神在梦中对他说，我知道你作这事是心中纯正；我也拦阻了你，免得你得罪我；所以我不让你碰她。 ###EN### And God said to him in the dream, Yes, I know that in the integrity of your heart you have done this, and I also prevented you from sinning against Me; therefore I
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: did not let you touch her.
Verse_Ch: 20:7 现在你把这人的妻子归还他；因为他是申言者，他要为你祷告，使你存活。你若不归还，你当知道，你和你所有的人都必要死。 ###EN### Now therefore return the man's wife, for he is a prophet, and he will pray for you, and you will live. But if you do not return her, know that you shall surely die, you
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: and all who are yours.
Verse_Ch: 20:8 亚比米勒清早起来，召了众臣仆来，将这些事都说给他们听，他们就甚惧怕。 ###EN### And Abimelech rose early in the morning and called all his servants and spoke all these things in their hearing. And the men were very afraid.
Verse_Ch: 20:9 亚比米勒召了亚伯拉罕来，对他说，你向我们作了什么事？我在什么事上得罪了你，你竟使我和我的国陷在大罪里？你向我作了不当作的事了！ ###EN### Then Abimelech called Abraham and said to him, What have you done to us? And how have I sinned against you, that you have brought on me and on my
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: kingdom a great sin? You have done to me things that ought not to be done.
Verse_Ch: 20:10 亚比米勒又对亚伯拉罕说，你见了什么才作这事呢？ ###EN### And Abimelech said to Abraham, What did you see, that you have done this thing?
Verse_Ch: 20:11 亚伯拉罕说，我以为这地方的人总不惧怕神，必为我妻子的缘故杀我。 ###EN### And Abraham said, Because I thought, Surely there is no fear of God in this place, and they will slay me because of my wife.
Verse_Ch: 20:12 况且她也实在是我的妹妹；她与我是同父异母，后来作了我的妻子。 ###EN### But she is also truly my sister, the daughter of my father, but not the daughter of my mother; and she became my wife.
Verse_Ch: 20:13 当神叫我离开父家、飘流在外的时候，我对她说，我们无论走到什么地方，你提到我，要说，他是我的哥哥；这就是你以恩慈待我了。 ###EN### And when God caused me to wander from my father's house, I said to her, This is your kindness which you must do to me: At every place where we go, say of
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: me, He is my brother.
Verse_Ch: 20:14 亚比米勒把牛、羊、仆人、婢女赐给亚伯拉罕，又把他的妻子撒拉归还他。 ###EN### Then Abimelech took sheep and oxen and male servants and female servants, and gave them to Abraham; and he returned to him Sarah his wife.
Verse_Ch: 20:15 亚比米勒又说，看哪，我的地都在你面前，你可以随意居住； ###EN### And Abimelech said, My land is now before you; dwell wherever it pleases you.
Verse_Ch: 20:16 又对撒拉说，我给你哥哥一千锭银子，作为你在全家人面前遮羞的，你就在各方面没有不是了。 ###EN### And to Sarah he said, I have now given your brother a thousand pieces of silver. It is now your vindication before all who are with you. And in every respect you
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: have been cleared.
Verse_Ch: 20:17 亚伯拉罕祷告神，神就医好了亚比米勒和他的妻子，并他的众女仆，她们便能生育。 ###EN### And Abraham prayed to God; and God healed Abimelech and his wife and his female servants, so that they bore children.
Verse_Ch: 20:18 因耶和华为亚伯拉罕的妻子撒拉的缘故，已经使亚比米勒家中所有的妇人，都不能生育。 ###EN### For Jehovah had completely shut up all the wombs of the house of Abimelech because of Sarah, Abraham's wife.
Chapter_Header: 21
Verse_Ch: 21:1 耶和华按先前的话眷顾撒拉，便照祂所应许的给撒拉成就。 ###EN### And Jehovah visited Sarah as he had said, and Jehovah did to Sarah as He had promised.
Verse_Ch: 21:2 当亚伯拉罕年老的时候，撒拉怀了孕；到神和亚伯拉罕约定的日期，就给亚伯拉罕生了一个儿子。 ###EN### And Sarah conceived and bore Abraham a son in his old age, at the appointed time of which God had spoken to him.
Verse_Ch: 21:3 亚伯拉罕为撒拉给他生的儿子起名叫以撒。 ###EN### And Abraham called the name of his son who was born to him, whom Sarah bore to him, Isaac.
Verse_Ch: 21:4 以撒生下来第八日，亚伯拉罕照着神所吩咐的，给他的儿子以撒行了割礼。 ###EN### And Abraham circumcised Isaac his son when he was eight days old, as God had commanded him.
Verse_Ch: 21:5 他儿子以撒出生的时候，亚伯拉罕年一百岁。 ###EN### And Abraham was a hundred years old when Isaac his son was born to him.
Verse_Ch: 21:6 撒拉说，神使我欢笑，凡听见的必与我一同欢笑； ###EN### And Sarah said, God has made me laugh; everyone who hears will laugh with me.
Verse_Ch: 21:7 又说，谁能预先对亚伯拉罕说，撒拉要乳养儿女呢？然而在他年老的时候，我竟给他生了一个儿子。 ###EN### And she said, Who would have said to Abraham that Sarah would nurse children? Yet I have borne him a son in his old age.
Verse_Ch: 21:8 孩子渐长，就断了奶。以撒断奶的日子，亚伯拉罕设摆盛大的筵席。 ###EN### And the child grew and was weaned. And Abraham made a great feast on the day that Isaac was weaned.
Verse_Ch: 21:9 当时，撒拉看见埃及人夏甲给亚伯拉罕所生的儿子戏笑， ###EN### And Sarah saw the son of Hagar the Egyptian, whom she had borne to Abraham, mocking.
Verse_Ch: 21:10 就对亚伯拉罕说，你把这使女和她儿子赶出去，因为这使女的儿子不可与我的儿子以撒，一同承受产业。 ###EN### So she said to Abraham, Cast out this maidservant and her son, for the son of this maidservant shall not inherit with my son Isaac.
Verse_Ch: 21:11 亚伯拉罕因他儿子的缘故甚是愁烦。 ###EN### And the matter displeased Abraham greatly on account of his son.
Verse_Ch: 21:12 神对亚伯拉罕说，你不必为这童子和你的使女愁烦。凡撒拉对你说的话，你都要听；因为从以撒生的，才要称为你的后裔。 ###EN### And God said to Abraham, Do not be displeased on account of the boy and on account of your maidservant. Whatever Sarah says to you, listen to her voice, for
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: in Isaac shall your seed be called.
Verse_Ch: 21:13 至于使女的儿子，我也必使他成为一国，因为他是你的后裔。 ###EN### And of the son of the maidservant I will also make a nation, because he is your seed.
Verse_Ch: 21:14 亚伯拉罕清早起来，拿饼和一皮袋水，给了夏甲，搭在她的肩上，又把孩子交给她，打发她走。夏甲就走了，在别是巴的旷野走迷了路。 ###EN### And Abraham rose up early in the morning and took bread and a waterskin full of water and gave them to Hagar, putting them on her shoulder, and gave her
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: the child and sent her away. And she departed and wandered in the wilderness of Beer-sheba.
Verse_Ch: 21:15 皮袋的水用尽了，夏甲就把孩子撇在一棵小树下， ###EN### When the water in the waterskin was finished, she cast the child under one of the bushes.
Verse_Ch: 21:16 自己走开约有一箭之远，相对而坐，说，我不忍见孩子死，就相对而坐，放声大哭。 ###EN### And she went and sat herself down opposite him, a fair distance away, about a bowshot away, for she said, Do not let me look upon the death of the child. And
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: as she sat opposite him, she lifted up her voice and wept.
Verse_Ch: 21:17 神听见童子的声音；神的使者从天上呼叫夏甲说，夏甲，你怎么了？不要害怕，神已经听见童子的声音了。 ###EN### And God heard the voice of the boy. And the Angel of God called to Hagar out of heaven and said to her, What troubles you, Hagar? Do not be afraid, for God
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: has heard the voice of the boy where he is.
Verse_Ch: 21:18 起来，把童子扶起来牵着；我必使他成为大国。 ###EN### Rise up; lift up the boy, and hold him with your hand, for I will make him a great nation.
Verse_Ch: 21:19 神开了夏甲的眼睛，她就看见一口水井，便去将皮袋盛满了水，给童子喝。 ###EN### And God opened her eyes, and she saw a well of water. And she went and filled the waterskin with water and gave the boy a drink.
Verse_Ch: 21:20 神与童子同在，他就渐长，住在旷野，成了弓箭手。 ###EN### And God was with the boy, and he grew. And he dwelt in the wilderness and became an archer.
Verse_Ch: 21:21 他住在巴兰的旷野；他母亲从埃及地给他娶了一个妻子。 ###EN### And he dwelt in the wilderness of Paran. And his mother took a wife for him from the land of Egypt.
Verse_Ch: 21:22 当那时候，亚比米勒同他军长非各对亚伯拉罕说，在你所作的一切事上，神都与你同在。 ###EN### And at that time Abimelech and Phicol the captain of his army spoke to Abraham, saying, God is with you in all that you do.
Verse_Ch: 21:23 我愿你如今在这里指着神对我起誓，不要以诡诈待我与我的子孙后代。我怎样以恩慈待你，你也要照样待我，与你所寄居这地的民。 ###EN### Now therefore swear to me here by God that you will not deal falsely with me or with my offspring or with my posterity. According to the kindness that I have
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: shown to you, you shall do to me and to the land in which you have sojourned.
Verse_Ch: 21:24 亚伯拉罕说，我愿意起誓。 ###EN### And Abraham said, I swear it.
Verse_Ch: 21:25 从前，亚比米勒的仆人霸占了一口水井，亚伯拉罕为这事指责亚比米勒。 ###EN### And Abraham confronted Abimelech concerning the well of water which Abimelech's servants had taken by force.
Verse_Ch: 21:26 亚比米勒说，谁作这事，我不知道；你也没有告诉我，今日我才听见了。 ###EN### And Abimelech said, I do not know who has done this thing; and you did not tell me about it, nor have I even heard of it until today.
Verse_Ch: 21:27 亚伯拉罕把羊和牛给了亚比米勒，二人就彼此立约。 ###EN### And Abraham took sheep and oxen and gave them to Abimelech. And the two of them made a covenant.
Verse_Ch: 21:28 亚伯拉罕把羊群中的七只母羊羔，另放在一处。 ###EN### And Abraham set seven ewe lambs of the flock by themselves.
Verse_Ch: 21:29 亚比米勒问亚伯拉罕说，你把这七只母羊羔另放在一处，是什么意思？ ###EN### And Abimelech said to Abraham, What is the meaning of these seven ewe lambs which you have set by themselves?
Verse_Ch: 21:30 他说，你要从我手里接受这七只母羊羔，作我挖这口井的证据。 ###EN### And he said, These seven ewe lambs you shall take from my hand, that it may be a witness for me that I dug this well.
Verse_Ch: 21:31 所以他称那地方为别是巴，因为他们二人在那里起了誓。 ###EN### Therefore he called that place Beer-sheba, because there the two of them swore an oath.
Verse_Ch: 21:32 他们在别是巴立了约。亚比米勒就同他军长非各起身，回非利士人的地去了。 ###EN### So they made a covenant at Beer-sheba; and Abimelech rose up with Phicol the captain of his host, and they returned into the land of the Philistines.
Verse_Ch: 21:33 亚伯拉罕在别是巴栽了一棵垂丝柳树，又在那里呼求耶和华永远之神的名。 ###EN### And Abraham planted a tamarisk tree in Beer-sheba, and there he called on the name of Jehovah, the Eternal God.
Verse_Ch: 21:34 亚伯拉罕在非利士人的地寄居了多日。 ###EN### And Abraham sojourned in the land of the Philistines many days.
Chapter_Header: 22
Verse_Ch: 22:1 这些事以后，神试验亚伯拉罕，对他说，亚伯拉罕。他说，我在这里。 ###EN### Now after these things God tested Abraham and said to him, Abraham. And he said, Here I am.
Verse_Ch: 22:2 神说，你带着你的儿子，就是你独生的儿子，你所爱的以撒，往摩利亚地去，在我所要指示你的山上，把他献为燔祭。 ###EN### And He said, Take now your son, your only son, whom you love, Isaac, and go to the land of Moriah and offer him there as a burnt offering on one of the
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: mountains of which I will tell you.
Verse_Ch: 22:3 亚伯拉罕清早起来，备上驴，带着两个仆人和他儿子以撒，也劈好了燔祭的柴，就起身往神所指示他的地方去。 ###EN### And Abraham rose early in the morning and saddled his donkey and took two of his young men with him and Isaac his son. And he split the wood for the burnt
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: offering and rose up and went to the place of which God had told him.
Verse_Ch: 22:4 到了第三日，亚伯拉罕举目远远的看见那地方。 ###EN### On the third day Abraham lifted up his eyes and saw the place from afar.
Verse_Ch: 22:5 亚伯拉罕对他的仆人说，你们和驴在这里等着，我与童子往那里去敬拜，然后回到你们这里来。 ###EN### And Abraham said to his young men, Stay here with the donkey; and I and the boy will go over there, and we will worship and then return to you.
Verse_Ch: 22:6 亚伯拉罕把燔祭的柴放在他儿子以撒身上，自己手里拿着火与刀；于是二人同行。 ###EN### And Abraham took the wood for the burnt offering and laid it upon Isaac his son. And he took in his hand the fire and the knife. And the two of them walked
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: together.
Verse_Ch: 22:7 以撒对他父亲亚伯拉罕说，父亲哪。亚伯拉罕说，我儿，我在这里。以撒说，请看，火与柴都有了，但燔祭的羊羔在那里？ ###EN### And Isaac spoke to Abraham his father and said, My father! And he said, Here I am, my son. And he said, The fire and the wood are here, but where is the lamb
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: for a burnt offering?
Verse_Ch: 22:8 亚伯拉罕说，我儿，神必自己预备作燔祭的羊羔。于是二人同行。 ###EN### And Abraham said, God Himself will provide the lamb for a burnt offering, my son. So the two of them walked on together.
Verse_Ch: 22:9 他们到了神所指示的地方，亚伯拉罕在那里筑坛，把柴摆好，就捆绑他的儿子以撒，放在坛的柴上。 ###EN### And they came to the place of which God had told him. And Abraham built the altar there and laid the wood in order and bound Isaac his son and laid him on
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: the altar on top of the wood.
Verse_Ch: 22:10 亚伯拉罕伸手拿刀，要杀他的儿子。 ###EN### And Abraham stretched out his hand and took the knife to slaughter his son.
Verse_Ch: 22:11 耶和华的使者从天上呼叫他说，亚伯拉罕！亚伯拉罕！他说，我在这里。 ###EN### And the Angel of Jehovah called to him from the heavens and said, Abraham, Abraham. And he said, Here I am.
Verse_Ch: 22:12 使者说，你不可在这童子身上下手，一点不可害他。现在我知道你是敬畏神的了，因为你没有将你的儿子，就是你独生的儿子，留下不给我。 ###EN### And he said, Do not stretch out your hand upon the boy, nor do anything to him; for now I know that you fear God, since you have not withheld your son, your
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: only son, from Me.
Verse_Ch: 22:13 亚伯拉罕举目观看，不料，在他后面有一只公羊，两角扣在树丛中，亚伯拉罕就去取了那只公羊来，献为燔祭，代替他的儿子。 ###EN### And Abraham lifted up his eyes and looked, and there behind him was a ram, caught in the thicket by its horns. And Abraham went and took the ram and
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: offered it up for a burnt offering in place of his son.
Verse_Ch: 22:14 亚伯拉罕给那地方起名叫耶和华以勒，直到今日人还说，在耶和华的山上必有预备。 ###EN### And Abraham called the name of that place Jehovah-jireh, as it is said to this day, On the mount of Jehovah it will be provided.
Verse_Ch: 22:15 耶和华的使者第二次从天上呼叫亚伯拉罕，说， ###EN### And the Angel of Jehovah called to Abraham a second time from the heavens
Verse_Ch: 22:16 耶和华宣示说，你既行了这事，不留下你的儿子，就是你独生的儿子，我指着自己起誓： ###EN### And said, By Myself I have sworn, declares Jehovah: Because you have done this thing and have not withheld your son, your only son,
Verse_Ch: 22:17 论福，我必赐福给你；论繁增，我必使你的后裔繁增，如同天上的星，海边的沙；你的后裔必得着仇敌的城门； ###EN### I will surely bless you and will greatly multiply your seed like the stars of the heavens and like the sand which is on the seashore; and your seed shall possess the
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: gate of his enemies.
Verse_Ch: 22:18 并且地上万国，都必因你的后裔得福；因为你听从了我的话。 ###EN### And in your seed all the nations of the earth shall be blessed, because you have obeyed My voice.
Verse_Ch: 22:19 于是亚伯拉罕回到他仆人那里，他们一同起身往别是巴去，亚伯拉罕就住在别是巴。 ###EN### So Abraham returned to his young men, and they rose up and went together to Beer-sheba. And Abraham dwelt in Beer-sheba.
Verse_Ch: 22:20 这些事以后，有人告诉亚伯拉罕说，密迦给你兄弟拿鹤生了几个儿子， ###EN### And after these things it was told Abraham, saying, Milcah has now also borne children to your brother Nahor:
Verse_Ch: 22:21 长子是乌斯，他的弟弟是布斯、亚兰的父亲基母利、 ###EN### Uz his firstborn and Buz his brother and Kemuel the father of Aram
Verse_Ch: 22:22 并基薛、哈琐、必达、益拉、彼土利。 ###EN### And Chesed and Hazo and Pildash and Jidlaph and Bethuel;
Verse_Ch: 22:23 彼土利生利百加，这八个人都是密迦给亚伯拉罕的兄弟拿鹤生的。 ###EN### And Bethuel begot Rebekah. These eight Milcah bore to Nahor, Abraham's brother.
Verse_Ch: 22:24 拿鹤的妾名叫流玛，生了提八、迦含、他辖和玛迦。 ###EN### And his concubine, whose name was Reumah, also bore Tebah and Gaham and Tahash and Maacah.
Chapter_Header: 23
Verse_Ch: 23:1 撒拉享寿一百二十七岁，这是撒拉一生的岁数。 ###EN### And the life of Sarah was one hundred twenty-seven years. These were the years of the life of Sarah.
Verse_Ch: 23:2 撒拉死在迦南地的基列亚巴，就是希伯仑。亚伯拉罕为她哀恸哭号。 ###EN### And Sarah died in Kiriath-arba (that is, Hebron) in the land of Canaan. And Abraham proceeded to mourn for Sarah and to weep for her.
Verse_Ch: 23:3 后来亚伯拉罕从死人面前起来，对赫人说， ###EN### Then Abraham rose up from before his dead wife and spoke to the children of Heth, saying,
Verse_Ch: 23:4 我在你们中间是外人，是寄居的，求你们让我在这里得着一块坟地，我好埋葬我的死人，使她不在我眼前。 ###EN### I am a stranger and a sojourner among you. Give me the possession of a burial place among you that I may bury my dead wife out of my sight.
Verse_Ch: 23:5 赫人回答亚伯拉罕说， ###EN### And the children of Heth answered Abraham, saying to him,
Verse_Ch: 23:6 我主请听，你在我们中间是神的王子，只管在我们最好的坟地埋葬你的死人；我们没有一人不容你在他的坟地埋葬你的死人。 ###EN### Hear us, my lord. You are a prince of God in our midst. In the choicest of our burial places bury your dead wife. None of us will withhold from you his burial place
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: for burying your dead wife.
Verse_Ch: 23:7 亚伯拉罕就起来，向那地的赫人下拜， ###EN### And Abraham rose up and bowed down to the people of the land, to the children of Heth.
Verse_Ch: 23:8 对他们说，你们若有意叫我埋葬我的死人，使她不在我眼前，就请听我的话，为我求琐辖的儿子以弗仑， ###EN### And he spoke with them, saying, If it is your desire that I should bury my dead wife out of my sight, hear me, and entreat for me Ephron the son of Zohar
Verse_Ch: 23:9 把他田地尽头那麦比拉洞给我；他可以按着足价卖给我，使我在你们中间得着一块坟地。 ###EN### That he would give me the cave of Machpelah, which is his, and which is at the end of his field. For the full price let him give it to me in your midst for the
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: possession of a burial place.
Verse_Ch: 23:10 当时以弗仑正坐在赫人中间。于是，赫人以弗仑在出入城门的赫人面前回答亚伯拉罕说， ###EN### Now Ephron was sitting in the midst of the children of Heth. And Ephron the Hittite answered Abraham in the hearing of the children of Heth, in the hearing of all
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: who went in at the gate of his city, saying,
Verse_Ch: 23:11 不然，我主请听，我送给你这块田，连田间的洞也送给你，在我同族的人面前都给你，可以埋葬你的死人。 ###EN### No, my lord, hear me. I give you the field and the cave that is in it, to you I give it. In the presence of the children of my people I give it to you; bury your dead wife.
Verse_Ch: 23:12 亚伯拉罕就在那地的人面前下拜， ###EN### And Abraham bowed down before the people of the land.
Verse_Ch: 23:13 在他们面前对以弗仑说，你若应允，请听我的话，我要把田价给你，求你收下，使我可以在那里埋葬我的死人。 ###EN### And he spoke to Ephron in the hearing of the people of the land, saying, But if you will, please hear me; I will give the price of the field. Take it from me, that I may
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: bury my dead wife there.
Verse_Ch: 23:14 以弗仑回答亚伯拉罕说， ###EN### And Ephron answered Abraham, saying to him,
Verse_Ch: 23:15 我主请听。值四百舍客勒银子的一块地，在你我中间还算什么呢？只管埋葬你的死人罢。 ###EN### My lord, listen to me. A piece of land worth four hundred shekels of silver, what is that between me and you? Therefore bury your dead wife.
Verse_Ch: 23:16 亚伯拉罕听从了以弗仑，照着他在赫人面前所题说的，把买卖通用的银子称了四百舍客勒给以弗仑。 ###EN### And Abraham listened to Ephron, and Abraham weighed out to Ephron the silver which he had named in the hearing of the children of Heth, four hundred
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: shekels of silver, current with the merchant.
Verse_Ch: 23:17 于是，在幔利前的麦比拉，以弗仑的那块田和其中的洞，并田间四围的树木， ###EN### So the field of Ephron, which was in Machpelah and which was before Mamre, the field and the cave which was in it and all the trees that were in the field, which
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: were in all its territory, were assured
Verse_Ch: 23:18 都定准归与亚伯拉罕为业，乃是他在出入城门的赫人面前买妥的。 ###EN### To Abraham for a possession in the presence of the children of Heth, in the presence of all who went in at the gate of his city.
Verse_Ch: 23:19 此后，亚伯拉罕把他妻子撒拉埋葬在迦南地幔利前，麦比拉田间的洞里。(幔利就是希伯仑。) ###EN### And after this, Abraham buried Sarah his wife in the cave of the field of Machpelah before Mamre (that is, Hebron) in the land of Canaan.
Verse_Ch: 23:20 从此，那块田和田间的洞，就定准从赫人归与亚伯拉罕为业，作坟地。 ###EN### And the field and the cave that is in it were assured to Abraham for the possession of a burial place from the children of Heth.
Chapter_Header: 24
Verse_Ch: 24:1 亚伯拉罕年纪老迈，向来在一切事上耶和华都赐福给他。 ###EN### And Abraham was old, and advanced in age. And Jehovah had blessed Abraham in all things.
Verse_Ch: 24:2 亚伯拉罕对管理他全业最老的仆人说，请你把手放在我大腿下。 ###EN### And Abraham said to his servant, the oldest of his house, who ruled over all that he had, Put your hand under my thigh;
Verse_Ch: 24:3 我要叫你指着耶和华天地的神起誓，不要从我所住这迦南人中，为我儿子娶他们的女子为妻。 ###EN### And I will make you swear by Jehovah, the God of heaven and the God of earth, that you will not take a wife for my son from the daughters of the Canaanites,
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: among whom I am dwelling.
Verse_Ch: 24:4 你要往我本地、亲族那里去，为我的儿子以撒娶一个妻子。 ###EN### But you shall go to my country and to my relatives, and take a wife for my son Isaac.
Verse_Ch: 24:5 仆人对他说，倘若女子不肯跟我到这地来，我必须将你的儿子带回你原出之地么？ ###EN### And the servant said to him, Perhaps the woman will not be willing to follow me to this land. Must I then take your son back to the land from where you came?
Verse_Ch: 24:6 亚伯拉罕对他说，你要谨慎，不要带我的儿子回那里去。 ###EN### And Abraham said to him, Be certain not to take my son back there.
Verse_Ch: 24:7 耶和华天上的神曾带领我离开父家和我的出生地，对我说话，向我起誓说，我要将这地赐给你的后裔。祂必差遣使者在你前面，你就可以从那里为我儿子娶一个妻子。 ###EN### Jehovah, the God of heaven, who took me from my father's house and from the land of my birth, and who spoke to me, and who swore to me, saying, To your
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: seed I will give this land, He will send His angel before you; and you shall take a wife for my son from there.
Verse_Ch: 24:8 倘若女子不肯跟你来，我使你起的这誓就与你无关了，只是不可带我的儿子回那里去。 ###EN### And if the woman is not willing to follow you, you shall be free from this oath of mine; only you shall not take my son back there.
Verse_Ch: 24:9 仆人就把手放在他主人亚伯拉罕的大腿下，为这事向他起誓。 ###EN### So the servant put his hand under the thigh of Abraham his master and swore to him concerning this matter.
Verse_Ch: 24:10 那仆人从他主人的骆驼中取了十匹骆驼，手里带了他主人各样的美物，就起身往米所波大米去，到了拿鹤的城。 ###EN### And the servant took ten camels from the camels of his master and departed, having all kinds of his master's good things in his hand. And he rose up and went
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: to Aram-naharaim, to the city of Nahor.
Verse_Ch: 24:11 天将晚，众女子出来打水的时候，他便叫骆驼跪在城外的水井旁。 ###EN### And he made the camels to kneel down outside the city by the well of water at the time of evening, at the time when women go out to draw water.
Verse_Ch: 24:12 他说，耶和华我主人亚伯拉罕的神阿，求你以恩慈待我主人亚伯拉罕，使我今日办事顺利。 ###EN### And he said, O Jehovah, the God of my master Abraham, Please grant me success today, and show kindness to my master Abraham.
Verse_Ch: 24:13 我现今站在水井旁，城内居民的女子们正出来打水。 ###EN### I am standing here by the spring of water as the daughters of the men of the city are coming out to draw water.
Verse_Ch: 24:14 我向那一个少女说，请你拿下水瓶，给我水喝；她若说，请喝，我也给你的骆驼喝；愿她就作你所定，给你仆人以撒的妻。这样，我便知道你以恩慈待我主人了。 ###EN### And may it be that the girl to whom I say, Please let down your pitcher that I may drink, and who says, Drink, and I will also give your camels a drink, may she be
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: the one whom You have appointed for Your servant, for Isaac; and in this I will know that You have shown kindness to my master.
Verse_Ch: 24:15 话还没有说完，不料，利百加肩头上扛着水瓶出来。利百加是彼土利所生的；彼土利是亚伯拉罕兄弟拿鹤妻子密迦的儿子。 ###EN### But before he had finished speaking, there was Rebekah, who was born to Bethuel the son of Milcah, the wife of Nahor, Abraham's brother, coming out with her
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: pitcher upon her shoulder.
Verse_Ch: 24:16 那少女容貌极其美丽，还是处女，未曾有人亲近她。她下到井旁，打满了瓶，又上来。 ###EN### And the girl was very beautiful in appearance, a virgin, and no man had known her. And she went down to the spring and filled her pitcher and came up.
Verse_Ch: 24:17 仆人跑上前去迎着她，说，求你将瓶里的水给我一点喝。 ###EN### And the servant ran to meet her and said, Please let me sip a little water from your pitcher.
Verse_Ch: 24:18 她说，我主请喝。就急忙拿下水瓶，托在手上给他喝。 ###EN### And she said, Drink, my lord. And she hurried and lowered her pitcher on her hand and gave him a drink.
Verse_Ch: 24:19 少女给他喝了，就说，我再为你的骆驼打水，叫骆驼也喝足。 ###EN### And when she had finished giving him a drink, she said, I will draw water for your camels also, until they have finished drinking.
Verse_Ch: 24:20 她就急忙把瓶里的水倒在槽里，又跑到井旁打水，为所有的骆驼打上水来。 ###EN### And she hurried and emptied her pitcher into the trough and ran again to the well to draw water, and she drew it for all his camels.
Verse_Ch: 24:21 那人定睛看她，一句话也不说，要晓得耶和华赐他亨通的道路没有。 ###EN### And the man gazed fixedly upon her in silence to know whether Jehovah had made his journey prosperous or not.
Verse_Ch: 24:22 等骆驼喝足了，那人就拿一个金鼻环，重半舍客勒，两个金手镯，重十舍客勒，给那少女， ###EN### And when the camels had finished drinking, the man took a golden nose-ring weighing half a shekel and two bracelets for her hands weighing ten gold shekels,
Verse_Ch: 24:23 说，请告诉我，你是谁的女儿？你父亲家里有我们住宿的地方没有？ ###EN### And said, Whose daughter are you? Please tell me, is there room in your father's house for us to lodge in?
Verse_Ch: 24:24 少女对他说，我是密迦与拿鹤之子彼土利的女儿； ###EN### And she said to him, I am the daughter of Bethuel the son of Milcah, whom she bore to Nahor.
Verse_Ch: 24:25 又说，我们家里足有草料和饲粮，也有住宿的地方。 ###EN### She also said to him, We have plenty of straw and fodder and also a place to lodge in.

UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: Jehovah has led me in the way to the house of my master's brothers.

UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: me, he went to the man. And there he was, standing by the camels at the spring.
Verse_Ch: 24:31 便对他说，你这蒙耶和华赐福的，请进来，为什么站在外边？我已经收拾了房屋，也为骆驼预备了地方。 ###EN### And he said, Come in, O blessed of Jehovah! Why do you stand outside when I have prepared the house and a place for the camels?

UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: men who were with him.

UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: them.

Verse_Ch: 25:29 有一天，雅各熬汤，以扫从田野回来累昏了。 ###EN### And Jacob cooked a stew. And Esau came in from the field, and he was faint.

Verse_Ch: 25:32 以扫说，我现在快死了，这长子的名分对我有什么用？ ###EN### And Esau said, I am now about to die, so of what use is this birthright to me?
Verse_Ch: 25:33 雅各说，你先对我起誓罢。以扫就对他起誓，把长子的名分卖给雅各。 ###EN### And Jacob said, First swear to me. And he swore to him and sold his birthright to Jacob.
Verse_Ch: 25:34 于是雅各将饼和红豆汤给了以扫，以扫吃了喝了，便起身走了。以扫就这样轻看了他长子的名分。 ###EN### And Jacob gave Esau bread and lentil stew, and he ate and drank and rose up and went away. Thus Esau despised his birthright.
Chapter_Header: 26
Verse_Ch: 26:1 在亚伯拉罕的日子，那地有过一次饥荒；这时又有饥荒，以撒就往基拉耳去，到非利士人的王亚比米勒那里。 ###EN### And there was a famine in the land, besides the former famine that had occurred in the days of Abraham. So Isaac went to Abimelech the king of the Philistines
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: at Gerar.
Verse_Ch: 26:2 耶和华向以撒显现，说，你不要下埃及去，要住在我所指示你的地。 ###EN### And Jehovah appeared to him and said, Do not go down to Egypt; dwell in the land of which I will tell you.
Verse_Ch: 26:3 你寄居在这地，我必与你同在，赐福给你，因为我要将这些地都赐给你和你的后裔；我必坚定我向你父亚伯拉罕所起的誓。 ###EN### Sojourn in this land, and I will be with you and will bless you; for to you and to your seed I will give all these lands, and I will establish the oath which I swore to
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: Abraham your father.
Verse_Ch: 26:4 我要使你的后裔繁增，如同天上的星那样多，又要将这些地都赐给你的后裔；并且地上万国必因你的后裔得福； ###EN### And I will multiply your seed as the stars of heaven and will give to your seed all these lands; and in your seed all the nations of the earth will be blessed,
Verse_Ch: 26:5 都因亚伯拉罕听从我的话，遵守我的吩咐、命令、律例、法度。 ###EN### Because Abraham obeyed My voice and kept My charge, My commandments, My statutes, and My laws.
Verse_Ch: 26:6 以撒就住在基拉耳。 ###EN### So Isaac dwelt in Gerar.
Verse_Ch: 26:7 那地方的人问到他的妻子，他便说，她是我的妹妹。原来他怕说，是我的妻子；他心里想，恐怕这地方的人为利百加的缘故杀我，因为她容貌美丽。 ###EN### And the men of the place asked about his wife. And he said, She is my sister, for he was afraid to say, My wife, thinking, The men of this place might slay me on
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: account of Rebekah, because she is beautiful in appearance.
Verse_Ch: 26:8 他在那里住了许久；有一天非利士人的王亚比米勒从窗户里往外观看，见以撒和他的妻子利百加戏玩。 ###EN### And when he had been there a long time, Abimelech the king of the Philistines looked out through his window and saw, and there was Isaac playfully caressing
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: Rebekah his wife.
Verse_Ch: 26:9 亚比米勒召了以撒来，说，她实在是你的妻子，你怎么说她是你的妹妹？以撒对他说，因为我想，恐怕我会因她而死。 ###EN### And Abimelech called Isaac and said, So she is indeed your wife. How then did you say, She is my sister? And Isaac said to him, Because I thought I might die on
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: account of her.
Verse_Ch: 26:10 亚比米勒说，你向我们作的是什么事？民中有人险些和你的妻同寝，那样你就使我们陷在罪里。 ###EN### And Abimelech said, What is this you have done to us? One of the people might easily have lain with your wife, and you would have brought guilt upon us.
Verse_Ch: 26:11 于是亚比米勒吩咐众民说，凡触犯这个人或他妻子的，定要把他治死。 ###EN### And Abimelech charged all the people, saying, He who touches this man or his wife shall surely be put to death.
Verse_Ch: 26:12 以撒在那地撒种，那一年有百倍的收成。耶和华赐福给他， ###EN### And Isaac sowed in that land and reaped in the same year a hundredfold. And Jehovah blessed him,
Verse_Ch: 26:13 他就昌大，越发昌盛，成了巨富。 ###EN### And the man became rich and continued to grow richer until he became very rich.
Verse_Ch: 26:14 他有羊群、牛群，又有许多仆婢，非利士人就嫉妒他。 ###EN### And he had possessions of flocks and possessions of herds and a great household, so that the Philistines envied him.
Verse_Ch: 26:15 当他父亲亚伯拉罕在世的日子，他父亲的仆人所挖的井，非利士人全都塞住，填满了土。 ###EN### Now all the wells which his father's servants had dug in the days of Abraham his father the Philistines had stopped up and filled with earth.
Verse_Ch: 26:16 亚比米勒对以撒说，你离开我们去罢，因为你比我们强盛得多。 ###EN### And Abimelech said to Isaac, Go away from us, for you are much mightier than we.
Verse_Ch: 26:17 以撒就离开那里，在基拉耳谷支搭帐棚，住在那里。 ###EN### So Isaac went away from there and camped in the valley of Gerar and dwelt there.
Verse_Ch: 26:18 当他父亲亚伯拉罕在世之日所挖的水井，因非利士人在亚伯拉罕死后塞住了，以撒就重新挖出来，仍照他父亲所起的，叫那些井的名字。 ###EN### And Isaac dug again the wells of water which had been dug in the days of Abraham his father, and which the Philistines had stopped up after the death of
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: Abraham; and he called them by the same names which his father had given them.
Verse_Ch: 26:19 以撒的仆人在谷中挖掘，得了一口活水井。 ###EN### And Isaac's servants dug in the valley and found there a well of flowing water.
Verse_Ch: 26:20 基拉耳的牧人与以撒的牧人争闹，说，这水是我们的。以撒就给那井起名叫埃色，因为他们和他相争。 ###EN### And the shepherds of Gerar strove with Isaac's shepherds, saying, The water is ours. So he called the name of the well Esek, because they contended with him.
Verse_Ch: 26:21 以撒的仆人又挖了一口井，他们又为这井争闹，因此以撒给这井起名叫西提拿。 ###EN### And they dug another well; and they strove over that also, so he called the name of it Sitnah.
Verse_Ch: 26:22 以撒离开那里，又挖了一口井，他们不为这井争闹了，他就给那井起名叫利河伯。他说，耶和华现在给我们宽阔之地，我们必在这地繁衍。 ###EN### And he moved away from there and dug another well, but they did not strive over it, so he called the name of it Rehoboth; and he said, Now Jehovah has made
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: room for us, and we will be fruitful in the land.
Verse_Ch: 26:23 以撒从那里上别是巴去。 ###EN### And he went up from there to Beer-sheba.
Verse_Ch: 26:24 当夜耶和华向他显现，说，我是你父亲亚伯拉罕的神，不要惧怕，因为我与你同在，必赐福给你，并要为我仆人亚伯拉罕的缘故，使你的后裔繁增。 ###EN### And Jehovah appeared to him the same night and said, I am the God of Abraham your father. Do not be afraid, for I am with you, and I will bless you and
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: multiply your seed for My servant Abraham's sake.
Verse_Ch: 26:25 以撒就在那里筑了一座坛，呼求耶和华的名，并且支搭帐棚；他的仆人便在那里挖了一口井。 ###EN### And he built an altar there and called upon the name of Jehovah and pitched his tent there. And there Isaac's servants dug a well.
Verse_Ch: 26:26 亚比米勒同他的谋士亚户撒、和他的军长非各，从基拉耳来见以撒。 ###EN### And Abimelech came to him from Gerar with Ahuzzath his adviser and Phicol the captain of his army.
Verse_Ch: 26:27 以撒对他们说，你们既然恨我，打发我走了，为什么到我这里来？ ###EN### And Isaac said to them, Why have you come to me, since you hate me and have sent me away from you?
Verse_Ch: 26:28 他们说，我们明明看见耶和华与你同在；所以我们说，我们不如两下彼此起誓，让我们与你立约， ###EN### And they said, We see plainly that Jehovah is with you; so we say, Let there now be an oath between us, even between us and you, and let us make a covenant
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: with you,
Verse_Ch: 26:29 使你不侵害我们，正如我们未曾触犯你，一味的善待你，并且打发你平平安安的走了。你是蒙耶和华赐福的了。 ###EN### That you will not do us any harm, just as we have not touched you, and just as we have done to you nothing but good and have sent you away in peace. You are
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: now the blessed of Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 26:30 以撒就为他们设摆筵席，他们便吃了喝了。 ###EN### And he made them a feast, and they ate and drank.
Verse_Ch: 26:31 他们清早起来彼此起誓。以撒打发他们走，他们就平平安安的离开他走了。 ###EN### And they rose up early in the morning and swore to one another. And Isaac sent them away, and they departed from him in peace.
Verse_Ch: 26:32 那一天，以撒的仆人来，将挖井的事告诉他说，我们得了水了。 ###EN### And the same day Isaac's servants came and told him about the well which they had dug and said to him, We have found water.
Verse_Ch: 26:33 他就给那井起名叫示巴；因此那城名叫别是巴，直到今日。 ###EN### And he called it Shibah. Therefore the name of the city is Beer-sheba to this day.
Verse_Ch: 26:34 以扫四十岁的时候娶了赫人比利的女儿犹滴，与赫人以伦的女儿巴实抹为妻。 ###EN### Now when Esau was forty years old, he took as wife Judith the daughter of Beeri the Hittite and Basemath the daughter of Elon the Hittite.
Verse_Ch: 26:35 她们使以撒和利百加灵里苦恼。 ###EN### And they caused bitterness of spirit to Isaac and to Rebekah.
Chapter_Header: 27
Verse_Ch: 27:1 以撒年老，眼睛昏花，不能看见，就叫了他大儿子以扫来，对他说，我儿。以扫说，我在这里。 ###EN### Now when Isaac was old, and his eyes had become so dim that he could not see, he called Esau his older son and said to him, My son. And he said to him, Here
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: I am.
Verse_Ch: 27:2 他说，我如今老了，不知道那一天死。 ###EN### And he said, Behold now, I am old, and I do not know the day of my death.
Verse_Ch: 27:3 现在拿你的器械，就是箭囊和弓，往田野去为我打些野味来， ###EN### Now then, please take your weapons, your quiver and your bow, and go out to the field, and hunt game for me,

Verse_Ch: 27:5 以撒对他儿子以扫说话的时候，利百加一直在听着。所以当以扫往田野去打猎，要得野味带回来， ###EN### Now Rebekah had been listening when Isaac spoke to Esau his son. So when Esau went to the field to hunt for game to bring it home,

Verse_Ch: 27:7 你去把野味带来，作成美味给我吃，我好在未死之前，在耶和华面前给你祝福。 ###EN### Bring me game, and prepare for me a tasty meal so that I may eat it and bless you before Jehovah before my death.
Verse_Ch: 27:8 现在，我儿，你要照着我所吩咐你的，听从我的话。 ###EN### Now therefore, my son, obey my voice, according to that which I command you.
Verse_Ch: 27:9 你到羊群去，给我拿两只肥山羊羔来，我便照你父亲所爱的，给他作成美味。 ###EN### Go now to the flock, and take two choice kids for me from there, and I will prepare them as a tasty meal for your father, such as he loves.
Verse_Ch: 27:10 你拿到你父亲那里给他吃，使他可以在未死之前给你祝福。 ###EN### Then you shall bring it to your father to eat, so that he may bless you before his death.
Verse_Ch: 27:11 雅各对他母亲利百加说，你看，我哥哥以扫浑身是有毛的，我身上是光滑的； ###EN### And Jacob said to Rebekah his mother, Behold, Esau my brother is a hairy man, and I am a smooth man.
Verse_Ch: 27:12 倘若我父亲摸着我，必以我为欺哄人的，我就招来咒诅，不得祝福。 ###EN### Perhaps my father will feel me, and I will be as a deceiver in his sight, and I will bring upon myself a curse and not a blessing.
Verse_Ch: 27:13 他母亲对他说，我儿，你招的咒诅归到我身上；你只管听我的话，去把羊羔给我拿来。 ###EN### And his mother said to him, Your curse be on me, my son; only obey my voice, and go, get them for me.
Verse_Ch: 27:14 他便去拿来，交给他母亲；他母亲就照他父亲所爱的，作成美味， ###EN### And he went and got them and brought them to his mother; and his mother prepared a tasty meal, such as his father loved.
Verse_Ch: 27:15 利百加又把家里她所存大儿子以扫上好的衣服，给她小儿子雅各穿上； ###EN### And Rebekah took the best clothes of Esau her older son, which were with her in the house, and put them on Jacob her younger son.

Verse_Ch: 27:17 就把所作的美味和饼，交在她儿子雅各的手里。 ###EN### And she put the tasty meal and the bread that she had prepared into the hand of Jacob her son.
Verse_Ch: 27:18 雅各到他父亲那里说，我父亲。他说，我在这里。我儿，你是谁？ ###EN### And he came to his father and said, My father. And he said, Here I am. Who are you, my son?
Verse_Ch: 27:19 雅各对他父亲说，我是你的长子以扫；我已照你所吩咐我的行了。请起来坐着，吃我的野味，好给我祝福。 ###EN### And Jacob said to his father, I am Esau your firstborn; I have done as you told me. Now rise up; sit up and eat some of my game, so that you may bless me.
Verse_Ch: 27:20 以撒对他儿子说，我儿，你怎么找得这么快？他说，因为耶和华你的神使我遇见好机会得着的。 ###EN### And Isaac said to his son, How is it that you have found it so quickly, my son? And he said, Because Jehovah your God put it in my way.

Verse_Ch: 27:22 雅各就挨近他父亲以撒。以撒摸着他，说，声音是雅各的声音，手却是以扫的手。 ###EN### And Jacob came near to Isaac his father. And he felt him and said, The voice is Jacob's voice, but the hands are Esau's hands.

Verse_Ch: 27:24 又说，你真是我儿子以扫么？他说，我是。 ###EN### And he said, Are you really my son Esau? And he said, I am.

UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: drank.
Verse_Ch: 27:26 他父亲以撒对他说，我儿，你上前来与我亲嘴。 ###EN### Then his father Isaac said to him, Please come near and kiss me, my son.
Verse_Ch: 27:27 他就上前与父亲亲嘴，他父亲一闻他衣服上的香气，就给他祝福，说，我儿的香气如同耶和华赐福之田地的香气一样。 ###EN### So he came near and kissed him; and when Isaac smelled the smell of his garments, he blessed him and said, See, the smell of my son-Like the smell of a field
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: Which Jehovah has blessed.
Verse_Ch: 27:28 愿神赐你天上的甘露，地上的肥土，并丰盈的五谷和新酒。 ###EN### And may God give you Of the dew of heaven and of the fatness of the earth, And an abundance of grain and new wine.
Verse_Ch: 27:29 愿多民服事你，多国跪拜你。愿你作你弟兄的主，你母亲的儿子向你跪拜。凡咒诅你的，愿他受咒诅；为你祝福的，愿他蒙福。 ###EN### Let peoples serve you, And nations bow down to you. Be lord over your brothers, And let your mother's sons bow down to you. Cursed be those who curse you,
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: And blessed be those who bless you.

UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: then I will slay my brother Jacob.

UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: bereaved of both of you in one day?

UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: of the land, what good will my life be to me?
Chapter_Header: 28
Verse_Ch: 28:1 以撒叫了雅各来，给他祝福，并嘱咐他说，你不要娶迦南的女子为妻。 ###EN### And Isaac called Jacob and blessed him; and he charged him and said to him, You shall not take a wife from the daughters of Canaan.
Verse_Ch: 28:2 你起身往巴旦亚兰去，到你外祖父彼土利家里，在你母舅拉班的女儿中娶一个为妻。 ###EN### Rise up, go to Paddan-aram, to the house of Bethuel your mother's father; and take from there a wife from the daughters of Laban your mother's brother.
Verse_Ch: 28:3 愿全足的神赐福给你，使你繁衍增多，成为多族； ###EN### And may the All-sufficient God bless you and make you fruitful and multiply you, that you may become a company of peoples.
Verse_Ch: 28:4 愿祂将应许亚伯拉罕的福赐给你和你的后裔，使你承受你所寄居的地为业，就是神赐给亚伯拉罕的地。 ###EN### And may He give you the blessing of Abraham, to you and to your seed with you, that you may possess the land of your sojournings, which God gave to
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: Abraham.
Verse_Ch: 28:5 以撒打发雅各走了，他就往巴旦亚兰去，到亚兰人彼土利的儿子拉班那里；拉班是雅各、以扫的母亲利百加的哥哥。 ###EN### And Isaac sent Jacob away, and he went to Paddan-aram, to Laban the son of Bethuel the Aramaean, the brother of Rebekah, Jacob's and Esau's mother.
Verse_Ch: 28:6 以扫见以撒已经给雅各祝福，打发他往巴旦亚兰去，在那里娶妻，并见以撒祝福的时候嘱咐他说，不要娶迦南的女子为妻， ###EN### Now Esau saw that Isaac had blessed Jacob and had sent him away to Paddan-aram to take a wife from there, and that when he blessed him, he charged him,
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: saying, You shall not take a wife from the daughters of Canaan,
Verse_Ch: 28:7 又见雅各听从父母的话，往巴旦亚兰去了， ###EN### And that Jacob had obeyed his father and his mother and had gone to Paddan-aram.
Verse_Ch: 28:8 以扫就看出他父亲以撒不喜欢迦南的女子， ###EN### So Esau saw that the daughters of Canaan displeased Isaac his father.
Verse_Ch: 28:9 便往以实玛利那里去，在他两个妻子之外，又娶了玛哈拉为妻。她是亚伯拉罕儿子以实玛利的女儿，尼拜约的妹妹。 ###EN### Then Esau went to Ishmael and took Mahalath the daughter of Ishmael, Abraham's son, and the sister of Nebaioth to be his wife, in addition to the wives that he
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: had.
Verse_Ch: 28:10 雅各出了别是巴，向哈兰走去； ###EN### And Jacob went out from Beer-sheba and went toward Haran.
Verse_Ch: 28:11 到了一个地方，因为太阳落了，就在那里过夜；他拾起那地方的一块石头枕在头下，在那里躺卧睡了。 ###EN### And he came to a certain place and spent the night there, because the sun had set; and he took one of the stones of the place and put it under his head, and he
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: lay down in that place.
Verse_Ch: 28:12 他梦见一个梯子立在地上，梯子的顶通着天，有神的使者在梯子上，上去下来。 ###EN### And he dreamed: There was a ladder set up on the earth, and its top reached to heaven; and there the angels of God were ascending and descending on it.
Verse_Ch: 28:13 耶和华站在梯子以上，说，我是耶和华你祖亚伯拉罕的神，也是以撒的神；我要将你现在所躺卧之地，赐给你和你的后裔。 ###EN### And there was Jehovah, standing above it; and He said, I am Jehovah, the God of Abraham your father and the God of Isaac. The land on which you lie, I will give
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: to you and to your seed.
Verse_Ch: 28:14 你的后裔必像地上的尘沙那样多，必向东西南北开展；地上万族必因你和你的后裔得福。 ###EN### And your seed will be as the dust of the earth, and you will spread abroad to the west and to the east and to the north and to the south, and in you and in your
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: seed will all the families of the earth be blessed.
Verse_Ch: 28:15 看哪，我与你同在；你无论往那里去，我必保守你，使你归回这地。我总不离弃你，直到我成就了向你所应许的。 ###EN### And, behold, I am with you and will keep you wherever you go and will cause you to return to this land, for I will not leave you until I have done what I have
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: promised you.
Verse_Ch: 28:16 雅各睡醒了，就说，耶和华真在这地方，我竟不知道。 ###EN### And Jacob awoke from his sleep and said, Surely Jehovah is in this place, and I did not know it.
Verse_Ch: 28:17 他就惧怕，说，这地方何等可畏！这不是别的，乃是神的家，也是天的门。 ###EN### And he was afraid and said, How awesome is this place! This is none other than the house of God, and this is the gate of heaven.
Verse_Ch: 28:18 雅各清早起来，把所枕的石头立作柱子，浇油在上面。 ###EN### And Jacob rose up early in the morning and took the stone that he had put under his head, and he set it up as a pillar and poured oil on top of it.
Verse_Ch: 28:19 他就给那地方起名叫伯特利；但那城起先名叫路斯。 ###EN### And he called the name of that place Bethel, but the name of the city was Luz previously.
Verse_Ch: 28:20 雅各许愿说，神若与我同在，在我去的路上保守我，又给我食物吃，衣服穿， ###EN### And Jacob vowed a vow, saying, If God will be with me and will keep me in this way that I go and will give me bread to eat and garments to put on,
Verse_Ch: 28:21 使我平平安安的回到我父亲的家，我就必以耶和华为我的神。 ###EN### So that I return to my father's house in peace, then Jehovah will be my God,
Verse_Ch: 28:22 我所立为柱子的石头也必作神的家；凡你所赐给我的，我必将十分之一献给你。 ###EN### And this stone, which I have set up as a pillar, will be God's house; and of all that You give me I will surely give one tenth to You.
Chapter_Header: 29
Verse_Ch: 29:1 雅各往前行，到了东方人之地， ###EN### Then Jacob went on his journey and came to the land of the children of the east.
Verse_Ch: 29:2 看见田间有一口井，有三群羊卧在井旁；因为人都是用那井里的水给羊群喝。井口上的石头很大。 ###EN### And he looked, and there in the field was a well, and there three flocks of sheep were lying beside it; for from that well they watered the flocks. And the stone on
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: the mouth of the well was large.
Verse_Ch: 29:3 当所有的羊群在那里聚齐了，人就把石头转离井口，给羊喝水，随后又把石头放回井口原处。 ###EN### And when all the flocks would gather there, they would roll the stone from the mouth of the well and water the sheep; then they would put the stone back on the
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: mouth of the well in its place.

Verse_Ch: 29:5 他问他们说，拿鹤的孙子拉班，你们认识么？他们说，我们认识。 ###EN### And he said to them, Do you know Laban the son of Nahor? And they said, We do know him.

Verse_Ch: 29:7 雅各说，你们看，日头还高，不是聚集牲口的时候，你们不如给羊喝了水，再去牧放。 ###EN### And he said, Look, it is still full day; and it is not time for the livestock to be gathered together. Water the sheep, and go feed them.
Verse_Ch: 29:8 他们说，我们不能，必须等羊群都聚齐，人把石头转离井口，那时才可给羊喝水。 ###EN### And they said, We cannot until all the flocks are gathered together and they roll the stone from the mouth of the well; then we water the sheep.
Verse_Ch: 29:9 雅各正和他们说话的时候，拉结领着她父亲的羊来了，因为那些羊是她牧放的。 ###EN### While he was still speaking with them, Rachel came with the sheep which belonged to her father, for she was a shepherdess.
Verse_Ch: 29:10 雅各看见母舅拉班的女儿拉结和母舅拉班的羊群，就上前把石头转离井口，给他母舅拉班的羊群喝水。 ###EN### Now when Jacob saw Rachel the daughter of Laban his mother's brother and the sheep of Laban his mother's brother, Jacob drew near and rolled the stone
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: from the mouth of the well, and watered the flock of Laban his mother's brother.
Verse_Ch: 29:11 雅各与拉结亲嘴，就放声而哭。 ###EN### Then Jacob kissed Rachel and lifted up his voice and wept.
Verse_Ch: 29:12 雅各告诉拉结，自己是她父亲的外甥，是利百加的儿子；拉结就跑去告诉她父亲。 ###EN### And Jacob told Rachel that he was her father's relative and that he was Rebekah's son. And she ran and told her father.
Verse_Ch: 29:13 拉班听见外甥雅各的消息，就跑去迎接，抱着他，与他亲嘴，领他到自己的家。雅各将一切的情由告诉了拉班。 ###EN### And when Laban heard the news of Jacob his sister's son, he ran to meet him. And he embraced him and kissed him and brought him to his house. Then Jacob
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: related to Laban all these things.
Verse_Ch: 29:14 拉班对他说，你实在是我的骨肉。雅各就和他同住了一个月。 ###EN### And Laban said to him, Surely you are my bone and my flesh. And he stayed with him a month.
Verse_Ch: 29:15 拉班对雅各说，你虽是我的外甥，岂可白白的服事我？请告诉我，你要什么为工价？ ###EN### And Laban said to Jacob, Because you are my relative, should you therefore serve me for nothing? Tell me, what shall your wages be?
Verse_Ch: 29:16 拉班有两个女儿，大的名叫利亚，小的名叫拉结。 ###EN### Now Laban had two daughters; the name of the older was Leah, and the name of the younger was Rachel.
Verse_Ch: 29:17 利亚的眼睛没有神气，拉结却生得形貌美丽。 ###EN### And Leah's eyes were dull, but Rachel was beautiful in form and beautiful in appearance.

Verse_Ch: 29:19 拉班说，我把她给你，胜过给别人；你与我同住罢。 ###EN### And Laban said, It is better that I give her to you than that I should give her to another man; stay with me.

Verse_Ch: 29:24 拉班又将自己的婢女悉帕给女儿利亚作使女。 ###EN### And Laban gave Zilpah his female servant to his daughter Leah to be her female servant.

UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: deceived me?
Verse_Ch: 29:26 拉班说，大女儿还没有给人，先把小女儿给人，在我们这地方没有这样作的。 ###EN### And Laban said, It is not done in this way in our place, to give the younger before the firstborn.

UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: was called Levi.

Chapter_Header: 30
Verse_Ch: 30:1 拉结见自己没有给雅各生孩子，就嫉妒她姐姐，对雅各说，你给我孩子，不然我就死了。 ###EN### And when Rachel saw that she bore Jacob no children, Rachel envied her sister and said to Jacob, Give me children, or else I die.
Verse_Ch: 30:2 雅各向拉结生气，说，叫你不怀胎的是神，我岂能代替祂作主呢？拉结说， ###EN### And Jacob's anger burned against Rachel, and he said, Am I in the place of God, who has withheld from you the fruit of the womb?
Verse_Ch: 30:3 有我的使女辟拉在这里，你可以与她同房，使她生子抱在我膝上，我便因她也得孩子。 ###EN### And she said, Here is my servant Bilhah; go in to her, that she may bear upon my knees and that I also may have children through her.
Verse_Ch: 30:4 拉结就把她的使女辟拉给丈夫为妻，雅各便与她同房。 ###EN### And she gave him Bilhah her female servant as a wife, and Jacob went in to her.
Verse_Ch: 30:5 辟拉就怀孕，给雅各生了一个儿子。 ###EN### And Bilhah conceived and bore Jacob a son.

Verse_Ch: 30:9 利亚见自己停了生育，就把她的使女悉帕给雅各为妻。 ###EN### Now when Leah saw that she ceased bearing, she took Zilpah her female servant and gave her to Jacob as a wife.

Verse_Ch: 30:13 利亚说，我真快乐，众女子都要称我为有福，于是给孩子起名叫亚设。 ###EN### And Leah said, Happy am I! For the daughters will call me blessed; so she called his name Asher.
Verse_Ch: 30:14 收割麦子的时候，流便出去，在田里寻见风茄，就拿来给他母亲利亚。拉结对利亚说，请你把你儿子的风茄给我一些。 ###EN### And Reuben went out in the days of wheat harvest and found mandrakes in the field and brought them to his mother Leah. Then Rachel said to Leah, Please give
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: me some of your son's mandrakes.
Verse_Ch: 30:15 利亚说，你夺了我的丈夫还算小事么？你又要夺我儿子的风茄？拉结说，那么，为了交换你儿子的风茄，今夜他可以与你同寝。 ###EN### And she said to her, Is it a small matter that you have taken away my husband? And would you take away my son's mandrakes also? So Rachel said, Then he
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: may lie with you tonight in return for your son's mandrakes.
Verse_Ch: 30:16 到了晚上，雅各从田里回来，利亚出来迎接他，说，你要与我同寝，因为我实在是用我儿子的风茄把你雇下了。那一夜，雅各就与她同寝。 ###EN### And Jacob came from the field in the evening, and Leah went out to meet him and said, You must come in to me, for I have surely hired you with my son's
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: mandrakes. So he lay with her that night.

Verse_Ch: 30:22 神记念拉结，垂听了她，使她能生育。 ###EN### Then God remembered Rachel, and God gave heed to her and opened her womb.
Verse_Ch: 30:23 拉结怀孕生子，说，神除去了我的羞辱， ###EN### And she conceived and bore a son and said, God has taken away my reproach.
Verse_Ch: 30:24 就给他起名叫约瑟，说，愿耶和华再给我增添一个儿子。 ###EN### And she called his name Joseph, saying, May Jehovah add to me another son.
Verse_Ch: 30:25 拉结生约瑟之后，雅各对拉班说，请打发我走，叫我回到我本乡本地去。 ###EN### And when Rachel had borne Joseph, Jacob said to Laban, Send me away, that I may go to my own place and to my own country.
Verse_Ch: 30:26 请你把我服事你所得的妻子和儿女给我，让我走；我怎样服事你，你都知道。 ###EN### Give me my wives and my children for whom I have served you, that I may go; for you indeed know my service by which I have served you.
Verse_Ch: 30:27 拉班对他说，我若在你眼前蒙恩，请你仍与我同住，因为我已算定，耶和华赐福与我是因你的缘故； ###EN### And Laban said to him, If you please, I have divined that Jehovah has blessed me on account of you.
Verse_Ch: 30:28 又说，请你指明你的工价，我就给你。 ###EN### And he said, Name me your wages, and I will give it.
Verse_Ch: 30:29 雅各对他说，我怎样服事你，你的牲口在我手里怎样，你是知道的。 ###EN### And Jacob said to him, You indeed know how I have served you, and how your livestock have fared with me.
Verse_Ch: 30:30 我未来之前，你所有的很少，现今却发达增多，耶和华随我的脚步赐福与你。如今，我什么时候也为自己的家作些事呢？ ###EN### For you had little before I came, and it has spread into a multitude, and Jehovah has blessed you wherever I turned. But now when shall I provide for my own
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: house also?
Verse_Ch: 30:31 拉班说，我当给你什么？雅各说，你什么也不必给我；只要你为我作这一件事，我便仍旧牧放看守你的羊群。 ###EN### And he said, What shall I give you? And Jacob said, You shall not give me anything. Just do this one thing for me: Let me again feed your flock and keep it.
Verse_Ch: 30:32 今天我要走遍你的羊群，把其中凡有点的、有斑的，就是绵羊中黑色的，并山羊中有斑的、有点的，都挑出来；将来这一等的就算是我的工价。 ###EN### Let me pass through all your flock today, removing from there every speckled and spotted animal, that is, every black animal among the sheep, and the spotted
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: and speckled among the goats; and such will be my wages.
Verse_Ch: 30:33 以后你来查看我的工价，凡在我手里的山羊不是有点有斑的，绵羊不是黑色的，那就算是我偷的；这样便可证出我的公义。 ###EN### So my righteousness will testify for me later, when you come concerning my wages, by what is before you. Every one that is not speckled and spotted among the
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: goats and black among the sheep, if found with me, will be counted stolen.
Verse_Ch: 30:34 拉班说，好阿，就照着你的话行罢。 ###EN### And Laban said, Fine; let it be according to your word.
Verse_Ch: 30:35 当日，拉班把有纹的、有斑的公山羊，有点的、有斑的母山羊，就是凡杂有白色的山羊，并黑色的绵羊，都挑出来，交在他儿子们的手下， ###EN### But on that day he removed the male goats that were streaked and spotted, and all the female goats that were speckled and spotted, every one that had white
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: in it, and all the black ones among the sheep, and gave them into the care of his sons;
Verse_Ch: 30:36 又使自己和雅各相离三天的路程；雅各就牧养拉班其余的羊。 ###EN### And he set a distance of a three days' journey between himself and Jacob, and Jacob fed the rest of Laban's flocks.
Verse_Ch: 30:37 雅各拿杨树、杏树、枫树的嫩枝，将皮剥成白纹，使枝子露出白的来； ###EN### And Jacob took rods of fresh poplar and almond and plane trees and peeled white stripes in them, exposing the white which was in the rods.
Verse_Ch: 30:38 他将剥了皮的枝子，对着羊群，插在羊群喝水的水槽里；羊来喝水的时候，公母交配。 ###EN### And he set the rods which he had peeled in front of the flocks in the troughs, that is, in the watering places where the flocks came to drink; and they bred when
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: they came to drink.
Verse_Ch: 30:39 羊对着枝子交配，就生下有纹的、有点的、有斑的来。 ###EN### And the flocks bred before the rods; and the flocks brought forth young that were streaked, speckled, and spotted.
Verse_Ch: 30:40 雅各把羊羔分出来，使拉班的羊与这有纹和黑色的羊相对，把自己的羊另放一处，不叫他的羊和拉班的羊混杂。 ###EN### And Jacob separated the lambs and set the faces of the flock toward the streaked and all the black in the flock of Laban, and he put his own herds apart and did
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: not put them with Laban's flock.
Verse_Ch: 30:41 当羊群中肥壮的交配的时候，雅各就把枝子插在水槽里，正在羊群的眼前，使羊对着枝子交配。 ###EN### And whenever the stronger of the flock were breeding, Jacob placed the rods before the eyes of the flock in the troughs so that they might breed among the rods;
Verse_Ch: 30:42 只是在羊群瘦弱的时候，就不插枝子。这样，瘦弱的就归拉班，肥壮的就归雅各。 ###EN### But when the flock was feebler, he did not put them in; so the feebler were Laban's, and the stronger Jacob's.
Verse_Ch: 30:43 于是雅各极其发达，得了许多的羊群、仆人、婢女、骆驼和驴。 ###EN### And the man became spread out exceedingly, and had large flocks, and female servants and male servants, and camels and donkeys.
Chapter_Header: 31
Verse_Ch: 31:1 雅各听见拉班的儿子们有话说，雅各把我们父亲所有的都夺去了，他是从我们父亲所有的得了这一切的财富； ###EN### Now Jacob heard the words of Laban's sons, saying, Jacob has taken away all that belonged to our father; and from what belonged to our father he has made
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: all this wealth.
Verse_Ch: 31:2 并且雅各见拉班的脸色向他不如从前了。 ###EN### And Jacob saw Laban's countenance, and now it was not favorable toward him as previously.
Verse_Ch: 31:3 耶和华对雅各说，你要回你祖你父之地，到你亲族那里去，我必与你同在。 ###EN### And Jehovah said to Jacob, Return to the land of your fathers and to your relatives, and I will be with you.
Verse_Ch: 31:4 雅各就打发人，叫拉结和利亚到田野他的羊群那里去， ###EN### So Jacob sent and called Rachel and Leah to his flock in the field,
Verse_Ch: 31:5 对她们说，我看你们父亲的脸色向我不如从前了；但我父亲的神向来与我同在。 ###EN### And he said to them, I see that your father's countenance is not favorable toward me as previously, but the God of my father has been with me.
Verse_Ch: 31:6 你们自己也知道，我尽了我的力量服事你们的父亲。 ###EN### And you yourselves know that with all my strength I have served your father.
Verse_Ch: 31:7 你们的父亲欺哄我，十次改了我的工价；然而神不容许他害我。 ###EN### And your father has cheated me and changed my wages ten times, but God did not allow him to harm me.
Verse_Ch: 31:8 他若说，有点的归你作工价，羊群所生的都有点；他若说，有纹的归你作工价，羊群所生的都有纹。 ###EN### If he spoke in this way, The speckled shall be your wages, then all the flock bore speckled; and if he spoke in this way, The streaked shall be your wages, then all
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: the flock bore streaked.
Verse_Ch: 31:9 这样，神把你们父亲的牲畜夺来赐给我了。 ###EN### Thus God has taken away your father's livestock and given them to me.
Verse_Ch: 31:10 羊群交配的时候，我在梦中举目一看，见跳母羊的公山羊都是有纹的、有点的、有花斑的。 ###EN### And at the time the flock was breeding, I lifted up my eyes and saw in a dream; and there were the male goats, leaping upon the flock-streaked, speckled, and
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: spotted.
Verse_Ch: 31:11 神的使者在那梦中对我说，雅各。我说，我在这里。 ###EN### And the Angel of God said to me in the dream, Jacob; and I said, Here I am.
Verse_Ch: 31:12 祂说，你举目观看，跳母羊的公山羊都是有纹的、有点的、有花斑的；凡拉班向你所作的，我都看见了。 ###EN### And He said, Lift up now your eyes, and see that all the male goats which leap upon the flock are streaked, speckled, and spotted; for I have seen all that Laban
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: has been doing to you.
Verse_Ch: 31:13 我是伯特利的神；你在那里用油抹过柱子，向我许过愿。现在你起来，离开这地，回你的出生地去罢。 ###EN### I am the God of Bethel, where you anointed a pillar, where you vowed a vow to Me. Rise up now; go out from this land, and return to the land of your birth.
Verse_Ch: 31:14 拉结和利亚回答雅各说，在我们父亲的家里还有我们可得的分么？还有我们的产业么？ ###EN### And Rachel and Leah answered and said to him, Do we still have any portion or inheritance in our father's house?
Verse_Ch: 31:15 我们不是被他当作外人么？因为他卖了我们，吞尽了我们的身价。 ###EN### Are we not regarded by him as foreigners? For he has sold us and has even entirely used up the money given for us.
Verse_Ch: 31:16 神从我们父亲所夺出来的一切财富，那就是我们和我们孩子们的。现今凡神所吩咐你的，你只管去行罢。 ###EN### Surely all the wealth which God has taken away from our father is ours and our children's. So do now whatever God has said to you.
Verse_Ch: 31:17 于是雅各起来，使他的儿子和妻子都骑上骆驼， ###EN### Then Jacob rose up and set his sons and his wives upon the camels;
Verse_Ch: 31:18 又带着他在巴旦亚兰所得的一切牲畜和财物，往迦南地他父亲以撒那里去了。 ###EN### And he drove away all his livestock and all his property which he had acquired, the livestock in his possession which he had acquired in Paddan-aram, in order
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: to go to Isaac his father in the land of Canaan.
Verse_Ch: 31:19 当时拉班剪羊毛去了，拉结偷了他父亲的神像。 ###EN### Now Laban had gone to shear his sheep, and Rachel stole the household idols that were her father's.
Verse_Ch: 31:20 雅各瞒着亚兰人拉班逃走了，并不告诉他， ###EN### And Jacob deceived Laban the Aramaean by not telling him that he was fleeing.
Verse_Ch: 31:21 就带着所有的逃跑。他起身过了大河，面向基列山地行去。 ###EN### So he fled with all that he had, and he rose up and crossed over the River and set his face toward the hill country of Gilead.
Verse_Ch: 31:22 到第三日，有人告诉拉班，雅各逃跑了。 ###EN### And it was told Laban on the third day that Jacob had fled.
Verse_Ch: 31:23 拉班带领他的众弟兄去追赶，追了七日，就在基列山地追上了。 ###EN### And he took his brothers with him and pursued after him the distance of a seven days' journey; and he overtook him in the hill country of Gilead.
Verse_Ch: 31:24 夜间，神到亚兰人拉班那里，在梦中对他说，你要小心，不可与雅各说好说歹。 ###EN### And God came to Laban the Aramaean in a dream of the night and said to him, Be careful that you do not speak to Jacob either good or bad.
Verse_Ch: 31:25 拉班追上雅各。雅各在山地支搭帐棚；拉班和他的众弟兄也在基列山地支搭帐棚。 ###EN### And Laban caught up with Jacob. Now Jacob had pitched his tent in the hill country, and Laban with his brothers also pitched tents in the hill country of Gilead.
Verse_Ch: 31:26 拉班对雅各说，你作的是什么事呢？你瞒着我逃走了，又把我的女儿们带走了，如同用刀剑掳去的一般。 ###EN### And Laban said to Jacob, What are you doing deceiving me and carrying away my daughters like captives of the sword?
Verse_Ch: 31:27 你为什么暗暗的逃跑，偷着走，并不告诉我，叫我可以欢乐、唱歌、击鼓、弹琴来给你送行？ ###EN### Why did you flee secretly and steal away from me and not tell me, when I might have sent you away with joy and with songs, with tambourine and with lyre?
Verse_Ch: 31:28 又不让我与外孙和女儿亲嘴？你所行的真是愚昧。 ###EN### And you did not allow me to kiss my sons and my daughters. Now you have acted foolishly.
Verse_Ch: 31:29 我原有能力害你，只是你父亲的神昨夜对我说，你要小心，不可与雅各说好说歹。 ###EN### It is in my power to do you harm, but the God of your father spoke to me last night, saying, Be careful that you do not speak to Jacob either good or bad.
Verse_Ch: 31:30 现在你虽然很想你父家，不得不去，为什么又偷了我的神像呢？ ###EN### And now, though you had to go because you longed greatly for your father's house, why did you steal my gods?
Verse_Ch: 31:31 雅各回答拉班说，因为我害怕，以为你会把你的女儿从我手里夺去。 ###EN### And Jacob answered and said to Laban, Because I was afraid, for I thought that you might take your daughters from me by force.
Verse_Ch: 31:32 至于你的神像，你在谁那里搜出来，谁就不得存活。当着我们的众弟兄，你认一认，在我这里有什么东西是你的，就拿去。原来雅各不知道拉结偷了那些神像。 ###EN### The one with whom you find your gods shall not live. In the presence of our brothers indicate what there is with me that is yours, and take it. Now Jacob did not
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: know that Rachel had stolen them.
Verse_Ch: 31:33 拉班进了雅各、利亚、并两个使女的帐棚，都没有搜出来，就从利亚的帐棚出来，进了拉结的帐棚。 ###EN### And Laban went into Jacob's tent and into Leah's tent and into the two female servants' tent, but he did not find them. Then he went from Leah's tent and entered
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: Rachel's tent.
Verse_Ch: 31:34 拉结已经把神像藏在骆驼的驮篓里，并且坐在上头。拉班摸遍了那帐棚，并没有摸着。 ###EN### Now Rachel had taken the household idols and put them in the camel's saddle, and she sat upon them. And Laban rummaged through all the tent but did not
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: find them.
Verse_Ch: 31:35 拉结对她父亲说，现在我身上不便，不能在你面前起来，求我主不要动怒。这样，拉班搜寻神像，竟没有搜出来。 ###EN### And she said to her father, Let not my lord be angry that I cannot rise up before you, for the manner of women is upon me. So he searched but did not find the
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: household idols.
Verse_Ch: 31:36 雅各就发怒，与拉班争论，说，我有什么过犯，有什么罪，你竟这样火速的追我？ ###EN### And Jacob became angry and contended with Laban; and Jacob answered and said to Laban, What is my transgression? What is my sin, that you have so hotly
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: pursued me?
Verse_Ch: 31:37 你摸遍了我一切的物件，搜出什么是你家的东西呢？可以放在你我的弟兄们面前，叫他们在我们二人中间判断判断。 ###EN### Although you have rummaged through all my possessions, what have you found of all your household goods? Set it here before my brothers and your brothers,
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: that they may decide between the two of us.
Verse_Ch: 31:38 我同你在一起这二十年，你的母绵羊、母山羊没有掉过胎；你群中的公羊，我没有吃过； ###EN### These twenty years have I been with you; your ewes and your female goats have not miscarried, and I have not eaten the rams of your flocks.
Verse_Ch: 31:39 被野兽撕裂的，我没有带来给你，是我自己赔上。无论是白日，是黑夜，被偷去的，你都向我索要。 ###EN### That which was torn by beasts I did not bring to you; I bore the loss of it myself. Of my hand you required it, whether stolen by day or stolen by night.
Verse_Ch: 31:40 我白日受干热销磨，黑夜受寒霜侵蚀，不得合眼睡着，我常是这样。 ###EN### Thus I was: By day the dry heat consumed me, and the frost by night, and my sleep fled from my eyes.
Verse_Ch: 31:41 我这二十年在你家里，为你的两个女儿服事你十四年，为你的羊群服事你六年，你十次改了我的工价。 ###EN### These twenty years have I been in your house; I served you fourteen years for your two daughters and six years for your flock, and you have changed my wages
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: ten times.
Verse_Ch: 31:42 若不是我父亲的神，就是亚伯拉罕的神，以撒所敬畏的神与我同在，你如今必定打发我空手而去。神看见我的苦情和我的劳碌，就在昨夜责备你。 ###EN### If the God of my father, the God of Abraham, and the Dread of Isaac, had not been with me, surely now you would have sent me away empty. God has seen my
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: affliction and the labor of my hands and rebuked you last night.
Verse_Ch: 31:43 拉班回答雅各说，女儿是我的女儿，孩子是我的孩子，羊群也是我的羊群；凡在你眼前的都是我的。我的女儿并她们所生的孩子，我今日能向他们作什么呢？ ###EN### And Laban answered and said to Jacob, The daughters are my daughters, and the children are my children, and the flocks are my flocks, and all that you see is
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: mine. But what can I do this day to these my daughters or to their children whom they have borne?
Verse_Ch: 31:44 来罢，你我二人可以立约，作你我中间的证据。 ###EN### So come now; let us make a covenant, I and you; and let it be a witness between me and you.
Verse_Ch: 31:45 雅各就拿一块石头，立作柱子， ###EN### So Jacob took a stone and set it up as a pillar.
Verse_Ch: 31:46 又对众弟兄说，你们捡聚石头。他们就拿石头来堆成一堆，大家便在旁边吃喝。 ###EN### And Jacob said to his brothers, Gather stones. So they took stones and made a heap, and they ate there by the heap.
Verse_Ch: 31:47 拉班称那石堆为伊迦尔撒哈杜他，雅各却称那石堆为迦累得。 ###EN### And Laban called it Jegar-sahadutha, but Jacob called it Galeed.
Verse_Ch: 31:48 拉班说，今日这石堆作你我中间的证据。因此那地方名叫迦累得， ###EN### And Laban said, This heap is witness between me and you today. Therefore its name was called Galeed
Verse_Ch: 31:49 又叫米斯巴，因为他说，我们彼此离别以后，愿耶和华在你我中间鉴察。 ###EN### And Mizpah, because he said, Jehovah watch between me and you when we are absent from one another.
Verse_Ch: 31:50 你若苦待我的女儿，又在我的女儿以外另娶妻子，虽然没有人同我们在一起，却有神在你我中间作见证。 ###EN### If you afflict my daughters, and if you take wives besides my daughters-even though no man is with us-see, God is witness between me and you.
Verse_Ch: 31:51 拉班又对雅各说，你看这石堆，和我在你我中间所立的柱子。 ###EN### And Laban said to Jacob, Here is this heap, and here is the pillar which I have set between me and you.
Verse_Ch: 31:52 这石堆作证据，这柱子也作证据；我必不过这石堆去害你，你也不可过这石堆和柱子来害我。 ###EN### This heap is a witness, and the pillar is a witness, that I will not pass beyond this heap to you and that you will not pass beyond this heap and this pillar to me, for
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: harm.
Verse_Ch: 31:53 但愿亚伯拉罕的神和拿鹤的神，就是他们父亲的神，在你我中间判断。雅各就指着他父亲以撒所敬畏的神起誓， ###EN### The God of Abraham and the God of Nahor, the God of their father, judge between us. And Jacob swore by the Dread of his father Isaac.
Verse_Ch: 31:54 又在山上献祭，请众弟兄来吃饭。他们吃了饭，便在山上过夜。 ###EN### And Jacob offered a sacrifice on the mountain and called his brothers to eat a meal, and they ate a meal and spent the night in the mountain.
Verse_Ch: 31:55 拉班清早起来，与他外孙和女儿亲嘴，给他们祝福，就离开那里，回自己的地方去了。 ###EN### And early in the morning Laban rose up and kissed his sons and his daughters and blessed them, and Laban departed and returned to his place.
Chapter_Header: 32
Verse_Ch: 32:1 雅各仍旧行路，神的众使者遇见他。 ###EN### And Jacob went on his way, and the angels of God met him.
Verse_Ch: 32:2 雅各看见他们就说，这是神的军营，于是给那地方起名叫玛哈念。 ###EN### And Jacob said when he saw them, This is God's camp. So he called the name of that place Mahanaim.
Verse_Ch: 32:3 雅各打发报信的人先往西珥地，以东乡间，见他哥哥以扫； ###EN### And Jacob sent messengers before him to Esau his brother, into the land of Seir, the field of Edom.
Verse_Ch: 32:4 他吩咐他们说，你们要对我主以扫这样说：你的仆人雅各这样说，我在拉班那里寄居，直留到如今。 ###EN### And he commanded them, saying, Thus you shall say to my lord Esau: Thus says your servant Jacob, I have sojourned with Laban and stayed until now;
Verse_Ch: 32:5 我有牛、驴、羊群、仆人、婢女，现在打发人来报告我主，为要在你眼前蒙恩。 ###EN### And I have oxen and donkeys and flocks, and male servants and female servants; and I have sent to tell my lord this, that I may find favor in your sight.
Verse_Ch: 32:6 报信的人回到雅各那里，说，我们到了你哥哥以扫那里，他正迎着你来，同他一起的有四百人。 ###EN### And the messengers returned to Jacob, saying, We came to your brother Esau, and he also is coming to meet you; and four hundred men are with him.
Verse_Ch: 32:7 雅各就甚惧怕，而且愁烦，便把那与他同在的人口和羊群、牛群、骆驼分作两队， ###EN### Then Jacob was greatly afraid and distressed; and he divided the people who were with him and the flocks and the herds and the camels into two camps;
Verse_Ch: 32:8 说，以扫若来击杀这一队，剩下的那一队还可以逃避。 ###EN### And he said, If Esau comes to the one camp and attacks it, then the camp which is left will escape.
Verse_Ch: 32:9 雅各说，耶和华我祖亚伯拉罕的神，我父亲以撒的神阿，你曾对我说，回你本地，到你亲族那里去，我要善待你。 ###EN### Then Jacob said, O God of my father Abraham and God of my father Isaac, O Jehovah, who said to me, Return to your country and to your relatives, and I will do
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: you good,
Verse_Ch: 32:10 你向仆人所施的一切慈爱和信实，我一点也不配得；我先前只拿着我的杖过这约但河，如今我却成了两队。 ###EN### I am not worthy of all the lovingkindnesses and of all the faithfulness which You have shown to Your servant, for with my staff only I crossed over this Jordan, and
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: now I have become two camps.
Verse_Ch: 32:11 求你救我脱离我哥哥以扫的手；因为我怕他来击杀我，连妻子带儿女一同击杀了。 ###EN### Deliver me, please, from the hand of my brother, from the hand of Esau, for I fear him, lest he come and attack me, even the mother with the children.
Verse_Ch: 32:12 你曾说，我必定善待你，使你的后裔如同海沙，多得不可胜数。 ###EN### But You have said, I will surely do you good and make your seed like the sand of the sea, which cannot be numbered for multitude.
Verse_Ch: 32:13 当夜，雅各在那里住宿，就从他所有的物中拿礼物要送给他哥哥以扫： ###EN### And he spent that night there. Then from what he had with him he took a present for Esau his brother:
Verse_Ch: 32:14 母山羊二百只，公山羊二十只，母绵羊二百只，公绵羊二十只， ###EN### Two hundred female goats and twenty male goats, two hundred ewes and twenty rams,
Verse_Ch: 32:15 奶崽子的骆驼三十只，各带着崽子，母牛四十只，公牛十只，母驴二十匹，公驴十匹； ###EN### Thirty nursing camels and their young, forty cows and ten bulls, twenty female donkeys and ten male donkeys.
Verse_Ch: 32:16 每样各分一群，交在仆人手下，就对仆人说，你们要在我前头过去，使一群一群之间有个距离； ###EN### And he delivered them into the hand of his servants, every drove by itself, and said to his servants, Cross over before me, and put a space between each drove.
Verse_Ch: 32:17 又吩咐尽先走的说，我哥哥以扫遇见你的时候，问你说，你是那家的人？要往那里去？你前头这些牲畜是谁的？ ###EN### And he commanded the foremost, saying, When Esau my brother meets you and asks you, saying, To whom do you belong? And where are you going? And
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: whose animals are these before you?
Verse_Ch: 32:18 你就说，是你仆人雅各的，是送给我主以扫的礼物；他自己也在我们后边。 ###EN### Then you will say, Your servant Jacob's; it is a present sent to my lord Esau; and now he also is behind us.
Verse_Ch: 32:19 又吩咐第二、第三、和一切赶群畜的人说，你们遇见以扫的时候，也要这样对他说； ###EN### And he commanded also the second and the third, and all who followed the droves, saying, In this way you shall speak to Esau when you find him,
Verse_Ch: 32:20 并且你们要说，你仆人雅各就在我们后边。因为雅各心里说，我借着在我前头去的礼物解他的恨，然后再见他的面，或者他会接纳我。 ###EN### And you shall also say, Your servant Jacob is right behind us. For he said, I will appease him with the present that goes before me, and afterward I will see his
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: face; perhaps he will accept me.
Verse_Ch: 32:21 于是礼物在他前头过去了；那夜，他在队中住宿。 ###EN### So the present crossed over before him, and he himself spent that night in the camp.
Verse_Ch: 32:22 他夜间起来，带着两个妻子，两个使女，并十一个儿子，过雅博渡口。 ###EN### And he rose up that night and took his two wives and his two female servants and his eleven children and crossed over the ford of the Jabbok.
Verse_Ch: 32:23 他带着他们，打发他们过河，又打发所有的都过去。 ###EN### And he took them and sent them over the stream and sent over what he had.
Verse_Ch: 32:24 只剩下雅各一人，有一个人和他摔跤，直到黎明。 ###EN### And Jacob was left alone, and a man wrestled with him until the break of dawn.
Verse_Ch: 32:25 那人见自己胜不过他，就将他的大腿窝摸了一把；雅各正与那人摔跤的时候，他的大腿窝就脱了节。 ###EN### And when the man saw that He did not prevail against him, He touched the socket of his hip; and the socket of Jacob's hip was dislocated as he wrestled with
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: Him.
Verse_Ch: 32:26 那人说，天快亮了，让我去罢。雅各却说，你若不给我祝福，我就不让你去。 ###EN### And the man said, Let Me go, for the dawn is breaking. But Jacob said, I will not let You go unless You bless me.
Verse_Ch: 32:27 那人对他说，你名叫什么？他说，我名叫雅各。 ###EN### And He said to him, What is your name? And he said, Jacob.
Verse_Ch: 32:28 那人说，你的名不要再叫雅各，要叫以色列；因为你与神与人较力，都得了胜。 ###EN### And He said, Your name will no longer be called Jacob, but Israel; for you have struggled with God and with men and have prevailed.
Verse_Ch: 32:29 雅各问祂说，请将你的名告诉我。但那人说，你何必问我的名？于是祂在那里给雅各祝福。 ###EN### And Jacob asked Him and said, Please tell me Your name. But He said, Why is it that you ask My name? And He blessed him there.
Verse_Ch: 32:30 雅各便给那地方起名叫毗努伊勒，因为他说，我面对面看见了神，我的性命仍得保全。 ###EN### And Jacob called the name of the place Peniel, for, he said, I have seen God face to face, and yet my life has been preserved.
Verse_Ch: 32:31 日头升起，照在雅各身上，那时他渡过毗努伊勒，他的大腿就瘸了。 ###EN### And the sun rose upon him as he crossed over Penuel, and he limped because of his hip.
Verse_Ch: 32:32 故此，以色列人不吃大腿窝的筋，直到今日，因为那人摸了雅各大腿窝的筋。 ###EN### Therefore the children of Israel do not eat the thigh muscle, which is upon the socket of the hip, to this day, because He touched the socket of Jacob's hip at the
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: thigh muscle.
Chapter_Header: 33
Verse_Ch: 33:1 雅各举目观看，见以扫来了，同他一起的有四百人。他就把孩子们分开交给利亚、拉结、和两个使女， ###EN### And Jacob lifted up his eyes and looked, and there was Esau coming, and four hundred men with him. So he divided the children among Leah and among
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: Rachel and among the two female servants.
Verse_Ch: 33:2 并且叫两个使女和她们的孩子在前面，利亚和她的孩子在后面，拉结和约瑟在最后面。 ###EN### And he put the female servants and their children in front, and Leah and her children next, and Rachel and Joseph last.
Verse_Ch: 33:3 他自己在他们前头过去，一连七次俯伏在地，直到就近他哥哥。 ###EN### And he himself passed on before them and bowed down to the ground seven times until he came near to his brother.
Verse_Ch: 33:4 以扫跑来迎接他，将他抱住，又伏在他的颈项上，与他亲嘴，两个人就哭了。 ###EN### And Esau ran to meet him and embraced him and fell on his neck and kissed him, and they wept.
Verse_Ch: 33:5 以扫举目看见妇人孩子，就说，这些和你同行的是谁？雅各说，这些孩子是神施恩给你仆人的。 ###EN### And he lifted up his eyes and saw the women and the children and said, Who are these with you? And he said, The children whom God has graciously given your
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: servant.
Verse_Ch: 33:6 于是两个使女和她们的孩子前来下拜； ###EN### Then the female servants came near, they and their children, and they bowed down.
Verse_Ch: 33:7 利亚和她的孩子也前来下拜；随后约瑟和拉结也前来下拜。 ###EN### And Leah also came near with her children, and they bowed down; and afterward Joseph came near with Rachel, and they bowed down.
