Verse_Ch: 33:8 以扫说，我所遇见的这一整队是什么意思？雅各说，是要在我主眼前蒙恩的。 ###EN### And Esau said, What do you mean by all this camp which I met? And he said, To find favor in the sight of my lord.
Verse_Ch: 33:9 以扫说，弟弟阿，我的已经够了，你的仍归你罢。 ###EN### And Esau said, I have enough, my brother; let what you have be yours.
Verse_Ch: 33:10 雅各说，不然，我若在你眼前蒙恩，就求你从我手里收下这礼物；因为我看见你的面，如同看见神的面，并且你悦纳了我。 ###EN### And Jacob said, No, please, if now I have found favor in your sight, then take my present from my hand; for I see your face as one sees the face of God, and you
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: have received me favorably.
Verse_Ch: 33:11 求你收下我带来给你的礼物；因为神恩待了我，并且我一切都有了。雅各再三的求他，他才收下了。 ###EN### Please take my blessing which has been brought to you, because God has dealt graciously with me, and because I have all that I need. So he urged him, and he
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: took it.
Verse_Ch: 33:12 以扫说，我们可以起身前去，我要在你前头走。 ###EN### Then Esau said, Let us take our journey and go, and I will go before you.
Verse_Ch: 33:13 雅各对他说，我主知道孩子们年幼娇嫩，正在乳养的牛羊也是我所挂心的，若是催赶一天，群畜都必死了。 ###EN### And he said to him, My lord knows that the children are frail and that the nursing flocks and herds are a concern to me; and if they overdrive them for one day, all
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: the flock will die.
Verse_Ch: 33:14 求我主在仆人前头走，我要按着在我前面群畜和孩子们的步速慢慢前行，直走到西珥我主那里。 ###EN### Let my lord please pass on before his servant, and I will lead on slowly according to the pace of the cattle which are before me and according to the pace of the
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: children until I come to my lord at Seir.
Verse_Ch: 33:15 以扫说，让我把跟随我的人留几个在你这里。雅各说，何必呢？只要在我主眼前蒙恩就是了。 ###EN### So Esau said, Let me please leave with you some of the people who are with me. And he said, What need is there? Let me find favor in the sight of my lord.
Verse_Ch: 33:16 于是，以扫当日起行，回西珥去了。 ###EN### So Esau returned that day on his way to Seir.
Verse_Ch: 33:17 雅各就往疏割去，在那里为自己盖造一座房屋，又为牲畜搭棚；因此那地方名叫疏割。 ###EN### And Jacob journeyed to Succoth and built a house for himself and made booths for his livestock; therefore the name of the place is called Succoth.
Verse_Ch: 33:18 雅各从巴旦亚兰回来的时候，平平安安的到了迦南地的示剑城，在城对面支搭帐棚， ###EN### And Jacob came safely to the city of Shechem, which is in the land of Canaan, when he came from Paddan-aram; and he camped before the city.
Verse_Ch: 33:19 就用一百块银子向示剑的父亲哈抹的子孙，买了支帐棚的那块地， ###EN### And he bought the piece of land where he had pitched his tent from the hand of the children of Hamor, Shechem's father, for a hundred qesitahs.
Verse_Ch: 33:20 在那里筑了一座坛，起名叫伊利伊罗伊以色列。 ###EN### And there he erected an altar and called it El-Elohe-Israel.
Chapter_Header: 34
Verse_Ch: 34:1 利亚给雅各所生的女儿底拿出去，要见那地的女子们。 ###EN### And Dinah the daughter of Leah, whom she had borne to Jacob, went out to see the daughters of the land.
Verse_Ch: 34:2 那地的族长希未人哈抹的儿子示剑看见她，就拉住她，与她同寝，玷辱了她。 ###EN### And when Shechem the son of Hamor the Hivite, the prince of the land, saw her, he took her and lay with her and humbled her.
Verse_Ch: 34:3 示剑的心系恋雅各的女儿底拿，爱这少女，甜言蜜语的安慰她。 ###EN### And his soul clung to Dinah the daughter of Jacob, and he loved the girl and spoke affectionately to the girl.
Verse_Ch: 34:4 示剑对他父亲哈抹说，求你为我聘这女孩子为妻。 ###EN### And Shechem spoke to his father Hamor, saying, Get me this young girl as a wife.
Verse_Ch: 34:5 雅各听见示剑玷污了他的女儿底拿；那时他的儿子们正和群畜在田野，雅各就不作声，等他们回来。 ###EN### Now when Jacob heard that he had defiled Dinah his daughter, his sons were with his livestock in the field; so Jacob kept silent until they came in.
Verse_Ch: 34:6 示剑的父亲哈抹出来见雅各，要和他商议。 ###EN### And Hamor the father of Shechem went out to Jacob to speak with him.
Verse_Ch: 34:7 雅各的儿子们听见这事，就从田野回来，人人悲愤，极其恼怒；因为示剑在以色列家作了愚妄的事，与雅各的女儿同寝，这本是不该作的事。 ###EN### And the sons of Jacob came in from the field when they heard of it. And the men were grieved and became very angry, because he had committed folly in Israel
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: by lying with Jacob's daughter, for such a thing ought not to be done.
Verse_Ch: 34:8 哈抹和他们商议说，我儿子示剑的心恋慕你们的女儿，求你们将她给我的儿子为妻。 ###EN### And Hamor spoke with them, saying, The soul of my son Shechem longs for your daughter; please give her to him as a wife.
Verse_Ch: 34:9 你们与我们彼此结亲，你们可以把女儿嫁给我们，也可以娶我们的女儿。 ###EN### And make marriages with us: Give your daughters to us, and take our daughters for yourselves.
Verse_Ch: 34:10 你们与我们同住罢。这地都在你们面前，只管住下来，在这里作买卖，置产业。 ###EN### And you shall dwell with us, and the land will be before you; dwell and trade in it, and acquire holdings in it.
Verse_Ch: 34:11 示剑对少女的父亲和弟兄们说，但愿我在你们眼前蒙恩，你们向我要什么，我必给你们。 ###EN### And Shechem said to her father and to her brothers, Let me find favor in your sight, and whatever you say to me I will give.
Verse_Ch: 34:12 任凭向我要多重的聘金和礼物，我必照你们向我所说的给你们；只要把少女给我为妻。 ###EN### Impose upon me a very large bridal price and gift, and I will give whatever you say to me; but give me the girl as a wife.
Verse_Ch: 34:13 雅各的儿子们因为示剑玷污了他们的姊妹底拿，就用诡诈的话回答示剑和他父亲哈抹， ###EN### Then the sons of Jacob answered Shechem and Hamor his father deceitfully; and because he had defiled Dinah their sister they spoke,
Verse_Ch: 34:14 对他们说，我们不能作这事，把我们的姊妹给没有受割礼的人为妻，因为那是我们的羞辱。 ###EN### And said to them, We are not able to do this thing, to give our sister to one who is uncircumcised, for that would be a reproach to us.
Verse_Ch: 34:15 惟有一件事你们必须作，我们才可以应允：若你们所有的男丁都受割礼，和我们一样， ###EN### Only on this condition will we consent to you: If you become like us, and every male among you is circumcised,
Verse_Ch: 34:16 我们就把女儿嫁给你们，也娶你们的女儿；我们便与你们同住，成为一样的人民。 ###EN### Then we will give our daughters to you, and will take your daughters for ourselves; and we will dwell with you and become one people.
Verse_Ch: 34:17 倘若你们不听我们，不受割礼，我们就带着我们的姊妹走了。 ###EN### But if you will not listen to us and be circumcised, then we will take our daughter and go.
Verse_Ch: 34:18 哈抹和他的儿子示剑认为这话甚好。 ###EN### And their words seemed good to Hamor and Shechem, Hamor's son.
Verse_Ch: 34:19 那少年人作这事并不迟延，因为他喜爱雅各的女儿；他在他父亲家中也是人最尊重的。 ###EN### And the young man did not delay to do the thing, because he delighted in Jacob's daughter. Now he was honored above all the house of his father.
Verse_Ch: 34:20 哈抹和他儿子示剑到本城的门口，对本城的人说， ###EN### And Hamor and Shechem his son came to the gate of their city and spoke with the men of their city, saying,
Verse_Ch: 34:21 这些人与我们和睦相处，不如让他们在这地居住，作买卖；这地也宽阔，足可容纳他们。我们可以娶他们的女儿为妻，也可以把我们的女儿嫁给他们。 ###EN### These men are with us peacefully; therefore let them dwell in the land and trade in it, for here the land is large enough for them. Let us take their daughters for
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: ourselves as wives, and let us give them our daughters.
Verse_Ch: 34:22 惟有一件事我们必须作，他们才应允和我们同住，成为一样的人民，就是我们中间所有的男丁都受割礼，和他们一样。 ###EN### Only on this condition will the men consent to us to dwell with us, to become one people: that every male among us be circumcised as they are circumcised.
Verse_Ch: 34:23 他们的群畜、财物、和一切的牲口岂不都归我们么？只要依从他们，他们就与我们同住。 ###EN### Will not their livestock and their property and all their animals be ours? Only let us consent to them, and they will dwell with us.
Verse_Ch: 34:24 凡从城门出入的人，就都听从哈抹和他儿子示剑的话；于是凡从城门出入的男丁都受了割礼。 ###EN### And all who went out of the gate of his city listened to Hamor and to Shechem his son; and every male was circumcised, all who went out of the gate of his city.
Verse_Ch: 34:25 到第三天，众人正在疼痛的时候，雅各的两个儿子，就是底拿的哥哥西缅和利未，各拿刀剑，趁着众人想不到的时候，来到城中，把一切男丁都杀了， ###EN### Then on the third day, when they were still in pain, two of Jacob's sons, Simeon and Levi, Dinah's brothers, each took his sword and came upon the city unawares,
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: and slew every male.
Verse_Ch: 34:26 又用刀杀了哈抹和他儿子示剑，把底拿从示剑家里带出来走了。 ###EN### And they slew Hamor and Shechem his son with the edge of the sword, and they took Dinah out of Shechem's house and went away.
Verse_Ch: 34:27 雅各的儿子们因为他们的姊妹受了玷污，就来到被杀的人那里，掳掠那城， ###EN### The sons of Jacob came upon the slain and plundered the city, because they had defiled their sister.
Verse_Ch: 34:28 夺了他们的羊群、牛群和驴，并城里田间所有的； ###EN### They took their flocks and their herds and their donkeys and whatever was in the city and whatever was in the field;
Verse_Ch: 34:29 又把他们的一切财产、小孩、妇女，并房屋中所有的，都掳掠去了。 ###EN### And they took captive and plundered all their wealth and all their little ones and their wives, and even all that was in the houses.
Verse_Ch: 34:30 雅各对西缅和利未说，你们连累我，使我在这地的居民中，就是在迦南人和比利洗人中，有了臭名。我的人丁既然稀少，他们必聚集来攻击我，我和全家的人都必灭绝。 ###EN### And Jacob said to Simeon and Levi, You have brought trouble upon me by making me odious among the inhabitants of the land, among the Canaanites and the
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: Perizzites; and I am few in number, and they will gather themselves together against me and strike me; and I will be destroyed, I and my house.
Verse_Ch: 34:31 他们说，他岂可待我们的姊妹如同妓女么？ ###EN### And they said, Should he treat our sister like a harlot?
Chapter_Header: 35
Verse_Ch: 35:1 神对雅各说，起来，上伯特利去，住在那里；要在那里筑一座坛给神，就是你逃避你哥哥以扫的时候向你显现的那位。 ###EN### And God said to Jacob, Rise up, go up to Bethel, and dwell there; and make an altar there to the God who appeared to you when you fled from your brother Esau.
Verse_Ch: 35:2 雅各就对他家中的人，并一切与他同在的人说，你们要除掉你们中间的外邦神像，也要自洁，更换衣裳。 ###EN### Then Jacob said to his household and to all who were with him, Put away the foreign gods that are among you, and purify yourselves, and change your
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: garments.
Verse_Ch: 35:3 我们要起来，上伯特利去，在那里我要筑一座坛给神，就是在我遭难的日子应允我的祷告，在我所行的路上与我同在的那位。 ###EN### And let us rise up and go up to Bethel, that I may make an altar there to the God who answered me in the day of my distress and has been with me wherever I
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: have gone.
Verse_Ch: 35:4 他们就把手中的一切外邦神像和耳朵上的环子，交给雅各；雅各把这些都藏在示剑附近的橡树底下。 ###EN### So they gave Jacob all the foreign gods which were in their hand and the rings which were in their ears, and Jacob hid them under the oak that was near
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: Shechem.
Verse_Ch: 35:5 当他们起行往前时，神使周围城邑的人都惊惧，就不追赶雅各的众子。 ###EN### And as they journeyed, the terror of God was upon the cities that were around them, so they did not pursue the sons of Jacob.
Verse_Ch: 35:6 于是雅各和一切与他同在的人，到了迦南地的路斯，就是伯特利。 ###EN### And Jacob came to Luz (that is, Bethel), which is in the land of Canaan, he and all the people who were with him.
Verse_Ch: 35:7 他在那里筑了一座坛，并且称那地方为伊勒伯特利，因为当他逃避他哥哥的时候，神在那里向他启示祂自己。 ###EN### And he built an altar there and called the place El-bethel, because there God had revealed Himself to him when he fled from his brother.
Verse_Ch: 35:8 利百加的乳母底波拉死了，就葬在伯特利下边的橡树底下；那棵树名叫亚伦巴古。 ###EN### And Deborah, Rebekah's nurse, died, and she was buried below Bethel under the oak; so its name was called Allon-bacuth.
Verse_Ch: 35:9 雅各从巴旦亚兰回来，神又向他显现，赐福与他， ###EN### And God appeared to Jacob again when he came from Paddan-aram and blessed him.
Verse_Ch: 35:10 并且对他说，你的名原是雅各，从今以后不要再叫雅各，要叫以色列。这样，神就给他起名叫以色列。 ###EN### And God said to him, Your name is Jacob; Your name shall no longer be called Jacob, But Israel shall be your name. Thus He called his name Israel.
Verse_Ch: 35:11 神又对他说，我是全足的神；你要繁衍增多，将来有一国，有多民从你而生，又有君王从你腰中而出。 ###EN### And God said to him, I am the All-sufficient God: Be fruitful and multiply; A nation and a company of nations shall come from you, And kings shall come forth
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: from your loins.
Verse_Ch: 35:12 我所赐给亚伯拉罕和以撒的地，我要赐给你；我也要把这地赐给你的后裔。 ###EN### And the land which I gave to Abraham and to Isaac, I will give to you; And I will give the land to your seed after you.
Verse_Ch: 35:13 神就从祂与雅各说话的地方，离开他升上去了。 ###EN### Then God went up from him in the place where He had spoken with him.
Verse_Ch: 35:14 雅各便在神与他说话的地方立了一根石柱，在柱上浇了奠祭，并且浇上油。 ###EN### And Jacob set up a pillar in the place where He had spoken with him, a pillar of stone; and he poured out a drink offering on it and poured oil on it.
Verse_Ch: 35:15 雅各就给神与他说话的地方起名叫伯特利。 ###EN### And Jacob called the name of the place where God had spoken with him Bethel.
Verse_Ch: 35:16 他们从伯特利起行，离以法他还有一段路程，拉结临产甚是艰难。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Bethel. And while there was still some distance to come to Ephrath, Rachel began to give birth; and she had hard labor.
Verse_Ch: 35:17 正在艰难的时候，收生婆对她说，不要怕，你又要得一个儿子了。 ###EN### And while she was in hardest labor, the midwife said to her, Do not be afraid, for now you have another son.
Verse_Ch: 35:18 她将近于死，魂要离开的时候，就给她儿子起名叫便俄尼；他父亲却给他起名叫便雅悯。 ###EN### And as her soul was departing (for she died), she called his name Ben-oni; but his father called him Benjamin.
Verse_Ch: 35:19 拉结死了，葬在通往以法他的路旁；以法他就是伯利恒。 ###EN### So Rachel died and was buried on the way to Ephrath (that is, Bethlehem).
Verse_Ch: 35:20 雅各在她的坟上立了一个碑，就是拉结的墓碑，到今日还在。 ###EN### And Jacob set up a pillar on her grave; that is the pillar of Rachel's grave, which is there to this day.
Verse_Ch: 35:21 以色列起行前往，在以得台的那一边支搭帐棚。 ###EN### And Israel journeyed and pitched his tent beyond the tower of Eder.
Verse_Ch: 35:22 以色列住在那地的时候，流便去与他父亲的妾辟拉同寝，以色列也听见了。雅各共有十二个儿子。 ###EN### And while Israel dwelt in that land, Reuben went and lay with Bilhah his father's concubine, and Israel heard of it. Now the sons of Jacob were twelve:
Verse_Ch: 35:23 利亚所生的是雅各的长子流便，还有西缅、利未、犹大、以萨迦、西布伦。 ###EN### The sons of Leah: Reuben, Jacob's firstborn, and Simeon and Levi and Judah and Issachar and Zebulun.
Verse_Ch: 35:24 拉结所生的是约瑟、便雅悯。 ###EN### The sons of Rachel: Joseph and Benjamin.
Verse_Ch: 35:25 拉结的使女辟拉所生的是但、拿弗他利。 ###EN### And the sons of Bilhah, Rachel's female servant: Dan and Naphtali.
Verse_Ch: 35:26 利亚的使女悉帕所生的是迦得、亚设。这些是雅各在巴旦亚兰所生的儿子。 ###EN### And the sons of Zilpah, Leah's female servant: Gad and Asher. These are the sons of Jacob, who were born to him in Paddan-aram.
Verse_Ch: 35:27 雅各来到他父亲以撒那里，到了基列亚巴的幔利，乃是亚伯拉罕和以撒寄居的地方；基列亚巴就是希伯仑。 ###EN### And Jacob came to Isaac his father at Mamre, at Kiriath-arba (that is, Hebron), where Abraham and Isaac had sojourned.
Verse_Ch: 35:28 以撒共活了一百八十岁。 ###EN### And the days of Isaac were a hundred and eighty years.
Verse_Ch: 35:29 以撒年纪老迈，日子满足，气绝而死，归到他本民那里；他两个儿子以扫、雅各把他埋葬了。 ###EN### And Isaac expired and died and was gathered to his people, an old man and full of days; and Esau and Jacob his sons buried him.
Chapter_Header: 36
Verse_Ch: 36:1 以扫就是以东，他的后代记在下面： ###EN### Now these are the generations of Esau (that is, Edom).
Verse_Ch: 36:2 以扫娶迦南的女子为妻，就是赫人以伦的女儿亚大，和希未人祭便的孙女，亚拿的女儿阿何利巴玛， ###EN### Esau took his wives from the daughters of Canaan: Adah the daughter of Elon the Hittite; and Oholibamah the daughter of Anah, the daughter of Zibeon the
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: Hivite;
Verse_Ch: 36:3 又娶了以实玛利的女儿，尼拜约的妹妹巴实抹。 ###EN### And Basemath Ishmael's daughter, the sister of Nebaioth.
Verse_Ch: 36:4 亚大给以扫生了以利法；巴实抹生了流珥； ###EN### And Adah bore Eliphaz to Esau, and Basemath bore Reuel,
Verse_Ch: 36:5 阿何利巴玛生了耶乌施、雅兰、可拉。这些都是以扫的儿子，是在迦南地生的。 ###EN### And Oholibamah bore Jeush and Jalam and Korah. These are the sons of Esau, who were born to him in the land of Canaan.
Verse_Ch: 36:6 以扫带着他的妻子、儿女、与家中一切的人口，并他的牛羊、牲畜、和一切财物，就是他在迦南地所得的，往别地去，离开了他的弟弟雅各。 ###EN### And Esau took his wives and his sons and his daughters and all his household and his livestock and all his cattle and all his possessions which he had acquired
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: in the land of Canaan, and he went into a land away from his brother Jacob.
Verse_Ch: 36:7 因为二人的家产甚多，使他们不能同住一起，他们的群畜太多，寄居的地容不下他们。 ###EN### For their property was too great for them to dwell together, and the land where they sojourned could not sustain them because of their livestock.
Verse_Ch: 36:8 于是以扫住在西珥山；以扫就是以东。 ###EN### And Esau dwelt in Mount Seir; Esau is Edom.
Verse_Ch: 36:9 以扫是西珥山以东人的始祖，他的后代记在下面。 ###EN### And these are the generations of Esau the father of the Edomites in Mount Seir:
Verse_Ch: 36:10 以扫众子的名字如下：以扫的妻子亚大生以利法；以扫的妻子巴实抹生流珥。 ###EN### These are the names of Esau's sons: Eliphaz the son of Esau's wife Adah, Reuel the son of Esau's wife Basemath.
Verse_Ch: 36:11 以利法的儿子是提幔、阿抹、洗玻、迦坦、基纳斯。 ###EN### And the sons of Eliphaz were Teman, Omar, Zepho, and Gatam and Kenaz.
Verse_Ch: 36:12 亭纳是以扫儿子以利法的妾；她给以利法生了亚玛力。这些是以扫妻子亚大的子孙。 ###EN### And Timna was a concubine to Eliphaz Esau's son, and she bore Amalek to Eliphaz. These are the sons of Esau's wife Adah.
Verse_Ch: 36:13 流珥的儿子是拿哈、谢拉、沙玛、米撒。这些是以扫妻子巴实抹的子孙。 ###EN### And these are the sons of Reuel: Nahath and Zerah, Shammah and Mizzah. These were the sons of Esau's wife Basemath.
Verse_Ch: 36:14 以扫的妻子阿何利巴玛是祭便的孙女，亚拿的女儿；她给以扫生了耶乌施、雅兰、可拉。 ###EN### And these were the sons of Oholibamah the daughter of Anah, the daughter of Zibeon, Esau's wife: And she bore to Esau Jeush and Jalam and Korah.
Verse_Ch: 36:15 以扫子孙中的各族记在下面：以扫的长子以利法的子孙中，有提幔族、阿抹族、洗玻族、基纳斯族、 ###EN### These are the clans of the sons of Esau. The sons of Eliphaz the firstborn of Esau: Clan Teman, Clan Omar, Clan Zepho, Clan Kenaz,
Verse_Ch: 36:16 可拉族、迦坦族、亚玛力族。这些是在以东地从以利法所出的各族，都是亚大的子孙。 ###EN### Clan Korah, Clan Gatam, Clan Amalek; these are the clans of Eliphaz in the land of Edom. These are the sons of Adah.
Verse_Ch: 36:17 以扫的儿子流珥的子孙中，有拿哈族、谢拉族、沙玛族、米撒族。这些是在以东地从流珥所出的各族，都是以扫妻子巴实抹的子孙。 ###EN### And these are the sons of Reuel, Esau's son: Clan Nahath, Clan Zerah, Clan Shammah, Clan Mizzah; these are the clans of Reuel in the land of Edom. These are
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: the sons of Basemath, Esau's wife.
Verse_Ch: 36:18 以扫妻子阿何利巴玛的子孙中，有耶乌施族、雅兰族、可拉族。这些是从以扫的妻子，亚拿的女儿，阿何利巴玛所出的各族。 ###EN### And these are the sons of Oholibamah, Esau's wife: Clan Jeush, Clan Jalam, Clan Korah. These are the clans of Oholibamah the daughter of Anah, Esau's wife.
Verse_Ch: 36:19 以上的各族都是以扫的子孙；以扫就是以东。 ###EN### These are the sons of Esau (that is, Edom), and these are their clans.
Verse_Ch: 36:20 那地原有的居民，何利人西珥的子孙记在下面，就是罗坍、朔巴、祭便、亚拿、 ###EN### These are the sons of Seir the Horite, the inhabitants of the land: Lotan and Shobal and Zibeon and Anah
Verse_Ch: 36:21 底顺、以察、底珊。这些是从以东地西珥的子孙，何利人中所出的族长。 ###EN### And Dishon and Ezer and Dishan; these are the clans of the Horites, the children of Seir in the land of Edom.
Verse_Ch: 36:22 罗坍的儿子是何利、希幔；罗坍的妹妹是亭纳。 ###EN### And the sons of Lotan were Hori and Heman; and Lotan's sister was Timna.
Verse_Ch: 36:23 朔巴的儿子是亚勒文、玛拿辖、以巴录、示玻、阿南。 ###EN### And these are the sons of Shobal: Alvan and Manahath and Ebal, Shepho and Onam.
Verse_Ch: 36:24 祭便的儿子是亚雅、亚拿。当时在旷野放他父亲祭便的驴，发现温泉的，就是这亚拿。 ###EN### And these are the sons of Zibeon: Aiah and Anah. This is the Anah who found the hot springs in the wilderness as he fed the donkeys of Zibeon his father.
Verse_Ch: 36:25 亚拿的儿子是底顺；亚拿的女儿是阿何利巴玛。 ###EN### And these are the children of Anah: Dishon and Oholibamah the daughter of Anah.
Verse_Ch: 36:26 底顺的儿子是欣但、伊是班、益兰、基兰。 ###EN### And these are the sons of Dishon: Hemdan and Eshban and Ithran and Cheran.
Verse_Ch: 36:27 以察的儿子是辟罕、撒番、亚干。 ###EN### These are the sons of Ezer: Bilhan and Zaavan and Akan.
Verse_Ch: 36:28 底珊的儿子是乌斯、亚兰。 ###EN### These are the sons of Dishan: Uz and Aran.
Verse_Ch: 36:29 从何利人所出的各族记在下面，就是罗坍族、朔巴族、祭便族、亚拿族、 ###EN### These are the clans of the Horites: Clan Lotan, Clan Shobal, Clan Zibeon, Clan Anah,
Verse_Ch: 36:30 底顺族、以察族、底珊族。这些是从何利人所出的各族，都在西珥地，各按各族。 ###EN### Clan Dishon, Clan Ezer, Clan Dishan. These are the clans of the Horites, according to their clans in the land of Seir.
Verse_Ch: 36:31 以色列人未有君王治理以前，在以东地作王的记在下面。 ###EN### And these are the kings who reigned in the land of Edom before a king of the children of Israel reigned:
Verse_Ch: 36:32 比珥的儿子比拉在以东作王，他的京城名叫亭哈巴。 ###EN### Now Bela the son of Beor reigned in Edom, and the name of his city was Dinhabah.
Verse_Ch: 36:33 比拉死了，波斯拉人谢拉的儿子约巴接续他作王。 ###EN### And Bela died, and Jobab the son of Zerah of Bozrah reigned in his place.
Verse_Ch: 36:34 约巴死了，提幔地的人户珊接续他作王。 ###EN### And Jobab died, and Husham of the land of the Temanites reigned in his place.
Verse_Ch: 36:35 户珊死了，比达的儿子哈达接续他作王；这哈达就是在摩押田野击杀米甸人的，他的京城名叫亚未得。 ###EN### And Husham died; and Hadad the son of Bedad, who struck Midian in the field of Moab, reigned in his place; and the name of his city was Avith.
Verse_Ch: 36:36 哈达死了，玛士利加人桑拉接续他作王。 ###EN### And Hadad died, and Samlah of Masrekah reigned in his place.
Verse_Ch: 36:37 桑拉死了，大河边的利河伯人扫罗接续他作王。 ###EN### And Samlah died, and Shaul of Rehoboth by the River reigned in his place.
Verse_Ch: 36:38 扫罗死了，亚革波的儿子巴勒哈南接续他作王。 ###EN### And Shaul died, and Baal-hanan the son of Achbor reigned in his place.
Verse_Ch: 36:39 亚革波的儿子巴勒哈南死了，哈达接续他作王，他的京城名叫巴乌；他的妻子名叫米希他别，是米萨合的孙女，玛特列的女儿。 ###EN### And Baal-hanan the son of Achbor died, and Hadar reigned in his place. And the name of his city was Pau; and his wife's name was Mehetabel the daughter of
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: Matred, the daughter of Mezahab.
Verse_Ch: 36:40 从以扫所出的各族，按着他们的家族、地方，名字记在下面，就是亭纳族、亚勒瓦族、耶帖族、 ###EN### And these are the names of the clans of Esau, according to their families, according to their places, by their names: Clan Timna, Clan Alvah, Clan Jetheth,
Verse_Ch: 36:41 阿何利巴玛族、以拉族、比嫩族、 ###EN### Clan Oholibamah, Clan Elah, Clan Pinon,
Verse_Ch: 36:42 基纳斯族、提幔族、米比萨族、 ###EN### Clan Kenaz, Clan Teman, Clan Mibzar,
Verse_Ch: 36:43 玛基叠族、以兰族。这些是以东人在所得为业的地上，按着他们住处的各族。以东人的始祖就是以扫。 ###EN### Clan Magdiel, Clan Iram. These are the clans of Edom according to their habitations in the land of their possession. This is Esau the father of the Edomites.
Chapter_Header: 37
Verse_Ch: 37:1 雅各住在迦南地，就是他父亲寄居的地。 ###EN### And Jacob dwelt in the land where his father had sojourned, in the land of Canaan.
Verse_Ch: 37:2 雅各的记略如下。约瑟十七岁时与他哥哥们一同牧羊。他是个少年人，与他父亲的妻辟拉、悉帕的儿子们常在一处。约瑟将他哥哥们的恶行报给他们的父亲。 ###EN### These are the generations of Jacob. Joseph, when he was seventeen years old, was shepherding the flock with his brothers while he was still a youth, with the
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: sons of Bilhah and with the sons of Zilpah, his father's wives. And Joseph brought an evil report of them to their father.
Verse_Ch: 37:3 以色列原来爱约瑟过于爱他的众子，因为约瑟是他年老生的；他给约瑟作了一件彩衣。 ###EN### Now Israel loved Joseph more than all his sons, because he was the son of his old age; and he had made him a coat of many colors.
Verse_Ch: 37:4 约瑟的哥哥们见父亲爱约瑟过于爱他们，就恨约瑟，不与他说和睦的话。 ###EN### And when his brothers saw that their father loved him more than all his brothers, they hated him and could not speak peaceably to him.
Verse_Ch: 37:5 约瑟作了一个梦，把这梦告诉他哥哥们，他们就越发恨他。 ###EN### Then Joseph had a dream; and when he told it to his brothers, they hated him even more.
Verse_Ch: 37:6 约瑟对他们说，请听我所作的这梦： ###EN### And he said to them, Listen to this dream which I have had:
Verse_Ch: 37:7 我们在田里捆禾稼，忽然间我的禾捆起来站着，你们的禾捆来围着我的禾捆下拜。 ###EN### There we were, binding sheaves in the field, when suddenly my sheaf rose up and remained standing; and then your sheaves gathered around and bowed
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: down to my sheaf.
Verse_Ch: 37:8 他的哥哥们对他说，难道你真要作我们的王，真要管辖我们么？他们就因为他的梦和他的话越发恨他。 ###EN### And his brothers said to him, Will you indeed reign over us and actually be a ruler among us? So they hated him even more for his dreams and for his words.
Verse_Ch: 37:9 后来他又作了一个梦，也把这梦告诉他的哥哥们说，看哪，我又作了一个梦，梦见太阳、月亮与十一颗星，向我下拜。 ###EN### And he had still another dream and told it to his brothers and said, Now I have had another dream: There were the sun and the moon and eleven stars, bowing
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: down to me.
Verse_Ch: 37:10 约瑟将这梦告诉他父亲和他哥哥们，他父亲就责备他说，你作的这是什么梦！难道我和你母亲、你弟兄，果然要来俯伏在地，向你下拜么？ ###EN### And he told it to his father and to his brothers; and his father rebuked him and said to him, What is this dream that you have had? Shall I and your mother and
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: your brothers indeed come to bow down to the ground to you?
Verse_Ch: 37:11 他哥哥们都嫉妒他，他父亲却把这话存在心里。 ###EN### And his brothers were jealous of him, but his father kept the saying in his heart.
Verse_Ch: 37:12 约瑟的哥哥们往示剑去放他们父亲的羊。 ###EN### Then his brothers went to shepherd their father's flock in Shechem.
Verse_Ch: 37:13 以色列对约瑟说，你哥哥们不是正在示剑放羊么？你来，我要打发你往他们那里去。约瑟说，我在这里。 ###EN### And Israel said to Joseph, Your brothers are now shepherding the flock in Shechem. Come, and I will send you to them. And he said to him, Here I am.
Verse_Ch: 37:14 以色列说，你去看看你哥哥们平安不平安，群羊平安不平安，就回来报信给我；于是打发他出希伯仑谷，他就往示剑去了。 ###EN### And he said to him, Go now, see if it is well with your brothers and well with the flock, and bring word back to me. So he sent him from the valley of Hebron, and
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: he came to Shechem.
Verse_Ch: 37:15 有人遇见他在田野走迷了路，就问他说，你找什么？ ###EN### And a man found him; and there he was, wandering in the field, and the man asked him, saying, What are you seeking?
Verse_Ch: 37:16 他说，我找我的哥哥们；求你告诉我，他们在那里放羊。 ###EN### And he said, I am seeking my brothers. Please tell me where they are shepherding the flock.
Verse_Ch: 37:17 那人说，他们已经离开这里走了，我听见他们说要往多坍去。约瑟就去追赶他哥哥们，在多坍找到他们。 ###EN### And the man said, They have moved on from here; for I heard them say, Let us go to Dothan. And Joseph went after his brothers and found them in Dothan.
Verse_Ch: 37:18 他们远远的看见他，趁他还没有走到跟前，大家就同谋要害死他， ###EN### And when they saw him from a distance and before he came near to them, they conspired against him to put him to death.
Verse_Ch: 37:19 彼此说，你看，那作梦的来了。 ###EN### And they said one to another, Here comes this master of dreams.
Verse_Ch: 37:20 来罢，我们将他杀了，丢在一个坑里，就说有恶兽把他吃了；我们且看他的梦将来怎么样。 ###EN### Now then, come and let us slay him and throw him into one of the pits; and we will say, A wild beast has devoured him; then we will see what will become of his
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: dreams.
Verse_Ch: 37:21 流便听见了，要救他脱离他们的手，就说，我们不可害他的性命； ###EN### But when Reuben heard it, he tried to deliver him out of their hand and said, Let us not take his life.
Verse_Ch: 37:22 又说，不可流他的血；可以把他丢在这野地的坑里，只是不可下手害他。流便的意思是要救他脱离他们的手，把他归还他的父亲。 ###EN### And Reuben said to them, Shed no blood; throw him into this pit that is in the wilderness, but do not lay a hand on him-that he might deliver him out of their
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: hand to restore him to his father.
Verse_Ch: 37:23 约瑟到了他哥哥们那里，他们就剥了他的外衣，就是他穿的那件彩衣， ###EN### And when Joseph came to his brothers, they stripped Joseph of his coat, the coat of many colors that was on him;
Verse_Ch: 37:24 把他丢在坑里；那坑是空的，里头没有水。 ###EN### And they took him and threw him into the pit. Now the pit was empty; there was no water in it.
Verse_Ch: 37:25 于是他们坐下吃饭；他们举目观看，见有一伙米甸的以实玛利人从基列来，用骆驼驮着香胶、香油、没药，要带下埃及去。 ###EN### Then they sat down to eat food; and they lifted up their eyes and looked, and there was a caravan of Ishmaelites, coming from Gilead, with their camels bearing
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: aromatic gum and balm and myrrh, going to carry it down to Egypt.
Verse_Ch: 37:26 犹大对众弟兄说，我们杀我们的弟弟，藏了他的血，有什么益处呢？ ###EN### Then Judah said to his brothers, What gain is there if we slay our brother and conceal his blood?
Verse_Ch: 37:27 我们不如将他卖给以实玛利人，不可下手害他；因为他是我们的弟弟，我们的骨肉。众弟兄就听从了他。 ###EN### Come, and let us sell him to the Ishmaelites, and let our hand not be on him; for he is our brother, our flesh. And his brothers listened to him.
Verse_Ch: 37:28 所以当米甸的商人从那里经过，约瑟的哥哥们就把约瑟从坑里拉上来，讲定二十锭银子，把约瑟卖给以实玛利人。他们就把约瑟带到埃及去了。 ###EN### So when some Midianite traders passed by, they pulled Joseph up, lifting him out of the pit, and they sold Joseph to the Ishmaelites for twenty pieces of silver.
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: And these brought Joseph into Egypt.
Verse_Ch: 37:29 流便回到坑边，见约瑟不在坑里，就撕裂衣服， ###EN### And when Reuben returned to the pit and saw that Joseph was not in the pit, he tore his clothes.
Verse_Ch: 37:30 回到弟弟们那里，说，童子没有了，我怎么办？ ###EN### And he returned to his brothers and said, The boy is not there; so as for me, what shall I do?
Verse_Ch: 37:31 他们宰了一只公山羊，把约瑟的外衣蘸了血。 ###EN### Then they took Joseph's coat and slaughtered a male goat and dipped the coat in the blood.
Verse_Ch: 37:32 他们打发人把那件彩衣送到他们父亲那里，说，我们捡到了这个；请认一认是你儿子的外衣不是？ ###EN### And they sent the coat of many colors and had it brought to their father and said, We found this; please examine it, and see if it is your son's coat or not.
Verse_Ch: 37:33 他认得，就说，这是我儿子的外衣。有恶兽把他吃了，约瑟必定被撕碎了！ ###EN### And he recognized it and said, It is my son's coat. A wild beast has devoured him; Joseph is without doubt torn to pieces.
Verse_Ch: 37:34 雅各便撕裂衣服，腰间围上麻布，为他儿子悲哀了许多日子。 ###EN### And Jacob tore his garments and put sackcloth upon his loins and mourned for his son many days.
Verse_Ch: 37:35 他的儿子女儿都起来安慰他，他却不肯受安慰，说，我必悲悲哀哀的下阴间，到我儿子那里。约瑟的父亲就为他哀哭。 ###EN### And all his sons and all his daughters rose up to comfort him; but he refused to be comforted and said, Surely I will go down to Sheol to my son, mourning. Thus
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: his father wept for him.
Verse_Ch: 37:36 米甸人在埃及把约瑟卖给法老的内臣，护卫长波提乏。 ###EN### Meanwhile the Midianites had sold him in Egypt to Potiphar, an official of Pharaoh, the captain of the guard.
Chapter_Header: 38
Verse_Ch: 38:1 那时，犹大离开他弟兄们下去，到一个名叫希拉的亚杜兰人那里去。 ###EN### Now at that time Judah went down from his brothers and pitched his tent near a certain Adullamite, whose name was Hirah.
Verse_Ch: 38:2 犹大在那里看见一个迦南人名叫书亚的女儿，就娶她为妻，与她同房。 ###EN### And Judah saw there the daughter of a certain Canaanite whose name was Shua. And he took her and went in to her.
Verse_Ch: 38:3 她就怀孕生了一个儿子，犹大给他起名叫珥。 ###EN### And she conceived and bore a son, and he called his name Er.
Verse_Ch: 38:4 她再怀孕生了一个儿子，给他起名叫俄南。 ###EN### And she conceived again and bore a son, and she called his name Onan.
Verse_Ch: 38:5 她又生了一个儿子，给他起名叫示拉。她生示拉的时候，犹大正在基悉。 ###EN### And yet again she bore a son and called his name Shelah, and she was in Chezib when she bore him.
Verse_Ch: 38:6 犹大为长子珥娶妻，名叫他玛。 ###EN### And Judah took a wife for Er his firstborn, and her name was Tamar.
Verse_Ch: 38:7 犹大的长子珥在耶和华眼中看为恶，耶和华就叫他死了。 ###EN### And Er, Judah's firstborn, was wicked in the sight of Jehovah. And Jehovah put him to death.
Verse_Ch: 38:8 犹大对俄南说，你当与你哥哥的妻子同房，向她尽你为弟的本分，为你哥哥生子立后。 ###EN### And Judah said to Onan, Go in to your brother's wife, and perform the duty of a brother-in-law to her, and raise up seed to your brother.
Verse_Ch: 38:9 但俄南知道生子不归自己，所以每当同房便遗在地，免得给他哥哥留后。 ###EN### But since Onan knew that the seed would not be his, whenever he went in to his brother's wife, he spilled it on the ground, so that he would not give seed to his
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: brother.
Verse_Ch: 38:10 他所作的在耶和华眼中看为恶，耶和华也叫他死了。 ###EN### But what he did was evil in the sight of Jehovah, so He put him to death also.
Verse_Ch: 38:11 犹大心里说，恐怕示拉也死，像他两个哥哥一样，就对他儿媳他玛说，你去，在你父亲家里守寡，等我儿子示拉长大。他玛就回去，住在她父亲家里。 ###EN### Then Judah said to Tamar his daughter-in-law, Remain a widow in your father's house until Shelah my son grows up. For he thought, He also may die, like his
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: brothers. So Tamar went and dwelt in her father's house.
Verse_Ch: 38:12 过了许久，犹大的妻子，书亚的女儿死了。后来犹大得了安慰，就和他的朋友亚杜兰人希拉上亭拿去，到他剪羊毛的人那里。 ###EN### And in process of time Shua's daughter, the wife of Judah, died; and Judah was comforted and went up to his sheepshearers at Timnah, he and his friend Hirah
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: the Adullamite.
Verse_Ch: 38:13 有人告诉他玛说，你的公公上亭拿剪羊毛去了。 ###EN### And it was told to Tamar, saying, Your father-in-law is now going up to Timnah to shear his sheep.
Verse_Ch: 38:14 他玛见示拉已经长大，还没有娶她为妻，就脱了她作寡妇的衣裳，用帕子蒙着脸，又遮住身体，坐在往亭拿路上的伊拿印城门口。 ###EN### And she removed from herself her widow's garments and covered herself with a veil and wrapped herself and sat in the gate of Enaim, which is on the way to
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: Timnah; for she saw that Shelah had grown up, and she had not been given to him as his wife.
Verse_Ch: 38:15 犹大看见她，以为是妓女，因为她蒙着脸。 ###EN### And when Judah saw her, he thought she was a harlot, for she had covered her face.
Verse_Ch: 38:16 犹大就转到她那里去，说，来罢，让我与你同寝。他原不知道是他的儿媳。他玛说，你要与我同寝，把什么给我呢？ ###EN### And he turned aside to her by the way and said, Come now, let me come in to you; for he did not know that she was his daughter-in-law. And she said, What
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: will you give me, that you may come in to me?
Verse_Ch: 38:17 犹大说，我从羊群里取一只山羊羔，打发人送来给你。他玛说，在未送以先，你要给我一个抵押才行。 ###EN### And he said, I will send you a kid from the flock. And she said, Only if you give me a pledge until you send it.
Verse_Ch: 38:18 他说，我给你什么作抵押呢？他玛说，你的印、你的带子、和你手里的杖。犹大就给了她，与她同寝，她就从犹大怀了孕。 ###EN### And he said, What pledge shall I give you? And she said, Your seal and your cord and your staff that is in your hand. And he gave them to her and went in to her,
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: and she conceived by him.
Verse_Ch: 38:19 他玛起来走了，除去帕子，仍旧穿上作寡妇的衣裳。 ###EN### And she arose and went away, and removed her veil from herself and put on her widow's garments.
Verse_Ch: 38:20 犹大托他朋友亚杜兰人送一只山羊羔去，要从那女人手里取回抵押，却找不着她， ###EN### And Judah sent the kid by the hand of his friend the Adullamite, to receive the pledge from the woman's hand; but he did not find her.
Verse_Ch: 38:21 就问那地方的人说，伊拿印路旁的妓女在那里？他们说，这里从来没有妓女。 ###EN### Then he asked the men of her place, saying, Where is the prostitute who was by the road at Enaim? And they said, There has been no prostitute here.
Verse_Ch: 38:22 他回去见犹大说，我没有找着她，并且那地方的人说，这里从来没有妓女。 ###EN### And he returned to Judah and said, I did not find her; and also the men of the place said, There has been no prostitute here.
Verse_Ch: 38:23 犹大说，我把这山羊羔送去了，你竟找不着她。任凭她留着那些东西罢，免得我们成了笑柄。 ###EN### And Judah said, Let her keep the things for herself, lest we become a laughing stock; you see, I sent her this kid, but you did not find her.
Verse_Ch: 38:24 约过了三个月，有人告诉犹大说，你的儿媳他玛作了妓女，且因行淫有了身孕。犹大说，拉出她来，把她烧了！ ###EN### And about three months later it was told Judah, saying, Tamar your daughter-in-law has played the harlot; moreover, now she is pregnant by harlotry. And
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: Judah said, Bring her out, and let her be burned.
Verse_Ch: 38:25 他玛被拉出来的时候，打发人去见她公公，对他说，这些东西是谁的，我就是从谁怀的孕。请你认一认，这印和带子并杖都是谁的？ ###EN### As she was being brought out, she sent word to her father-in-law, saying, I am pregnant by the man to whom these belong. And she said, Please note whose
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: these are, the seal and the cords and the staff.
Verse_Ch: 38:26 犹大认出这些东西，就说，她比我更有义，因为我没有将她给我的儿子示拉。从此犹大不再与她同寝了。 ###EN### And Judah took note of them and said, She is more righteous than I, because I did not give her to my son Shelah. And he did not know her again anymore.
Verse_Ch: 38:27 他玛将要生产，不料她腹里是孪生子。 ###EN### And at the time of her delivery, there were twins in her womb.
Verse_Ch: 38:28 到生产的时候，一个孩子伸出一只手来；收生婆拿一条朱红线拴在他手上，说，这一个是先生出来的。 ###EN### And while she was giving birth, one put out a hand; and the midwife took and tied on his hand a scarlet thread, saying, This one came out first.
Verse_Ch: 38:29 随后这孩子把手收回去，他哥哥生出来了；收生婆说，你为什么抢着来呢？因此他名叫法勒斯。 ###EN### But when he drew back his hand, his brother suddenly came out; and she said, What a breach you have made for yourself! Therefore his name was called Perez.
Verse_Ch: 38:30 后来，他那手上有朱红线的弟弟也生出来，他就名叫谢拉。 ###EN### And afterward his brother came out, who had the scarlet thread on his hand; and his name was called Zerah.
Chapter_Header: 39
Verse_Ch: 39:1 约瑟被带下埃及去。有一个埃及人，法老的内臣，护卫长波提乏，从那些带他下来的以实玛利人手下把他买去。 ###EN### Now Joseph was brought down to Egypt; and Potiphar, an official of Pharaoh, the captain of the guard, an Egyptian, bought him from the Ishmaelites who had
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: brought him down there.
Verse_Ch: 39:2 约瑟住在他主人埃及人的家中，耶和华与他同在，他就凡事亨通。 ###EN### And Jehovah was with Joseph, and he became a prosperous man; and he was in the house of his Egyptian master.
Verse_Ch: 39:3 他主人见耶和华与他同在，又见耶和华使他手里所办的尽都顺利， ###EN### And his master saw that Jehovah was with him and that Jehovah caused all that he did to prosper in his hand.
Verse_Ch: 39:4 约瑟就在主人眼前蒙恩，伺候他主人；主人派他管理家务，把一切所有的都交在他手里。 ###EN### And Joseph found favor in his sight, and he ministered to him; and he made him overseer of his house and put all that he hadin his charge.
Verse_Ch: 39:5 自从主人派约瑟管理家务和他一切所有的，耶和华就因约瑟的缘故赐福与那埃及人的家；他家里和田间一切所有的，都蒙耶和华赐福。 ###EN### And from the time he made him overseer in his house and put him over all that he had, Jehovah blessed the Egyptian's house on account of Joseph; and the
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: blessing of Jehovah was upon all that he had, in the house and in the field.
Verse_Ch: 39:6 波提乏将一切所有的都交在约瑟的手中，除了自己所吃的饭，别的事一概不管。约瑟原来形貌俊美。 ###EN### And he left all that he had in Joseph's charge; and with him there, he was not concerned about anything except the food that he ate. And Joseph was handsome
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: in form and handsome in appearance.
Verse_Ch: 39:7 这事以后，约瑟主人的妻子以目送情给约瑟，说，你与我同寝罢。 ###EN### Now after these things his master's wife cast her eyes upon Joseph and said, Lie with me.
Verse_Ch: 39:8 约瑟不肯，对他主人的妻子说，看哪，有我在，家里一切事务我主人都不管；他把所有的都交在我手里。 ###EN### But he refused and said to his master's wife, Behold, with me here, my master is not concerned about anything in the house, and he has put everything he has in
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: my charge.
Verse_Ch: 39:9 在这家里没有比我大的；并且他没有留下一样不交给我，只留下了你，因为你是他的妻子。我怎能作这大恶，得罪神呢？ ###EN### There is no one greater in this house than I, and he has withheld nothing from me except you, because you are his wife. How then can I do this great evil, and sin
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: against God?
Verse_Ch: 39:10 后来她天天对约瑟说，约瑟却不听从，不与她同寝，也不和她在一处。 ###EN### And although she spoke to Joseph day after day, he would not listen to her to lie beside her or be with her.
Verse_Ch: 39:11 有一天，约瑟进屋里去办事，家中的人没有一个在屋里， ###EN### And one such day he went into the house to do his work, and none of the men of the house were there in the house.
Verse_Ch: 39:12 妇人就拉住他的衣裳，说，你与我同寝罢。约瑟把衣裳撇在妇人手里，跑到外面去了。 ###EN### And she grabbed him by his garment, saying, Lie with me! But he left his garment in her hand, and fled and went outside.
Verse_Ch: 39:13 妇人看见约瑟把衣裳撇在她手里跑出去了， ###EN### And when she saw that he had left his garment in her hand and had fled outside,
Verse_Ch: 39:14 就叫了家里的人来，对他们说，你们看，他带了一个希伯来人到我们这里，要戏弄我们。他到我这里来，要与我同寝，我就大声喊叫。 ###EN### She called to the men of her house and spoke to them, saying, See, he has brought in a Hebrew man to us to mock us. He came in to me to lie with me, and I
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: called out with a loud voice;
Verse_Ch: 39:15 他听见我放声喊起来，就把衣裳撇在我身边，跑到外面去了。 ###EN### And when he heard that I lifted up my voice and called out, he left his garment beside me, and fled and went outside.
Verse_Ch: 39:16 妇人把约瑟的衣裳放在自己身边，等着他主人回家， ###EN### And she placed his garment beside her until his master came home.
Verse_Ch: 39:17 就对他如此说：你所带到我们这里的那希伯来仆人，进来要戏弄我， ###EN### And she spoke to him with these words, saying, The Hebrew servant, whom you have brought to us, came in to me to mock me.
Verse_Ch: 39:18 我放声喊起来，他就把衣裳撇在我身边，跑出去了。 ###EN### And when I lifted up my voice and called out, he left his garment beside me and fled outside.
Verse_Ch: 39:19 约瑟的主人听见他妻子对他所说的话，说，你的仆人如此待我，他就发怒， ###EN### And when his master heard the words of his wife that she had spoken to him, saying, This is the way your servant treated me; his anger burned.
Verse_Ch: 39:20 把约瑟拿住，下在监里，就是王的囚犯被囚的地方。但是当约瑟在监里的时候， ###EN### And Joseph's master took him and put him into the prison, the place where the king's prisoners were confined. But while he was there in the prison,
Verse_Ch: 39:21 耶和华与约瑟同在，向他施恩慈，使他在狱长眼前蒙恩。 ###EN### Jehovah was with Joseph; and He extended kindness to him and gave him favor in the sight of the chief jailer.
Verse_Ch: 39:22 狱长把监里所有的囚犯都交在约瑟手下；他们在那里无论作什么事，都是经他的手作的。 ###EN### And the chief jailer put in Joseph's charge all the prisoners who were in the prison; and whatever was done there, he was the one to do it.
Verse_Ch: 39:23 凡在约瑟手下的事，狱长一概不察，因为耶和华与约瑟同在；耶和华使他所作的尽都顺利。 ###EN### The chief jailer did not supervise anything that was in his charge, because Jehovah was with him; and whatever he did, Jehovah caused it to prosper.
Chapter_Header: 40
Verse_Ch: 40:1 这些事以后，埃及王的司酒和司膳得罪了他们的主埃及王， ###EN### And after these things, the cupbearer and the baker of the king of Egypt offended their lord, the king of Egypt.
Verse_Ch: 40:2 法老就恼怒司酒长和司膳长这两个内臣， ###EN### And Pharaoh was angry with his two officials, the chief of the cupbearers and the chief of the bakers.
Verse_Ch: 40:3 把他们拘禁在护卫长府内的监里，就是约瑟被囚的地方。 ###EN### And he put them in custody at the house of the captain of the guard, in the prison, the place where Joseph was confined.
Verse_Ch: 40:4 护卫长把他们交给约瑟，约瑟便伺候他们；他们被拘禁了一些日子。 ###EN### And the captain of the guard put Joseph in charge of them, and he ministered to them; and they were in custody for some time.
Verse_Ch: 40:5 被囚在监之埃及王的司酒和司膳，二人同夜各作了一个梦，各梦都有讲解。 ###EN### And the cupbearer and the baker of the king of Egypt, who were confined in the prison, both of them had a dream, each man with his own dream in one night,
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: and each dream with its own interpretation.
Verse_Ch: 40:6 到了早晨，约瑟到他们那里，见他们甚是愁闷。 ###EN### And Joseph came to them in the morning and looked at them, and they were troubled.
Verse_Ch: 40:7 他便问法老的两个内臣，就是与他同被拘禁在他主人府里的，说，你们今日为什么面带愁容？ ###EN### And he asked Pharaoh's officials, who were with him in custody in his master's house, saying, Why are your faces so sad today?
Verse_Ch: 40:8 他们对他说，我们各人作了一个梦，没有人能解。约瑟说，解梦不是神的事么？请你们将梦告诉我。 ###EN### And they said to him, We have had a dream, and there is no one to interpret it. And Joseph said to them, Do not interpretations belong to God? Please tell it to
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: me.
Verse_Ch: 40:9 司酒长便将他的梦告诉约瑟，说，我梦见在我面前有一棵葡萄树， ###EN### And the chief of the cupbearers told his dream to Joseph and said to him, In my dream there was a vine before me,
Verse_Ch: 40:10 树上有三根枝子，一发了芽，就开花，并且上头一挂一挂的葡萄都成熟了。 ###EN### And on the vine were three branches. And as soon as it budded, its blossoms came out, and its clusters ripened into grapes.
Verse_Ch: 40:11 法老的杯在我手中，我就拿葡萄挤在法老的杯里，将杯递在他手中。 ###EN### And Pharaoh's cup was in my hand, and I took the grapes and squeezed them into Pharaoh's cup, and I put the cup in Pharaoh's hand.
Verse_Ch: 40:12 约瑟对他说，这梦的讲解是这样：三根枝子就是三天； ###EN### And Joseph said to him, This is its interpretation: The three branches are three days.
Verse_Ch: 40:13 三天之内，法老必提你出监，叫你恢复原职，你就要照先前作司酒时的惯例，递杯在法老的手中。 ###EN### Within three more days Pharaoh will lift up your head and restore you to your office, and you will put Pharaoh's cup into his hand according to your former custom
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: when you were his cupbearer.
Verse_Ch: 40:14 但你得好处的时候，求你记得我，施恩慈与我，向法老题说我，救我出这府牢。 ###EN### But remember my being with you when it is well with you, and please do me a kindness and make mention of me to Pharaoh and so have me brought out of this
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: house.
Verse_Ch: 40:15 我实在是从希伯来人之地被拐来的；我在这里也没有作过什么，叫他们把我下在牢里。 ###EN### For I was actually kidnapped out of the land of the Hebrews, and here also I have not done anything that they should put me into the dungeon.
Verse_Ch: 40:16 司膳长见梦解得好，就对约瑟说，我也作了一个梦，见我头上顶着三筐白饼； ###EN### Now when the chief of the bakers saw that the interpretation was good, he said to Joseph, I also saw this in my dream: There were three baskets of white bread
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: on my head.
Verse_Ch: 40:17 最上面的筐子里有为法老烤的各样食物，但是有飞鸟来吃我头上筐子里的食物。 ###EN### And in the uppermost basket there were all sorts of baked food for Pharaoh, but the birds were eating them out of the basket on my head.
Verse_Ch: 40:18 约瑟回答说，这梦的讲解是这样：三个筐子就是三天； ###EN### And Joseph answered and said, This is its interpretation: The three baskets are three days.
Verse_Ch: 40:19 三天之内，法老必斩你的头，把你挂在木头上，必有飞鸟来吃你身上的肉。 ###EN### Within three more days Pharaoh will lift up your head from you and will hang you on a tree, and the birds will eat your flesh from you.
Verse_Ch: 40:20 到了第三天，是法老的生日，他为众臣仆设摆筵席，把司酒长和司膳长提出监来， ###EN### And on the third day, which was Pharaoh's birthday, he made a feast for all his servants; and he lifted up the head of the chief of the cupbearers and the head of
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: the chief of the bakers among his servants.
Verse_Ch: 40:21 使司酒长恢复司酒的职位，他就递杯在法老手中； ###EN### And he restored the chief of the cupbearers to his cupbearing, and he put the cup into Pharaoh's hand;
Verse_Ch: 40:22 却把司膳长挂起来，正如约瑟向他们所讲解的。 ###EN### But the chief of the bakers he hanged, just as Joseph had interpreted to them.
Verse_Ch: 40:23 司酒长却不记得约瑟，竟把他忘了。 ###EN### Yet the chief of the cupbearers did not remember Joseph, but forgot him.
Chapter_Header: 41
Verse_Ch: 41:1 过了整整两年，法老作了一个梦，见自己站在河边， ###EN### And at the end of two full years Pharaoh had a dream, and there he was, standing by the River.
Verse_Ch: 41:2 有七只母牛从河里上来，又美好又肥壮，在芦苇中吃草。 ###EN### And there came up out of the River seven cows, fine looking and fat fleshed; and they grazed in the reed grass.
Verse_Ch: 41:3 随后又有七只母牛从河里上来，又丑陋又干瘦，站在河岸上那七只母牛的旁边。 ###EN### Then there came up after them seven other cows out of the River, ugly looking and thin fleshed; and they stood beside the other cows on the bank of the River.
Verse_Ch: 41:4 这些又丑陋又干瘦的母牛，吃尽了那七只又美好又肥壮的母牛；法老就醒了。 ###EN### And the ugly looking and thin fleshed cows ate up the seven fine looking and fat cows. Then Pharaoh awoke.
Verse_Ch: 41:5 他又睡着，第二次作梦，见一棵麦子长了七个穗子，又肥大又佳美， ###EN### And he slept and dreamed a second time. And there were seven ears of grain, coming up on one stalk, fat and good.
Verse_Ch: 41:6 随后又长了七个穗子，又细弱，又被东风吹焦了。 ###EN### Then there were seven ears, thin and scorched by the east wind, that sprouted after them.
Verse_Ch: 41:7 这些细弱的穗子，吞下了那七个又肥大又饱满的穗子；法老醒了，原来是个梦。 ###EN### And the thin ears swallowed up the seven fat and full ears. Then Pharaoh awoke, and it was a dream.
Verse_Ch: 41:8 到了早晨，法老灵里不安，就差人召了埃及所有的术士和智慧人来；法老把所作的梦告诉他们，却没有人能给法老讲解。 ###EN### And in the morning his spirit was troubled, so he sent and called for all the magicians of Egypt and all her wise men; and Pharaoh told them his dream, but there
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: was no one who could interpret them to Pharaoh.
Verse_Ch: 41:9 那时司酒长对法老说，我今日想起我的罪来。 ###EN### Then the chief cupbearer spoke to Pharaoh, saying, I do remember my sins today.
Verse_Ch: 41:10 从前法老恼怒臣仆，把我和司膳长拘禁在护卫长府内。 ###EN### Pharaoh was angry with his servants, and he put me in custody at the house of the captain of the guard, both me and the chief baker.
Verse_Ch: 41:11 我们二人同夜各作了一个梦，各梦都有讲解。 ###EN### And we both had a dream in one night, I and he; each of us had a dream with its own interpretation.
Verse_Ch: 41:12 在那里同着我们有一个希伯来的少年人，是护卫长的仆人，我们将梦告诉他，他就给我们讲解，是按着各人的梦讲解的。 ###EN### And a young Hebrew man was there with us, a servant of the captain of the guard. And we told him our dreams, and he interpreted them for us; to each one he
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: interpreted according to his dream.
Verse_Ch: 41:13 后来正如他给我们讲解的成就了；法老使我官复原职，却把司膳长挂了起来。 ###EN### And as he interpreted to us, so it happened; Pharaoh restored me to my office, and he hanged the baker.
Verse_Ch: 41:14 于是法老差人去召约瑟，他们便急忙带他出牢，他就剃头刮脸，换衣裳，进到法老面前。 ###EN### Then Pharaoh sent and called for Joseph, and they brought him hastily out of the dungeon; and he had shaved himself and changed his garments, and he came
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: to Pharaoh.
Verse_Ch: 41:15 法老对约瑟说，我作了一个梦，没有人能解；我听见人说，你听了梦就能解。 ###EN### And Pharaoh said to Joseph, I have had a dream, but there is no one who can interpret it; and I have heard it said of you that when you hear a dream you can
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: interpret it.
Verse_Ch: 41:16 约瑟回答法老说，这不在于我，神必将平安的话回答法老。 ###EN### And Joseph answered Pharaoh, saying, It is not of me; God will give Pharaoh a favorable answer.
Verse_Ch: 41:17 法老对约瑟说，我梦见我站在河岸上， ###EN### And Pharaoh spoke to Joseph, In my dream, there I was, standing on the bank of the River.
Verse_Ch: 41:18 有七只母牛从河里上来，又肥壮又美好，在芦苇中吃草。 ###EN### And there came up out of the River seven cows, fat fleshed and fine looking; and they grazed in the reed grass.
Verse_Ch: 41:19 随后又有七只母牛上来，又软弱又丑陋又干瘦，在埃及遍地，我没有见过这样不好的。 ###EN### Then there came up after them seven other cows, poor and very ugly looking and thin fleshed; I had never seen such in all the land of Egypt for ugliness.
Verse_Ch: 41:20 这些又干瘦又丑陋的母牛，吃尽了那以先的七只肥母牛， ###EN### And the thin and ugly looking cows ate up the first seven fat cows.
Verse_Ch: 41:21 吞吃了以后，却看不出是吞吃了，它们丑陋的样子仍和先前一样；我就醒了。 ###EN### And when they had swallowed them, no one would have known that they had swallowed them, for they were still as ugly looking as at the beginning. Then I
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: awoke.
Verse_Ch: 41:22 我又梦见一棵麦子，长了七个穗子，又饱满又佳美； ###EN### And I saw this in my next dream: There were seven ears of grain, coming up on one stalk, full and good.
Verse_Ch: 41:23 随后又长了七个穗子，枯槁细弱，被东风吹焦了。 ###EN### Then there were seven ears, withered, thin, and scorched by the east wind, that sprouted after them.
Verse_Ch: 41:24 这些细弱的穗子，吞下了那七个佳美的穗子。我将这梦告诉了术士，却没有人能给我解说。 ###EN### And the thin ears swallowed up the seven good ears. And I told it to the magicians, but there was no one who could explain it to me.
Verse_Ch: 41:25 约瑟对法老说，法老的梦乃是一个；神已将祂要作的事指示法老了。 ###EN### Then Joseph said to Pharaoh, Pharaoh's dream is one dream; what God is about to do He has told Pharaoh.
Verse_Ch: 41:26 七只好母牛是七年，七个好穗子也是七年；这梦乃是一个。 ###EN### The seven good cows are seven years, and the seven good ears are seven years; the dream is one.
Verse_Ch: 41:27 那随后上来的七只又干瘦又丑陋的母牛是七年，那七个中空、被东风吹焦的穗子也是七年，都是七个荒年。 ###EN### And the seven thin and ugly looking cows that came up after them are seven years, and so are the seven empty ears scorched by the east wind; they will be
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: seven years of famine.
Verse_Ch: 41:28 这就是我对法老所说，神已将祂要作的事显明给法老了。 ###EN### This matter is just as I have spoken to Pharaoh; what God is about to do He has shown to Pharaoh.
Verse_Ch: 41:29 埃及遍地必来七个大丰年； ###EN### Seven years of great abundance are now about to come throughout all the land of Egypt.
Verse_Ch: 41:30 随后又来七个荒年，甚至埃及地都忘了先前的丰收，这地必被饥荒所耗尽。 ###EN### Then seven years of famine will arise after them, and all the abundance in the land of Egypt will be forgotten, and the famine will consume the land.
Verse_Ch: 41:31 因那后来的饥荒极重，这地便不觉得先前的丰收了。 ###EN### And the abundance will be unknown in the land because of that famine which follows, for it will be very severe.
Verse_Ch: 41:32 至于法老两次重复作梦，是因这事乃神所命定，而且神必速速成就。 ###EN### And as for the repeating of the dream to Pharaoh twice, it means that the matter is determined by God, and God will quickly bring it about.
Verse_Ch: 41:33 所以法老当拣选一个精明、智慧的人，派他治理埃及地。 ###EN### Now therefore let Pharaoh look out for a discerning and wise man, and set him over the land of Egypt.
Verse_Ch: 41:34 法老当这样行：派官员管理这地，在七个丰年的时候，征收埃及地出产的五分之一； ###EN### Let Pharaoh take action to appoint overseers over the land and take a fifth of the produce of the land of Egypt in the seven years of abundance.
Verse_Ch: 41:35 叫他们把将来好年一切的粮食聚敛起来，积蓄谷物，收存在各城里作粮食，归于法老的手下。 ###EN### And let them gather all the food of these coming good years and lay up grain under Pharaoh's authority for food in the cities, and let them keep it.
Verse_Ch: 41:36 所储存的粮食，可以防备埃及地将有的七个荒年，免得这地被饥荒所灭。 ###EN### And let the food become a reserve for the land against the seven years of famine that will be in the land of Egypt, so that the land does not perish in the famine.
Verse_Ch: 41:37 法老和他的众臣仆，都以这话为美。 ###EN### And the word seemed good to Pharaoh and to all his servants.
Verse_Ch: 41:38 法老对臣仆说，像这样的人，有神的灵在他里面，我们岂能找得着呢？ ###EN### And Pharaoh said to his servants, Can we find such a man like this, in whom the Spirit of God is?
Verse_Ch: 41:39 法老对约瑟说，神既将这事都指示你，可见没有人像你这样精明、智慧。 ###EN### And Pharaoh said to Joseph, Since God let you know all this, there is no one as discerning and wise as you.
Verse_Ch: 41:40 你必掌管我的家，我的民都必照你的话受管理；惟独在宝座上我比你大。 ###EN### You shall be over my household, and according to your word all my people shall be ruled; only in the throne will I be greater than you.
Verse_Ch: 41:41 法老又对约瑟说，看哪，我派你治理埃及全地。 ###EN### Then Pharaoh said to Joseph, See, I have set you over all the land of Egypt.
Verse_Ch: 41:42 法老就摘下手上打印的戒指，戴在约瑟的手上，给他穿上细麻衣，把金链戴在他的颈项上； ###EN### And Pharaoh took off his signet ring from his hand and put it upon Joseph's hand, and clothed him in garments of fine linen, and put a gold chain around his
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: neck.
Verse_Ch: 41:43 又叫约瑟坐他的副车，喝道的在前呼叫说，跪下。这样，法老派他治理埃及全地。 ###EN### And he made him ride in the chariot of his second-in-command, and they cried out before him, Bow the knee! And he set him over all the land of Egypt.
Verse_Ch: 41:44 法老对约瑟说，我是法老，在埃及全地，若没有你的许可，人不得擅自办事。 ###EN### And Pharaoh said to Joseph, I am Pharaoh, yet without your consent no man will lift up his hand or his foot in all the land of Egypt.
Verse_Ch: 41:45 法老赐名给约瑟，叫撒发那忒巴内亚，又将安城的祭司波提非拉的女儿亚西纳给他为妻。约瑟就出去巡行埃及地。 ###EN### And Pharaoh called Joseph's name Zaphenath-paneah, and he gave him Asenath, the daughter of Potiphera priest of On, as his wife. And Joseph went out over
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: the land of Egypt.
Verse_Ch: 41:46 约瑟开始侍立在埃及王法老面前的时候，年三十岁。他从法老面前出去，遍行埃及全地。 ###EN### Now Joseph was thirty years old when he stood before Pharaoh, the king of Egypt. And Joseph went out from the presence of Pharaoh and passed through all
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: the land of Egypt.
Verse_Ch: 41:47 七个丰年之内，地的出产极丰极盛。 ###EN### And in the seven years of abundance the earth produced copiously.
Verse_Ch: 41:48 约瑟聚敛埃及地那七年一切的粮食，把粮食积存在各城里；各城周围田地的粮食，都积存在本城里。 ###EN### And he gathered up all the food of the seven years which came upon the land of Egypt and put the food in the cities; he placed the food from the surrounding
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: fields within each city.
Verse_Ch: 41:49 约瑟积蓄谷物甚多，如同海沙，多到不再加以计算，因为无法计算。 ###EN### And Joseph stored grain in great abundance like the sand of the sea until he stopped measuring it; for it was beyond measure.
Verse_Ch: 41:50 荒年未到以前，安城的祭司波提非拉的女儿亚西纳，给约瑟生了两个儿子。 ###EN### And before the year of famine came, two sons were born to Joseph, whom Asenath, the daughter of Potiphera priest of On, bore to him.
Verse_Ch: 41:51 约瑟给长子起名叫玛拿西，因为他说，神使我忘了一切的困苦，和我父的全家。 ###EN### And Joseph called the name of the firstborn Manasseh, for, he said, God has made me forget all my trouble and all my father's house.
Verse_Ch: 41:52 他给次子起名叫以法莲，因为他说，神使我在受苦之地繁衍。 ###EN### And he called the name of the second Ephraim, for, he said, God has made me fruitful in the land of my affliction.
Verse_Ch: 41:53 埃及地的七个丰年一过， ###EN### And the seven years of plenty that came upon the land of Egypt came to an end.
Verse_Ch: 41:54 七个荒年就来了，正如约瑟所说的。各地都有饥荒，惟独埃及全地有粮食。 ###EN### And the seven years of famine began to come, as Joseph had said. And there was famine in all lands, but in all the land of Egypt there was bread.
Verse_Ch: 41:55 等到埃及全地有了饥荒，众民就向法老哀求粮食。法老对所有的埃及人说，你们往约瑟那里去，凡他所说的，你们都要作。 ###EN### So when all the land of Egypt became hungry, the people cried out to Pharaoh for bread. And Pharaoh said to all the Egyptians, Go to Joseph; whatever he says
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: to you, you shall do.
Verse_Ch: 41:56 当时饥荒遍满地面，约瑟开了各处的粮仓，卖粮给埃及人；在埃及地的饥荒逐渐加重。 ###EN### And when the famine was over all the face of the earth, Joseph opened all the storehouses of grain and sold grain to the Egyptians; and the famine became
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: severe in the land of Egypt.
Verse_Ch: 41:57 全地的人都往埃及去，到约瑟那里买粮，因为全地的饥荒甚重。 ###EN### And all the earth came to Joseph in Egypt to buy grain, because the famine was severe in all the earth.
Chapter_Header: 42
Verse_Ch: 42:1 雅各见埃及有粮，就对儿子们说，你们为什么彼此观望呢？ ###EN### Now when Jacob saw that there was grain in Egypt, Jacob said to his sons, Why do you keep looking at one another?
Verse_Ch: 42:2 我听见埃及有粮，你们可以下去，从那里为我们买些来，使我们可以存活，不至于死。 ###EN### And he said, I have now heard that there is grain in Egypt; go down there, and buy grain for us from there, that we may live and not die.
Verse_Ch: 42:3 于是，约瑟的十个哥哥都下埃及买粮去了。 ###EN### So Joseph's ten brothers went down to buy grain from Egypt.
Verse_Ch: 42:4 但雅各没有打发约瑟的弟弟便雅悯与他哥哥们同去，因为雅各说，恐怕他遭害。 ###EN### But Jacob did not send Joseph's brother Benjamin with his brothers, for he said, Perhaps harm may befall him.
Verse_Ch: 42:5 来买粮的人中有以色列的儿子们，因为迦南地也有饥荒。 ###EN### And the sons of Israel came to buy grain among those who also came, for the famine was in the land of Canaan.
Verse_Ch: 42:6 当时治理埃及地的是约瑟；卖粮给那地众民的就是他。约瑟的哥哥们来了，面伏于地，向他下拜。 ###EN### Now Joseph was the governor over the land; it was he who sold grain to all the people of the land. And Joseph's brothers came and bowed down to him with
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: their faces to the ground.
Verse_Ch: 42:7 约瑟看见他哥哥们，就认得他们，却装作生人，向他们说些严厉的话，问他们说，你们从那里来？他们说，我们从迦南地来买粮。 ###EN### And Joseph saw his brothers and recognized them, but he disguised himself to them and spoke harshly with them. And he said to them, Where have you come
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: from? And they said, From the land of Canaan, to buy grain for food.
Verse_Ch: 42:8 约瑟认得他哥哥们，他们却不认得他。 ###EN### And Joseph recognized his brothers, but they did not recognize him.
Verse_Ch: 42:9 约瑟想起从前所作关于他们的那两个梦，就对他们说，你们是奸细，来窥探这地的虚实。 ###EN### And Joseph remembered the dreams that he had dreamed about them, and he said to them, You are spies; you have come to see the nakedness of the land.
Verse_Ch: 42:10 他们对他说，我主阿，不是的，仆人们是来买粮食的。 ###EN### And they said to him, No, my lord; rather your servants have come to buy grain for food.
Verse_Ch: 42:11 我们都是一个人的儿子，是诚实人；仆人们从来没有作过奸细。 ###EN### We are all sons of one man. We are honest men; your servants have never been spies.
Verse_Ch: 42:12 约瑟说，不然，你们必是来窥探这地虚实的。 ###EN### And he said to them, No; but you have come to see the nakedness of the land.
Verse_Ch: 42:13 他们说，仆人们本是弟兄十二人，是迦南地一个人的儿子，最小的现今在我们的父亲那里，还有一个没有了。 ###EN### And they said, We, your servants, are twelve brothers, the sons of one man in the land of Canaan; and at this moment the youngest is with our father today, and
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: one is no more.
Verse_Ch: 42:14 约瑟说，我才说你们是奸细，这话实在不错。 ###EN### But Joseph said to them, It is just as I spoke to you, saying, You are spies.
Verse_Ch: 42:15 我指着法老的性命起誓，若是你们最小的弟弟不到这里来，你们就不得出这地方，藉此就可以把你们试验出来了。 ###EN### By this you shall be tested: As Pharaoh lives, you shall not go away from this place unless your youngest brother comes here.
Verse_Ch: 42:16 要打发你们中间一个人去，把你们的弟弟带来。至于你们，都要囚在这里，好试验你们的话真不真；若不真，我指着法老的性命起誓，你们必定是奸细。 ###EN### Send one of you to get your brother, while you remain bound, that your words may be tested whether there is truth in you. And if not, as Pharaoh lives, surely you
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: are spies.
Verse_Ch: 42:17 于是约瑟把他们一起拘禁了三天。 ###EN### And he put them all together in custody three days.
Verse_Ch: 42:18 到第三天，约瑟对他们说，我是敬畏神的；你们照我的话行，就可以存活。 ###EN### And Joseph said to them on the third day, Do this and live, for I fear God.
Verse_Ch: 42:19 你们如果是诚实人，可以留你们弟兄中的一个，囚在你们拘禁的地方，但你们其余的可以带着粮回去，救你们家里的饥荒。 ###EN### If you are honest men, let one of your brothers remain bound in your place of custody; and the rest of you go, carry grain for the famine of your households.
Verse_Ch: 42:20 把你们最小的弟弟带到我这里来，如此，你们的话便得证实，你们也不至于死。他们就这样行。 ###EN### And bring your youngest brother to me, that your words may be verified; and you will not die. And they did so.
Verse_Ch: 42:21 他们彼此说，我们对我们的弟弟实在有罪。他哀求我们的时候，我们见他魂里的痛苦，却不肯听，所以这场苦难临到了我们。 ###EN### And they said one to another, We are indeed guilty concerning our brother, because we saw the distress of his soul when he pleaded with us, yet we would not
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: listen; therefore this distress has come to us.
Verse_Ch: 42:22 流便说，我岂不是对你们说过，不可犯罪害那孩子么？只是你们不肯听，所以流他血的罪现在向我们追讨。 ###EN### And Reuben answered them, saying, Did I not speak to you, saying, Do not sin against the child? But you would not listen. So now also his blood is required.
Verse_Ch: 42:23 他们不知道约瑟听得懂，因为在他们中间有传译的人。 ###EN### And they did not know that Joseph understood, for there was an interpreter between them.
Verse_Ch: 42:24 约瑟转身退去，哭了一场，又回来对他们说话。他从他们中间挑出西缅来，在他们眼前把他捆绑了。 ###EN### And he turned away from them and wept. Then he returned to them and spoke to them. And he took Simeon from among them and bound him before their eyes.
Verse_Ch: 42:25 约瑟吩咐人把谷物装满他们的器皿，把各人的银子归还在各人的粮袋里，又给他们路上用的食物；人就照他的话办了。 ###EN### Then Joseph gave orders to fill their bags with grain and to restore every man's silver pieces into his sack and to give them provisions for the way. And thus was it
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: done for them.
Verse_Ch: 42:26 他们就把粮驮在驴上，离开那里去了。 ###EN### And they loaded their grain upon their donkeys and departed from there.
Verse_Ch: 42:27 到了住宿的地方，他们中间有一个人打开粮袋，要拿饲粮喂驴，才看见自己的银子仍在袋口； ###EN### And one of them opened his sack to give his donkey fodder at the lodging place, and he saw his silver; there it was in the mouth of his sack.
Verse_Ch: 42:28 就对弟兄们说，我的银子归还了，看哪，仍在我袋子里。他们就提心吊胆，战战兢兢的彼此说，这是神向我们作什么呢？ ###EN### And he said to his brothers, My silver has been returned; and here it is in my sack! And their heart stopped, and they turned trembling to one another, saying,
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: What is this that God has done to us?
Verse_Ch: 42:29 他们来到迦南地他们的父亲雅各那里，将所遭遇的事都告诉他，说， ###EN### And they came to Jacob their father in the land of Canaan and told him all that had happened to them, saying,
Verse_Ch: 42:30 那人，那地的主，对我们说严厉的话，把我们当作窥探那地的奸细。 ###EN### The man, the lord of the land, spoke harshly to us and took us for spies on the land.
Verse_Ch: 42:31 我们对他说，我们是诚实人，从来没有作过奸细。 ###EN### But we said to him, We are honest men; we have never been spies.
Verse_Ch: 42:32 我们本是弟兄十二人，都是一个父亲的儿子，有一个没有了，最小的如今同我们的父亲在迦南地。 ###EN### We are twelve brothers, sons of our father; the one is no more, and the youngest is with our father today in the land of Canaan.
Verse_Ch: 42:33 那人，那地的主，对我们说，若要我知道你们是诚实人，可以留下你们弟兄中的一个在我这里，你们带着粮食回去，救你们家里的饥荒。 ###EN### And the man, the lord of the land, said to us, By this will I know that you are honest men: Leave one of your brothers with me, and take grain for the famine of
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: your households, and go.
Verse_Ch: 42:34 把你们最小的弟弟带到我这里来，我便知道你们不是奸细，乃是诚实人。这样，我就把你们的弟兄交给你们，你们也可以在这地作买卖。 ###EN### And bring your youngest brother to me that I may know that you are not spies but are honest men. I will give you your brother, and you may trade in the land.
Verse_Ch: 42:35 后来他们倒粮袋，不料，各人的银包都在粮袋里；他们和父亲看见银包就都害怕。 ###EN### And when they emptied their sacks, there was each man's bundle of silver pieces, in his sack. And when they and their father saw their bundles of silver, they
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: were afraid.
Verse_Ch: 42:36 他们的父亲雅各对他们说，你们使我丧失我的儿子：约瑟没有了，西缅也没有了，你们又要将便雅悯带去；这些事都落到我身上了。 ###EN### And Jacob their father said to them, You have bereaved me of my children: Joseph is no more, and Simeon is no more, and you would take Benjamin; all these
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: things are against me.
Verse_Ch: 42:37 流便对他父亲说，我若不带他回来交给你，你可以杀我的两个儿子。只管把他交在我手里，我必带他回来交给你。 ###EN### And Reuben spoke to his father, saying, You may put to death my two sons if I do not bring him to you. Put him in my hand, and I will return him to you.
Verse_Ch: 42:38 雅各说，我的儿子不可与你们一同下去；他哥哥死了，只剩下他，他若在你们所行的路上遭害，那便是你们使我白发苍苍、悲悲惨惨的下阴间去了。 ###EN### But he said, My son shall not go down with you, for his brother is dead, and he alone is left. And if harm should befall him on the way in which you go, then you
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: will bring down my gray hairs in sorrow to Sheol.
Chapter_Header: 43
Verse_Ch: 43:1 那地的饥荒甚重。 ###EN### Now the famine was severe in the land.
Verse_Ch: 43:2 他们从埃及带来的粮吃尽了，他们的父亲就对他们说，你们再去给我们买一点粮食来。 ###EN### And when they had completely consumed the grain which they had brought out of Egypt, their father said to them, Go back; buy us a little food.
Verse_Ch: 43:3 但犹大对他说，那人郑重的警告我们说，你们的弟弟若不与你们同来，你们就不得见我的面。 ###EN### But Judah spoke to him, saying, The man solemnly warned us, saying, You shall not see my face unless your brother is with you.
Verse_Ch: 43:4 你若愿意打发我们的弟弟与我们同去，我们就下去给你买粮食； ###EN### If you are willing to send our brother with us, we will go down and buy you grain for food;
Verse_Ch: 43:5 你若不愿意打发他去，我们就不下去，因为那人对我们说，你们的弟弟若不与你们同来，你们就不得见我的面。 ###EN### But if you are not willing to send him, we will not go down; for the man said to us, You shall not see my face unless your brother is with you.
Verse_Ch: 43:6 以色列说，你们为什么这样害我，告诉那人你们还有弟弟呢？ ###EN### And Israel said, Why did you treat me so badly as to tell the man that you had another brother?
Verse_Ch: 43:7 他们说，那人详细的问到我们和我们的亲属，说，你们的父亲还健在么？你们还有兄弟么？我们就按着他所问的告诉他。我们怎能知道他会说，把你们的弟弟带下来呢？ ###EN### And they said, The man asked very carefully about us and about our relatives, saying, Is your father still alive? Do you have another brother? So we told him about
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: these things. Could we possibly know that he would say, Bring your brother down?
Verse_Ch: 43:8 犹大又对他父亲以色列说，你打发少年人与我同去，我们就起身下去，好叫我们和你，并我们的妇人孩子，都得存活，不至于死。 ###EN### And Judah said to Israel his father, Send the boy with me, and we will rise up and go, that we may live and not die, we and you and our little ones.
Verse_Ch: 43:9 我为他作保，你可以从我手中追讨。我若不带他回来交在你面前，我就永远在你面前担罪。 ###EN### I myself will be surety for him; of my hand you may require him. If I do not bring him to you and set him before you, then I shall bear the blame of sinning before
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: you forever.
Verse_Ch: 43:10 我们若没有耽搁，如今第二次都回来了。 ###EN### For if we had not delayed, by now we could have returned twice.
Verse_Ch: 43:11 他们的父亲以色列对他们说，若必须如此，你们就当这样行：可以取些这地佳美的出产，就是一点香油和一点蜂蜜、香胶和没药，榧子和杏仁，收在器皿里，带下去送给那人作礼物； ###EN### And their father Israel said to them, If it must be so, then do this: Take some of the choice fruits of the land in your bags, and carry a present down to the man-a
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: little balm and a little honey, aromatic gum and myrrh, pistachio nuts and almonds.
Verse_Ch: 43:12 又要手里带着加倍的银子，并要将归还在你们袋口的银子带回去；那或者是错了。 ###EN### And take double the silver in your hand, and carry back in your hand the silver that was returned in the mouth of your sacks; perhaps it was a mistake.
Verse_Ch: 43:13 也带着你们的弟弟，起身回去见那人。 ###EN### Take your brother also, and rise up. Return to the man,
Verse_Ch: 43:14 但愿全足的神在那人面前赐你们怜悯，使他释放你们的那弟兄和便雅悯回来。至于我，我若丧了儿子，就丧了罢。 ###EN### And may the All-sufficient God grant you mercy before the man, that he may release to you your other brother and Benjamin. And as for me, if I am to be
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: bereaved of my children, I shall be bereaved.
Verse_Ch: 43:15 于是，他们拿着礼物，手里带着加倍的银子，并且带着便雅悯，起身下到埃及，站在约瑟面前。 ###EN### So the men took this present, and they took double the silver in their hand and Benjamin; and they rose up and went down to Egypt and stood before Joseph.
Verse_Ch: 43:16 约瑟见便雅悯和他们同来，就对家宰说，将这些人领到屋里，要宰杀牲畜，预备筵席，因为正午这些人要同我吃饭。 ###EN### And when Joseph saw Benjamin with them, he said to him who was over his house, Bring the men into the house, and slaughter an animal, and prepare it; for
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: the men will eat with me at noon.
Verse_Ch: 43:17 家宰就遵着约瑟的命去行，领他们进约瑟的屋里。 ###EN### And the man did as Joseph said, and the man brought the men into Joseph's house.
Verse_Ch: 43:18 他们因为被领到约瑟的屋里，就害怕，说，必是因为头次归还在我们袋子里的银子，才领我们到这里来，要找机会下手害我们，强取我们作奴仆，抢夺我们的驴。 ###EN### And the men were afraid because they were brought to Joseph's house; and they said, It is because of the silver that was returned in our sacks the first time, that
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: we are being brought in, that he may come out against us and fall upon us and take us as slaves with our donkeys.
Verse_Ch: 43:19 他们就挨近约瑟的家宰，在屋门口和他说话， ###EN### And they came near to the man who was over Joseph's house and spoke to him at the door of the house,
Verse_Ch: 43:20 说，我主阿，我们头次下来实在是要买粮食。 ###EN### And said, Please, my lord, we indeed came down the first time to buy grain for food;
Verse_Ch: 43:21 后来到了住宿的地方，我们打开袋子，不料，各人的银子分量足数，仍在各人的袋口；现在我们手里又带回来了。 ###EN### And when we came to the lodging place, we opened our sacks, and there was each man's silver, in the mouth of his sack, our silver in full weight. So we have
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: brought it back in our hand.
Verse_Ch: 43:22 我们手里还另外带下银子来买粮食。我们不知道先前谁把银子放在我们的袋子里。 ###EN### And we have also brought down extra silver in our hand to buy grain for food. We do not know who put our silver in our sacks.
Verse_Ch: 43:23 家宰说，你们可以放心，不要害怕，是你们的神和你们父亲的神，赐给你们财宝在你们的袋子里；你们的银子，我早已收了。他就把西缅带出来，交给他们。 ###EN### And he said, Be at peace; do not fear. Your God and the God of your father has given you treasure in your sacks; your silver came to me. Then he brought Simeon
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: out to them.
Verse_Ch: 43:24 家宰就领他们进约瑟的屋里，给他们水洗脚，又给他们饲粮喂驴。 ###EN### And the man brought the men into Joseph's house and gave them water, and they washed their feet; and he gave their donkeys fodder.
Verse_Ch: 43:25 他们就预备礼物，等候约瑟正午来，因为他们听见要在那里吃饭。 ###EN### And they prepared the present for Joseph's coming at noon, for they had heard that they would eat a meal there.
Verse_Ch: 43:26 约瑟来到家里，他们就把手中的礼物拿进屋去给他，又俯伏在地，向他下拜。 ###EN### And when Joseph came into the house, they brought him the present which was in their hand into the house and bowed down to the ground to him.
Verse_Ch: 43:27 约瑟问他们安，又说，你们的父亲，就是你们所说的那老人家平安么？他还健在么？ ###EN### And he asked them about their welfare and said, Is your father well, the old man of whom you spoke? Is he still alive?
Verse_Ch: 43:28 他们回答说，你仆人我们的父亲平安；他还健在。于是他们低头下拜。 ###EN### And they said, Your servant our father is well; he is still alive. And they bowed and paid him homage.
Verse_Ch: 43:29 约瑟举目看见他同母的弟弟便雅悯，就说，你们向我所说那最小的弟弟，就是这位么？又说，小儿阿，愿神赐恩给你。 ###EN### And he lifted up his eyes and saw his brother Benjamin, his mother's son, and said, Is this your youngest brother, of whom you spoke to me? And he said, God
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: be gracious to you, my son.
Verse_Ch: 43:30 约瑟爱弟之情发动，就急忙寻找可哭之处，进入自己的内室，哭了一场。 ###EN### And Joseph hurried-for his inward parts burned for his brother-and sought a place to weep. So he entered into his chamber and wept there.
Verse_Ch: 43:31 他洗了脸出来，勉强忍住，吩咐人摆饭。 ###EN### Then he washed his face and came out, and he controlled himself and said, Serve the meal.
Verse_Ch: 43:32 他们就为约瑟单摆了一席，为那些人又摆了一席，也为和约瑟同吃饭的埃及人另摆了一席，因为埃及人不可和希伯来人一同吃饭；那原是埃及人所厌恶的。 ###EN### And they served him by himself, and them by themselves, and the Egyptians who ate with him by themselves, because the Egyptians could not eat a meal with
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: the Hebrews, for that is an abomination to the Egyptians.
Verse_Ch: 43:33 约瑟使众弟兄在他面前坐席，都按着长幼的次序，众弟兄就彼此惊奇相看。 ###EN### And they sat before him, the firstborn according to his birthright and the youngest according to his youth, and the men looked at one another in astonishment.
Verse_Ch: 43:34 约瑟把他面前的食物分出来，送给他们；但便雅悯所得的分，比别人多五倍。他们就饮酒，和约瑟一同宴乐。 ###EN### And he had portions brought to them from before him; however Benjamin's portion was five times as much as any of theirs. And they drank and were merry with
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: him.
Chapter_Header: 44
Verse_Ch: 44:1 约瑟吩咐家宰说，把粮食装满这些人的袋子，尽他们所能带的，又把各人的银子放在各人的袋口； ###EN### And he commanded him who was over his house, saying, Fill the men's sacks with food, as much as they can carry, and put each man's silver in the mouth of his
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: sack.
Verse_Ch: 44:2 并将我的银杯，和那最年幼的买粮的银子，一同装在他的袋口。家宰就照约瑟所说的话行了。 ###EN### And put my cup, the silver cup, in the mouth of the sack of the youngest with his silver for the grain. And he did so, according to the word that Joseph had spoken.
Verse_Ch: 44:3 早晨天一亮，就打发那些人带着驴走了。 ###EN### As soon as the morning was light, the men were sent away, they and their donkeys.
Verse_Ch: 44:4 他们出城走了不远，约瑟对家宰说，起来，追那些人去，追上了就对他们说，你们为什么以恶报善？ ###EN### When they had just gone out of the city and were not yet far off, Joseph said to him who was over his house, Rise up, follow after the men; and when you
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: overtake them, say to them, Why have you repaid evil for good?
Verse_Ch: 44:5 这不是我主人饮酒的杯么？岂不是他占卜用的么？你们这样行是作恶了。 ###EN### Is not this that from which my lord drinks, and which he indeed uses for divining? You have done wrong in so doing.
Verse_Ch: 44:6 家宰追上他们，将这些话对他们说了。 ###EN### And he overtook them and spoke these words to them.
Verse_Ch: 44:7 他们回答说，我主为什么说这样的话？你仆人断不会作这样的事。 ###EN### And they said to him, Why does my lord speak such words as these? Far be it from your servants to do such a thing.
Verse_Ch: 44:8 你看，我们从前在袋口里所发现的银子，尚且从迦南地带来还你，我们怎能从你主人家里偷窃金银呢？ ###EN### See how we brought back to you the silver which we found in the mouth of our sacks from the land of Canaan. How then could we steal silver or gold out of your
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: lord's house?
Verse_Ch: 44:9 在你仆人中，无论从谁那里搜出来，就叫他死，我们也作我主的奴仆。 ###EN### With whomever of your servants it is found, let him die; and we ourselves will become my lord's slaves.
Verse_Ch: 44:10 家宰说，现在就照你们的话行罢。从谁那里搜出来，谁就作我的奴仆，你们其余的都没有罪。 ###EN### And he said, Now also let it be according to your words: He with whom it is found will be my slave; and the rest of you will be blameless.
Verse_Ch: 44:11 于是他们各人急忙把袋子卸在地上，各人打开自己的袋子。 ###EN### Then each man hurried and lowered his sack to the ground, and each man opened his sack.
Verse_Ch: 44:12 家宰就搜查，从最年长的起，到最年幼的为止，那杯竟在便雅悯的袋子里搜出来。 ###EN### And he searched, beginning with the oldest and ending with the youngest; and the cup was found in Benjamin's sack.
Verse_Ch: 44:13 他们就撕裂衣服，各人把驮子抬在驴上，回城去了。 ###EN### Then they tore their garments, and each man loaded his donkey, and they returned to the city.
Verse_Ch: 44:14 犹大和他弟兄们来到约瑟的屋中，约瑟还在那里，他们就在他面前俯伏于地。 ###EN### And Judah and his brothers came to Joseph's house, and he was still there; and they fell to the ground before him.
Verse_Ch: 44:15 约瑟对他们说，你们作的是什么事？你们岂不知像我这样的人必能占卜么？ ###EN### And Joseph said to them, What deed is this that you have done? Do you not know that such a man as I can indeed divine?
Verse_Ch: 44:16 犹大说，我们能对我主说什么？还能说什么呢？我们怎能表白自己？神已经查出你仆人们的罪孽了。我们与那在他手中搜出杯来的，都是我主的奴仆。 ###EN### And Judah said, What can we say to my lord? What can we speak? And how can we justify ourselves? God has found out the iniquity of your servants. Here we
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: are, my lord's slaves, both we and the one in whose hand the cup has been found.
Verse_Ch: 44:17 约瑟说，我断不能这样行。在谁的手中搜出杯来，谁就作我的奴仆；至于你们其余的人，可以平平安安的上你们父亲那里去。 ###EN### But he said, Far be it from me to do this. The man in whose hand the cup has been found, he will be my slave; but as for the rest of you, go up in peace to your
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: father.
Verse_Ch: 44:18 犹大挨近他，说，我主阿，求你让仆人说一句话给我主听，不要向仆人发烈怒，因为你如同法老一样。 ###EN### Then Judah came near to him and said, Please, my lord, let your servant speak a word in my lord's ears, and let not your anger burn against your servant; for you
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: are even as Pharaoh.
Verse_Ch: 44:19 我主曾问仆人们说，你们有父亲、有兄弟没有？ ###EN### My lord asked his servants, saying, Do you have a father or a brother?
Verse_Ch: 44:20 我们对我主说，我们有年老的父亲，还有他老年所生的一个小孩子。他哥哥死了，他母亲只撇下他一个人，他父亲疼爱他。 ###EN### And we said to my lord, We have an old father and a young child of his old age; and his brother is dead, and he alone is left of his mother, and his father loves
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: him.
Verse_Ch: 44:21 你对仆人们说，把他带下来到我这里，叫我可以亲眼看看他。 ###EN### And you said to your servants, Bring him down to me, that I may set my eyes on him.
Verse_Ch: 44:22 我们对我主说，少年人不能离开他父亲，若是离开，他父亲必会死。 ###EN### And we said to my lord, The boy cannot leave his father; for if he should leave his father, his father would die.
Verse_Ch: 44:23 你对仆人说，你们最小的弟弟若不与你们一同下来，你们就不得再见我的面。 ###EN### And you said to your servants, Unless your youngest brother comes down with you, you shall see my face no more.
Verse_Ch: 44:24 我们上到你仆人我们父亲那里，就把我主的话告诉了他。 ###EN### And when we went up to your servant my father, we told him my lord's words.
Verse_Ch: 44:25 我们的父亲说，你们再去给我们买一点粮食来。 ###EN### And our father said, Return, buy us a little food.
Verse_Ch: 44:26 但我们说，我们不能下去。我们最小的弟弟若与我们同往，我们就下去。因为最小的弟弟若不与我们同往，我们必不得见那人的面。 ###EN### But we said, We cannot go down. If our youngest brother is with us, we will go down; for we cannot see the man's face unless our youngest brother is with us.
Verse_Ch: 44:27 你仆人我父亲对我们说，你们知道我的妻子给我生了两个儿子。 ###EN### And your servant my father said to us, You know that my wife bore me two sons;
Verse_Ch: 44:28 一个离开我去了，我说他必是被撕碎了，直到如今我没有见到他。 ###EN### And the one went away from me, and I said, Surely he has been torn to pieces; and I have not seen him to this day.
Verse_Ch: 44:29 现在你们又要把这个带去离开我，倘若他遭害，那便是你们使我白发苍苍、悲悲惨惨的下阴间去了。 ###EN### And if you take this one also from me and harm befalls him, you will bring down my gray hairs in misery to Sheol.
Verse_Ch: 44:30 我父亲的命与这少年人的命相连。如今我回到你仆人我父亲那里，若没有少年人与我们同在， ###EN### Now therefore when I come to your servant my father, and the boy is not with us, and his life being bound up in the boy's life,
Verse_Ch: 44:31 我们的父亲见没有少年人，他就必死。这便是我们使你仆人我们的父亲白发苍苍、悲悲惨惨的下阴间去了。 ###EN### When he sees that the boy is not with us, he will die; and your servants will bring down the gray hairs of your servant our father in sorrow to Sheol.
Verse_Ch: 44:32 因为仆人曾向我父亲为这少年人作保，说，我若不带他回来交给你，我便永远在父亲面前担罪。 ###EN### For your servant became surety for the lad to my father, saying, If I do not bring him to you, then I shall bear the blame of sinning before my father forever.
Verse_Ch: 44:33 现在求你让仆人留下，替这少年人作我主的奴仆，叫他和哥哥们一同上去。 ###EN### Now therefore, please let your servant remain as a slave to my lord instead of the boy, and let the boy go up with his brothers.
Verse_Ch: 44:34 若这少年人不和我同去，我怎能上去见我父亲？我怕看见灾祸临到我父亲身上。 ###EN### For how shall I go up to my father if the boy is not with me? I fear to see the evil that would come on my father.
Chapter_Header: 45
Verse_Ch: 45:1 约瑟在左右侍立的人面前情不自禁，大声吩咐说，各人都要离开我出去！约瑟和他弟兄们相认的时候，并没有一个人站在他身边。 ###EN### Then Joseph could not control himself before all those who attended him; and he cried out, Have everyone go out from me. So there was no one standing with
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: him when Joseph made himself known to his brothers.
Verse_Ch: 45:2 他就放声大哭，埃及人和法老家中的人都听见了。 ###EN### And he wept so loudly that the Egyptians heard it, and the household of Pharaoh heard it.
Verse_Ch: 45:3 约瑟对他弟兄们说，我是约瑟；我的父亲还健在么？他弟兄们不能回答，因为在他面前都甚惊惶。 ###EN### And Joseph said to his brothers, I am Joseph! Is my father still alive? But his brothers could not answer him, so troubled were they at his presence.
Verse_Ch: 45:4 约瑟又对他弟兄们说，请你们近前到我这里来。他们就近前来。他说，我是你们的弟兄约瑟，就是你们所卖到埃及的。 ###EN### And Joseph said to his brothers, Please come closer to me. And they came closer. And he said, I am your brother Joseph, whom you sold into Egypt.
Verse_Ch: 45:5 现在，不要因为你们把我卖到这里，自忧自恨。这是神差我在你们以先来，为要保全生命。 ###EN### And now do not be grieved or angry with yourselves because you sold me here, for God sent me before you to preserve life.
Verse_Ch: 45:6 现在这地的饥荒已经二年了，并且还有五年不能耕种，不能收成。 ###EN### For the famine has been in the midst of the land these two years, and there are still five years in which there will be neither plowing nor harvest.
Verse_Ch: 45:7 神差我在你们以先来，为要给你们存留余种在地上，又要大施拯救，使你们存活。 ###EN### And God sent me before you to preserve for you a remnant in the earth and to keep you alive by a great deliverance.
Verse_Ch: 45:8 这样看来，差我到这里来的不是你们，乃是神。祂又立我作法老的父，作他全家的主，并埃及全地的统治者。 ###EN### So now it was not you who sent me here, but God; and He has made me a father to Pharaoh and lord of all his house and ruler over all the land of Egypt.
Verse_Ch: 45:9 你们要赶紧上到我父亲那里，对他说，你的儿子约瑟这样说：神使我作全埃及的主，请你下到我这里来，不要耽延。 ###EN### Hurry and go up to my father, and say to him, Thus says your son Joseph, God has made me lord of all Egypt; come down to me; do not delay.
Verse_Ch: 45:10 你和你的儿子、孙子，连牛群、羊群，并一切所有的，都可以住在歌珊地，与我相近。 ###EN### And you shall dwell in the land of Goshen and be near to me, you and your children and your children's children and your flocks and your herds and all that you
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: have.
Verse_Ch: 45:11 我要在那里奉养你；因为还有五年的饥荒，免得你和你的眷属，并一切所有的，都穷乏了。 ###EN### And there I will sustain you-for there are still five years of famine to come-so that you and your household and all that you have do not become impoverished.
Verse_Ch: 45:12 况且你们的眼和我弟弟便雅悯的眼都看见，是我亲口对你们说话。 ###EN### And now your eyes see, and the eyes of my brother Benjamin see, that it is my own mouth that speaks to you.
Verse_Ch: 45:13 你们也要将我在埃及一切的荣耀，和你们所看见一切的事，都告诉我父亲，又要赶紧将我父亲搬到这里来。 ###EN### And you must tell my father of all my glory in Egypt and of all that you have seen, and you must hurry and bring my father down here.
Verse_Ch: 45:14 于是约瑟伏在他弟弟便雅悯的颈项上哭，便雅悯也在他的颈项上哭。 ###EN### And he fell upon his brother Benjamin's neck and wept, and Benjamin wept upon his neck.
Verse_Ch: 45:15 他又与众弟兄亲嘴，抱着他们哭，随后他弟兄们就和他说话。 ###EN### And he kissed all his brothers and wept upon them, and after that his brothers talked with him.
Verse_Ch: 45:16 这风声传到法老的宫里，说，约瑟的弟兄们来了。法老和他的臣仆都很喜欢。 ###EN### And when the report was heard in Pharaoh's house, saying, Joseph's brothers have come, it was pleasing to Pharaoh and to his servants.
Verse_Ch: 45:17 法老对约瑟说，你吩咐你的弟兄们说，你们要这样行：把驮子抬在牲口上，起程往迦南地去。 ###EN### And Pharaoh said to Joseph, Say to your brothers, Do this: Load your beasts, and depart; go to the land of Canaan;
Verse_Ch: 45:18 将你们的父亲和你们的眷属，都搬到我这里来，我要把埃及最好的地赐给你们，你们也要吃这地肥美的出产。 ###EN### And take your father and your households, and come to me; and I will give you the best of the land of Egypt, and you will eat the fat of the land.
Verse_Ch: 45:19 现在我吩咐你们要这样行：从埃及地带着车辆去，接你们的孩子和妻子，并把你们的父亲载来。 ###EN### And you are commanded, Do this: Take wagons out of the land of Egypt for your little ones and for your wives; and bring your father, and come.
Verse_Ch: 45:20 你们眼中不要顾惜你们的物件，因为埃及全地的美物都是你们的。 ###EN### And do not be concerned for your possessions, for the best of all the land of Egypt is yours.
Verse_Ch: 45:21 以色列的儿子们就如此行。约瑟照着法老的吩咐给他们车辆，和路上用的食物。 ###EN### And the sons of Israel did so, and Joseph gave them wagons according to the command of Pharaoh and gave them provisions for the way.
Verse_Ch: 45:22 又给他们各人一套衣服，惟独给便雅悯三百锭银子，五套衣服； ###EN### To each of them he gave changes of garments; but to Benjamin he gave three hundred pieces of silver and five changes of garments.
