Verse_Ch: 45:23 送给他父亲公驴十匹，驮着埃及的美物；母驴十匹，驮着谷物、饼、和其他食物，为他父亲路上用。 ###EN### And he sent to his father the following: ten donkeys loaded with the best of Egypt, and ten female donkeys loaded with grain and bread and provision for his
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: father on the way.
Verse_Ch: 45:24 于是约瑟打发他弟兄们回去；他们走的时候，约瑟对他们说，你们在路上不要相争。 ###EN### So he sent his brothers away; and as they departed, he said to them, Do not quarrel on the way.
Verse_Ch: 45:25 他们从埃及上去，来到迦南地，他们的父亲雅各那里， ###EN### So they went up out of Egypt and came to the land of Canaan to Jacob their father.
Verse_Ch: 45:26 告诉他说，约瑟还在，并且作了埃及全地的统治者。雅各心里麻木，因为不信他们。 ###EN### And they told him, saying, Joseph is still alive, and he is ruler over all the land of Egypt. And his heart became numb, for he did not believe them.
Verse_Ch: 45:27 他们便将约瑟对他们说的一切话，都告诉了他；他们父亲雅各又看见约瑟打发来接他的车辆，灵就苏醒了。 ###EN### And they told him all the words of Joseph, which he had said to them; and when he saw the wagons which Joseph had sent to carry him, the spirit of Jacob their
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: father revived.
Verse_Ch: 45:28 以色列说，罢了！罢了！我的儿子约瑟还在，我要趁着未死以先，去见他一面。 ###EN### And Israel said, It is enough. Joseph my son is still alive. I will go and see him before I die.
Chapter_Header: 46
Verse_Ch: 46:1 以色列带着一切所有的，起行来到别是巴，就献祭给他父亲以撒的神。 ###EN### So Israel set out with all that he had and came to Beer-sheba and offered sacrifices to the God of his father Isaac.
Verse_Ch: 46:2 神在夜间的异象中对以色列说，雅各，雅各。他说，我在这里。 ###EN### And God spoke to Israel in the visions of the night and said, Jacob, Jacob. And he said, Here I am.
Verse_Ch: 46:3 神说，我是神，就是你父亲的神；你下埃及去不要害怕，因为我必使你在那里成为大国。 ###EN### And He said, I am God, the God of your father; do not be afraid to go down to Egypt, for I will make of you a great nation there.
Verse_Ch: 46:4 我要亲自同你下埃及去，也必定亲自再带你上来；约瑟必给你送终。 ###EN### I Myself will go down with you to Egypt, and I Myself will also surely bring you up again; and Joseph's hand will close your eyes.
Verse_Ch: 46:5 雅各就从别是巴起身。以色列的儿子们使他们的父亲雅各、和他们的孩子、妻子，都坐上法老所送来载雅各的车。 ###EN### And Jacob rose up from Beer-sheba, and the sons of Israel carried Jacob their father and their little ones and their wives in the wagons which Pharaoh had sent
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: to carry him.
Verse_Ch: 46:6 他们又带着在迦南地所得的牲畜、财物来到埃及，雅各和他的一切子孙都一同来了。 ###EN### And they took their livestock and their possessions, which they had acquired in the land of Canaan, and Jacob and all his offspring with him came to Egypt.
Verse_Ch: 46:7 雅各把他的儿子和孙子，女儿和孙女，他的一切子孙，一同带到埃及。 ###EN### His sons and his grandsons with him, his daughters and his granddaughters, and all his offspring he brought with him to Egypt.
Verse_Ch: 46:8 来到埃及的以色列人，就是雅各和他的子孙，名字记在下面：雅各的长子是流便。 ###EN### And these are the names of the children of Israel, who came to Egypt, Jacob and his sons: Jacob's firstborn, Reuben.
Verse_Ch: 46:9 流便的儿子是哈诺、法路、希斯伦、迦米。 ###EN### And the sons of Reuben: Hanoch and Pallu and Hezron and Carmi.
Verse_Ch: 46:10 西缅的儿子是耶母利、雅悯、阿辖、雅斤、琐辖，还有迦南女子所生的扫罗。 ###EN### And the sons of Simeon: Jemuel and Jamin and Ohad and Jachin and Zohar and Shaul the son of a Canaanite woman.
Verse_Ch: 46:11 利未的儿子是革顺、哥辖、米拉利。 ###EN### And the sons of Levi: Gershon, Kohath, and Merari.
Verse_Ch: 46:12 犹大的儿子是珥、俄南、示拉、法勒斯、谢拉；只是珥与俄南死在迦南地。法勒斯的儿子是希斯伦、哈母勒。 ###EN### And the sons of Judah: Er and Onan and Shelah and Perez and Zerah; but Er and Onan died in the land of Canaan. And the sons of Perez were Hezron and
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: Hamul.
Verse_Ch: 46:13 以萨迦的儿子是陀拉、普瓦、约伯、伸仑。 ###EN### And the sons of Issachar: Tola and Puvah and Iob and Shimron.
Verse_Ch: 46:14 西布伦的儿子是西烈、以伦、雅利。 ###EN### And the sons of Zebulun: Sered and Elon and Jahleel.
Verse_Ch: 46:15 这些是利亚在巴旦亚兰给雅各所生的儿子，还有女儿底拿。儿孙共三十三人。 ###EN### These are the sons of Leah, whom she bore to Jacob in Paddan-aram, along with his daughter Dinah. His sons and his daughters were thirty-three persons in
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: all.
Verse_Ch: 46:16 迦得的儿子是洗非芸、哈基、书尼、以斯本、以利、亚罗底、亚列利。 ###EN### And the sons of Gad: Ziphion and Haggi, Shuni and Ezbon, Eri and Arodi and Areli.
Verse_Ch: 46:17 亚设的儿子是音拿、亦施瓦、亦施韦、比利亚，还有他们的妹妹西拉。比利亚的儿子是希别、玛结。 ###EN### And the sons of Asher: Imnah and Ishvah and Ishvi and Beriah, and Serah their sister; and the sons of Beriah: Heber and Malchiel.
Verse_Ch: 46:18 这些是拉班给他女儿利亚的婢女悉帕，从雅各所生的儿孙，共有十六人。 ###EN### These are the sons of Zilpah, whom Laban gave to his daughter Leah; and she bore these to Jacob, sixteen persons.
Verse_Ch: 46:19 雅各之妻拉结的儿子是约瑟和便雅悯。 ###EN### The sons of Rachel, Jacob's wife: Joseph and Benjamin.
Verse_Ch: 46:20 约瑟在埃及地生了玛拿西和以法莲，他们是安城的祭司波提非拉的女儿亚西纳给约瑟生的。 ###EN### And to Joseph in the land of Egypt were born Manasseh and Ephraim, whom Asenath the daughter of Potiphera priest of On bore to him.
Verse_Ch: 46:21 便雅悯的儿子是比拉、比结、亚实别、基拉、乃幔、以希、罗实、母平、户平、亚勒。 ###EN### And the sons of Benjamin: Bela and Becher and Ashbel, Gera and Naaman, Ehi and Rosh, Muppim and Huppim and Ard.
Verse_Ch: 46:22 这些是拉结给雅各所生的儿孙，共有十四人。 ###EN### These are the sons of Rachel, who were born to Jacob, fourteen persons in all.
Verse_Ch: 46:23 但的儿子是户伸。 ###EN### And the sons of Dan: Hushim.
Verse_Ch: 46:24 拿弗他利的儿子是雅薛、沽尼、耶色、示冷。 ###EN### And the sons of Naphtali: Jahzeel and Guni and Jezer and Shillem.
Verse_Ch: 46:25 这些是拉班给他女儿拉结的婢女辟拉，从雅各所生的儿孙，共有七人。 ###EN### These are the sons of Bilhah, whom Laban gave to Rachel his daughter, and she bore these to Jacob, seven persons in all.
Verse_Ch: 46:26 那与雅各同到埃及的除了他儿媳之外，凡从他所生的共有六十六人。 ###EN### All the persons who came with Jacob into Egypt, who came out of his loins, besides the wives of Jacob's sons, were sixty-six persons in all.
Verse_Ch: 46:27 还有约瑟在埃及所生的儿子，共二人。雅各家来到埃及的，共有七十人。 ###EN### And the sons of Joseph, who were born to him in Egypt, were two persons. All the persons of the house of Jacob, who came to Egypt, were seventy.
Verse_Ch: 46:28 雅各打发犹大先去见约瑟，请派人引路往歌珊去；于是他们来到歌珊地。 ###EN### And he sent Judah before him to Joseph to show the way before him to Goshen, and they came to the land of Goshen.
Verse_Ch: 46:29 约瑟套车上歌珊去，迎接他父亲以色列；等到见了面，就伏在父亲的颈项上哭了许久。 ###EN### And Joseph made his chariot ready and went up to Goshen to meet Israel his father. And when he appeared before him, he fell on his neck and wept on his neck
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: a good while.
Verse_Ch: 46:30 以色列对约瑟说，我既得见你的面，知道你还在，就是死我也甘心。 ###EN### And Israel said to Joseph, Let me die now since I have seen your face and know that you are still alive.
Verse_Ch: 46:31 约瑟对他的弟兄们和他父的全家说，我要上去告诉法老，对他说，我的弟兄们和我父的全家，从前在迦南地，现今都到我这里来了。 ###EN### And Joseph said to his brothers and to his father's household, I will go up and tell Pharaoh, and will say to him, My brothers and my father's household, who
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: were in the land of Canaan, have come to me.
Verse_Ch: 46:32 他们本是牧羊的人，以养牲畜为业；他们把羊群、牛群和一切所有的，都带来了。 ###EN### And the men are shepherds, for they have been keepers of livestock; and they have brought their flocks and their herds and all that they have.
Verse_Ch: 46:33 等法老召你们的时候，问你们说，你们以何事为业？ ###EN### And when Pharaoh calls you and says, What is your occupation?
Verse_Ch: 46:34 你们要说，你的仆人们从幼年直到如今，都以养牲畜为业，我们和我们的祖宗都是如此。这样，你们就可以住在歌珊地，因为凡牧羊的都被埃及人所厌恶。 ###EN### You shall say, Your servants have been keepers of livestock from our youth even until now, both we and our fathers; that you may dwell in the land of Goshen, for
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: every shepherd is an abomination to the Egyptians.
Chapter_Header: 47
Verse_Ch: 47:1 约瑟进去告诉法老说，我的父亲和我的弟兄们带着羊群、牛群、并一切所有的，从迦南地来了，如今在歌珊地。 ###EN### Then Joseph went in and told Pharaoh and said, My father and my brothers and their flocks and their herds and all that they have, have come out of the land of
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: Canaan; and now they are in the land of Goshen.
Verse_Ch: 47:2 约瑟从他众弟兄中挑出五个人来，引他们去见法老。 ###EN### And he took five men from among his brothers and presented them to Pharaoh.
Verse_Ch: 47:3 法老问约瑟的弟兄们说，你们以何事为业？他们对法老说，你仆人们是牧羊的，我们和我们的祖宗都是如此。 ###EN### And Pharaoh said to his brothers, What is your occupation? And they said to Pharaoh, Your servants are shepherds, both we and our fathers.
Verse_Ch: 47:4 他们又对法老说，迦南地的饥荒甚重，那里没有草场供应你仆人们的羊群，所以我们来到这地寄居。现在求你让仆人们住在歌珊地。 ###EN### And they said to Pharaoh, We have come to sojourn in the land because there is no pasture for your servants' flocks, for the famine is severe in the land of
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: Canaan. Now therefore, please let your servants dwell in the land of Goshen.
Verse_Ch: 47:5 法老对约瑟说，你父亲和你弟兄们到你这里来了。 ###EN### And Pharaoh spoke to Joseph, saying, Your father and your brothers have come to you.
Verse_Ch: 47:6 埃及地都在你面前，只管叫你父亲和你弟兄们住在最好的地；他们可以住在歌珊地。你若知道他们中间有什么能干的人，就派他们看管我的牲畜。 ###EN### The land of Egypt is before you; settle your father and your brothers in the best of the land; let them dwell in the land of Goshen. And if you know any capable
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: men among them, make them overseers over my livestock.
Verse_Ch: 47:7 约瑟领他父亲雅各进去，站在法老面前， ###EN### And Joseph brought in Jacob his father and set him before Pharaoh, and Jacob blessed Pharaoh.
Verse_Ch: 47:8 雅各就给法老祝福。法老问雅各说，你平生的年日是多少呢？ ###EN### And Pharaoh said to Jacob, How many are the years of your life?
Verse_Ch: 47:9 雅各对法老说，我寄居在世的年日是一百三十岁；我平生的年日又少又苦，不及我列祖在世寄居的年日。 ###EN### And Jacob said to Pharaoh, The years of my sojourning are one hundred thirty years; few and evil have been the years of my life, and they have not attained to
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: the years of the lives of my fathers during the days of their sojourning.
Verse_Ch: 47:10 雅各又给法老祝福，就从法老面前出去了。 ###EN### And Jacob blessed Pharaoh and went forth from Pharaoh's presence.
Verse_Ch: 47:11 约瑟遵着法老的命，叫他父亲和弟兄们住下，将埃及境内最好的地，就是兰塞地，给他们作为产业。 ###EN### And Joseph settled his father and his brothers and gave them a possession in the land of Egypt, in the best of the land, in the land of Rameses, as Pharaoh had
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: commanded.
Verse_Ch: 47:12 约瑟用粮食供养他父亲和他弟兄们，并他父亲全家的眷属，都是照各家的人口供养他们。 ###EN### And Joseph sustained his father and his brothers and all his father's household with food according to the number of their little ones.
Verse_Ch: 47:13 全地都绝了粮，因为饥荒极重，以致埃及地和迦南地因饥荒的缘故，都凋萎了。 ###EN### And there was no food in all the land, for the famine was so very severe that the land of Egypt and the land of Canaan languished because of the famine.
Verse_Ch: 47:14 约瑟收聚了埃及地和迦南地所有的银子，就是众人买粮的银子；约瑟就把那银子带到法老的宫里。 ###EN### And Joseph collected all the money that was to be found in the land of Egypt and in the land of Canaan for the grain which they bought, and Joseph brought the
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: money into Pharaoh's house.
Verse_Ch: 47:15 埃及地和迦南地的银子都花尽了，埃及众人都来见约瑟，说，我们的银子都用尽了，求你给我们粮食，我们为什么要死在你面前呢？ ###EN### And when the money from the land of Egypt and from the land of Canaan had been spent, all the Egyptians came to Joseph saying, Give us food, for why should
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: we die in your presence? For our money is gone.
Verse_Ch: 47:16 约瑟说，若是银子用尽了，可以把你们的牲畜带来，我就给你们粮食，来换你们的牲畜。 ###EN### And Joseph said, Bring your livestock, and I will give you food in exchange for your livestock, if your money is gone.
Verse_Ch: 47:17 于是他们把牲畜赶到约瑟那里，约瑟就拿粮食换了他们的马、羊群、牛群和驴；那一年因换他们一切的牲畜，就用粮食养活他们。 ###EN### And they brought their livestock to Joseph, and Joseph gave them food in exchange for the horses and for the flocks of sheep and for the herds of cattle and for
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: the donkeys; and he fed them with food in exchange for all their livestock that year.
Verse_Ch: 47:18 那一年过去，第二年他们又来见约瑟，说，我们不瞒我主，我们的银子都花尽了，牲畜也都归了我主。我们在我主眼前，除了我们的身体和田地之外，一无所剩。 ###EN### And when that year had ended, they came to him the second year and said to him, We cannot hide from my lord that our money has been spent, and the herds
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: of cattle are my lord's. There is nothing left in the sight of my lord except our bodies and our lands.
Verse_Ch: 47:19 我们为什么要在你面前人死地荒呢？求你用粮食买我们和我们的地，我们和我们的地就要给法老效力；并且求你给我们种子，使我们得以存活，不至死亡，地土也不至荒凉。 ###EN### Why should we die before your eyes, both we and our land? Buy us and our land in exchange for food, and we and our land will become servants to Pharaoh.
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: And give us seed that we may live and not die, and that the land may not be desolate.
Verse_Ch: 47:20 于是约瑟为法老买了埃及所有的地；埃及人因被饥荒所迫，各都卖了自己的田地；那地就都归了法老。 ###EN### So Joseph bought all the land of Egypt for Pharaoh; for every Egyptian sold his field, because the famine was severe upon them; and the land became Pharaoh's.
Verse_Ch: 47:21 至于百姓，约瑟叫他们从埃及境内的这边直到那边，都迁移到各城里。 ###EN### And as for the people, he removed them to the cities from one end of the border of Egypt even to the other end.
Verse_Ch: 47:22 惟有祭司的地，约瑟没有买，因为祭司有从法老所得的常俸。他们吃法老所给的常俸，所以他们不卖自己的地。 ###EN### Only the land of the priests he did not buy, for the priests had an assigned portion from Pharaoh, and they lived off their portion which Pharaoh gave them;
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: therefore they did not sell their land.
Verse_Ch: 47:23 那时约瑟对百姓说，看哪，我今日为法老买了你们和你们的地；这里有种子给你们，你们可以种地。 ###EN### Then Joseph said to the people, Now that I have this day bought you and your land for Pharaoh, here is seed for you that you may sow the land.
Verse_Ch: 47:24 到收割的时候，你们要把五分之一纳给法老，五分之四可以归你们自己作田地里的种子，也作你们、你们家人和孩童的食物。 ###EN### And when harvest comes, you shall give a fifth to Pharaoh, and four-fifths shall be your own as seed of the field and as food for you and for those of your
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: households and as food for your little ones.
Verse_Ch: 47:25 他们说，你救了我们的性命。但愿我们在我主眼前蒙恩，我们就作法老的仆人。 ###EN### And they said, You have saved our lives. May we find favor in the sight of my lord and be Pharaoh's servants.
Verse_Ch: 47:26 于是约瑟为埃及的地立下定例，直到今日：法老必得五分之一，惟独祭司的地不归法老。 ###EN### And Joseph made it a statute concerning the land of Egypt that stands to this day, that Pharaoh should have the fifth; only the land of the priests alone did not
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: become Pharaoh's.
Verse_Ch: 47:27 以色列人住在埃及的歌珊地；他们在那里置了产业，并且极其繁衍增多。 ###EN### And Israel dwelt in the land of Egypt, in the land of Goshen; and they acquired possessions in it and were fruitful and multiplied exceedingly.
Verse_Ch: 47:28 雅各住在埃及地十七年，雅各平生的年日是一百四十七岁。 ###EN### And Jacob lived in the land of Egypt seventeen years. Thus the days of Jacob, the years of his life, were one hundred forty-seven years.
Verse_Ch: 47:29 以色列的死期临近了，他就叫了他儿子约瑟来，说，我若在你眼前蒙恩，请你把手放在我大腿下起誓；用恩慈和诚信待我，请你不要将我葬在埃及。 ###EN### And the time for Israel to die drew near. And he called his son Joseph and said to him, If now I have found favor in your sight, please put your hand under my
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: thigh and deal with me in kindness and truth; please do not bury me in Egypt.
Verse_Ch: 47:30 我与我祖我父同睡的时候，你要将我带出埃及，葬在他们所葬的地方。约瑟说，我必遵着你的话而行。 ###EN### But when I lie down with my fathers, you shall carry me out of Egypt, and bury me in their burial place. And he said, I will do as you have said.
Verse_Ch: 47:31 雅各说，你要向我起誓。约瑟就向他起了誓，于是以色列在床头上敬拜神。 ###EN### And he said, Swear to me; and he swore to him. Then Israel bowed himself at the head of his bed.
Chapter_Header: 48
Verse_Ch: 48:1 这些事以后，有人告诉约瑟说，你的父亲病了。他就带着两个儿子玛拿西和以法莲同去。 ###EN### Now after these things Joseph was told, Your father is now sick. So he took with him his two sons, Manasseh and Ephraim.
Verse_Ch: 48:2 有人告诉雅各说，请看，你儿子约瑟到你这里来了。以色列就勉强在床上坐起来。 ###EN### And someone told Jacob and said, Your son Joseph is now coming to you. So Israel strengthened himself and sat up on his bed.
Verse_Ch: 48:3 雅各对约瑟说，全足的神曾在迦南地的路斯向我显现，赐福与我， ###EN### And Jacob said to Joseph, The All-sufficient God appeared to me at Luz in the land of Canaan and blessed me.
Verse_Ch: 48:4 对我说，我必使你繁衍增多，成为多族，又要把这地赐给你的后裔，永远为业。 ###EN### And He said to me, Behold, I am going to make you fruitful and multiply you, and I will make of you a company of peoples and will give this land to your seed
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: after you for an everlasting possession.
Verse_Ch: 48:5 我未到埃及见你之前，你在埃及地所生的两个儿子是我的；以法莲和玛拿西是我的，正如流便和西缅是我的一样。 ###EN### And now your two sons, who were born to you in the land of Egypt before I came to you in Egypt, are mine; Ephraim and Manasseh will be mine, as Reuben and
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: Simeon are.
Verse_Ch: 48:6 你在他们以后所生的就是你的，他们可以归于他们哥哥们的名下承继产业。 ###EN### And your offspring whom you beget after them will be yours; they will be called by the name of their brothers in their inheritance.
Verse_Ch: 48:7 至于我，我从巴旦来的时候，在迦南地的路上，离以法他还有一段路程，拉结在我悲痛中死了；我就把她葬在通往以法他的路旁(以法他就是伯利恒。) ###EN### And as for me, when I came from Paddan, Rachel died to my sorrow in the land of Canaan on the way, while there was still some distance to go to Ephrath; and I
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: buried her there on the way to Ephrath (that is, Bethlehem).
Verse_Ch: 48:8 以色列看见约瑟的两个儿子，就说，这两个是谁？ ###EN### And when Israel saw Joseph's sons, he said, Who are these?
Verse_Ch: 48:9 约瑟对他父亲说，他们是神在这里赐给我的儿子。以色列说，请你领他们到我跟前，我要给他们祝福。 ###EN### And Joseph said to his father, They are my sons, whom God has given to me here. And he said, Bring them to me, that I may bless them.
Verse_Ch: 48:10 以色列年纪老迈，眼睛昏花，不能看见；约瑟领他们挨近他，他就和他们亲嘴，抱着他们。 ###EN### Now the eyes of Israel were dim with age, and he could not see. So Joseph brought them near to him, and he kissed them and embraced them.
Verse_Ch: 48:11 以色列对约瑟说，我想不到得见你的面，不料，神又使我得见你的后裔。 ###EN### And Israel said to Joseph, I never expected to see your face, and now God has let me see your seed also.
Verse_Ch: 48:12 约瑟把两个儿子从以色列两膝中领出来，自己面伏于地下拜。 ###EN### And Joseph brought them out from between his knees and bowed himself with his face to the ground.
Verse_Ch: 48:13 随后约瑟又拉着他们两个，以法莲在他的右手里，对着以色列的左手；玛拿西在他的左手里，对着以色列的右手；领他们挨近以色列。 ###EN### And Joseph took them both, Ephraim in his right hand toward Israel's left hand and Manasseh in his left hand toward Israel's right hand, and brought them near
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: to him.
Verse_Ch: 48:14 但以色列伸出右手来，按在以法莲的头上(以法莲乃是次子，)又剪搭过左手来，按在玛拿西的头上(玛拿西原是长子。) ###EN### But Israel stretched out his right hand and laid it upon Ephraim's head-although he was the younger-and his left hand upon Manasseh's head, guiding his
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: hands with insight, even though Manasseh was the firstborn.
Verse_Ch: 48:15 他就给约瑟祝福说，愿我祖亚伯拉罕和我父以撒行事为人都在祂面前的神，就是一生牧养我直到今日的神， ###EN### And he blessed Joseph and said, The God before whom my fathers Abraham and Isaac walked, The God who has shepherded me all my life to this day,
Verse_Ch: 48:16 那救赎我脱离一切患难的使者，赐福与这两个少年人。愿他们归在我的名下，和我祖亚伯拉罕、我父以撒的名下。又愿他们在这地生养众多。 ###EN### The Angel who has redeemed me from all evil, bless the boys; And may my name be named on them, and the name of my fathers Abraham and Isaac; And
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: may they be a teeming multitude in the midst of the earth.
Verse_Ch: 48:17 约瑟见他父亲把右手按在以法莲的头上，就不喜悦，便提起他父亲的手，要从以法莲的头上挪到玛拿西的头上。 ###EN### And when Joseph saw that his father laid his right hand upon the head of Ephraim, it displeased him; and he took hold of his father's hand to remove it from
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: Ephraim's head onto Manasseh's head.
Verse_Ch: 48:18 约瑟对他父亲说，我父，不是这样。这个才是长子，求你把右手按在他的头上。 ###EN### And Joseph said to his father, Not so, my father, for this is the firstborn. Put your right hand upon his head.
Verse_Ch: 48:19 他父亲不肯，说，我知道，我儿，我知道。他也必成为一族，也必昌大。只是他的弟弟将来比他还大；他弟弟的后裔必成为多族。 ###EN### But his father refused and said, I know, my son, I know. He also will become a people, and he also will be great. However, his younger brother will become
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: greater than he, and his seed will become a multitude of nations.
Verse_Ch: 48:20 当日以色列给他们祝福说，以色列人必指着你们祝福说，愿神使你如以法莲、玛拿西一样。于是立以法莲在玛拿西之前。 ###EN### And he blessed them that day, saying, By you Israel will bless, saying, God make you like Ephraim and like Manasseh. Thus he set Ephraim before Manasseh.
Verse_Ch: 48:21 以色列又对约瑟说，看哪，我快要死了，但神必与你们同在，领你们回到你们列祖之地。 ###EN### And Israel said to Joseph, Now I am about to die, but God will be with you and will bring you again to the land of your fathers.
Verse_Ch: 48:22 并且我从前用刀用弓，从亚摩利人手里夺取的那块地，我都赐给你，使你比众弟兄多得一分。 ###EN### Moreover I have given to you one portion more than your brothers, which I took out of the hand of the Amorite with my sword and with my bow.
Chapter_Header: 49
Verse_Ch: 49:1 雅各叫了他的儿子们来，说，你们都来聚集，我好把你们日后必遇的事告诉你们。 ###EN### And Jacob called to his sons and said, Gather yourselves together that I may tell you what will happen to you in the last days.
Verse_Ch: 49:2 雅各的儿子们哪，你们要聚集而听，听你们父亲以色列的话。 ###EN### Assemble yourselves, and listen, O sons of Jacob; Yes, listen to Israel your father.
Verse_Ch: 49:3 流便哪，你是我的长子，是我的能力，我强壮时首生的，本当尊荣居首，权力也居首。 ###EN### Reuben, you are my firstborn, My might and the beginning of my strength, Preeminent in dignity and preeminent in power.
Verse_Ch: 49:4 但你的情欲沸溢如水，你必不得居首；因为你上了你父亲的床，污秽了我的榻。 ###EN### Boiling over like water, you will not have the preeminence, Because you went up to your father's bed; Then you defiled it-he went up to my couch.
Verse_Ch: 49:5 西缅和利未是弟兄；他们的刀剑是强暴的器械。 ###EN### Simeon and Levi are brothers; Weapons of violence are their swords.
Verse_Ch: 49:6 我的魂哪，不要与他们共同商议；我的荣耀阿，不要与他们联合聚集；因为他们趁怒杀害人命，任意砍断牛腿大筋。 ###EN### Come not into their council, O my soul; Be not united with their assembly, O my glory; For in their anger they slew men, And in their self-will they hamstrung oxen.
Verse_Ch: 49:7 他们的怒气暴烈可咒，他们的忿恨残忍可诅；我必使他们分居在雅各家，散住在以色列地。 ###EN### Cursed be their anger, for it is fierce; And their wrath, for it is cruel: I will divide them in Jacob, And scatter them in Israel.
Verse_Ch: 49:8 犹大阿，你弟兄们必赞美你；你手必掐住仇敌的颈项；你父亲的儿子们必向你下拜。 ###EN### Judah, your brothers will praise you; Your hand will be on the neck of your enemies; Your father's sons will bow down before you.
Verse_Ch: 49:9 犹大是个小狮子；我儿阿，你抓了食便上山去。他蹲伏如公狮，又如母狮，谁敢惹他？ ###EN### Judah is a young lion; From the prey, my son, you have gone up. He couches, he stretches out like a lion, And like a lioness; who will rouse him up?
Verse_Ch: 49:10 权杖必不离犹大，王杖必不离他两脚之间，直到细罗来到，万民都必归顺。 ###EN### The scepter will not depart from Judah, Nor the ruler's staff from between his feet, Until Shiloh comes, And to Him shall be the obedience of the peoples.
Verse_Ch: 49:11 犹大把小驴拴在葡萄树上，把驴驹拴在美好的葡萄树上。他在葡萄酒中洗了衣服，在葡萄汁中洗了袍褂。 ###EN### Binding his foal to the vine, And his donkey's colt to the choice vine, He washes his garment in wine, And his robe in the blood of grapes.
Verse_Ch: 49:12 他的眼睛因酒红润；他的牙齿因奶白亮。 ###EN### Dark are his eyes with wine, And white are his teeth with milk.
Verse_Ch: 49:13 西布伦必住在海边，必成为停船的海口；他的境界必延到西顿。 ###EN### Zebulun will dwell at the shore of the sea, And he will be a shore for ships, And his flank will be toward Sidon.
Verse_Ch: 49:14 以萨迦是个强壮的驴，卧在羊圈之间。 ###EN### Issachar is a strong donkey, Couching between the sheepfolds.
Verse_Ch: 49:15 他看安息之处为佳，看那地为美，便低肩背重，成为服苦的仆人。 ###EN### And he saw a resting place that was good And the land that was pleasant, And he bowed his shoulder to bear, And became a task worker to bring tribute.
Verse_Ch: 49:16 但必判断他的民，作以色列支派之一。 ###EN### Dan will judge his people, As one of the tribes of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 49:17 但必作道上的蛇，路中的虺，咬伤马蹄，使骑马的向后坠落。 ###EN### Dan will be a serpent in the way, A viper on the path, That bites the horse's heels, So that his rider falls backward.
Verse_Ch: 49:18 耶和华阿，我向来等候你的救恩。 ###EN### I have waited for Your salvation, O Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 49:19 迦得必被追击者追击，他却要追击他们的脚跟。 ###EN### Gad, raiders will raid him, But he will raid at their heel.
Verse_Ch: 49:20 亚设的食物丰美，他必出君王的美味。 ###EN### Asher's food will be rich, And he will yield royal dainties.
Verse_Ch: 49:21 拿弗他利是被释放的母鹿，他出嘉美的言语。 ###EN### Naphtali is a hind let loose; He gives beautiful words.
Verse_Ch: 49:22 约瑟是多结果子的树枝，是泉旁多结果子的枝子；他的枝条探出墙外。 ###EN### Joseph is a fruitful bough, A fruitful bough by a fountain; His branches run over the wall.
Verse_Ch: 49:23 弓箭手将他苦害，向他射箭，逼迫他。 ###EN### The archers bitterly attacked him, And shot at him and harassed him;
Verse_Ch: 49:24 但他的弓仍旧坚硬，他的手臂健壮敏捷；这是因雅各之大能者的手，那里有以色列的牧者，以色列的石头。 ###EN### But his bow remained firm, And the arms of his hands were agile, By the hands of the Mighty One of Jacob-From there is the Shepherd, the stone of Israel -
Verse_Ch: 49:25 你父亲的神必帮助你；那全足者必将天上所有的福，地下深渊所藏的福，以及生产乳养的福，都赐给你。 ###EN### From the God of your father, who will help you, And from the All-sufficient One, who will bless you With blessings of heaven above, Blessings of the deep that lies
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: beneath, Blessings of the breasts and of the womb.
Verse_Ch: 49:26 你父亲所祝的福，胜过我祖先所祝的福，直达到永世山岭的至极边界；这些福必降在约瑟的头上，临到那与他弟兄迥别之人的头顶。 ###EN### The blessings of your father surpass The blessings of my ancestors To the utmost bound of the everlasting hills. They will be on the head of Joseph, And on the
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: crown of the head of the one who was separate from his brothers.
Verse_Ch: 49:27 便雅悯是个撕掠的狼，早晨吃他所掠夺的，晚上分他所掳获的。 ###EN### Benjamin is a ravenous wolf, In the morning devouring the prey And in the evening dividing the spoil.
Verse_Ch: 49:28 这一切就是以色列的十二支派；这也是他们的父亲祝福他们时，对他们所说的话。他为他们所祝的福，都是按着各人的福分。 ###EN### All these are the twelve tribes of Israel, and this is what their father spoke to them when he blessed them; he blessed them, each one according to his blessing.
Verse_Ch: 49:29 他又嘱咐他们说，我将要归到我本民那里，你们要将我葬在赫人以弗仑田间的洞里，与我祖我父在一处， ###EN### And he charged them and said to them, I am being gathered to my people. Bury me with my fathers in the cave that is in the field of Ephron the Hittite,
Verse_Ch: 49:30 就是在迦南地的幔利前、麦比拉田间的洞里；那洞和田是亚伯拉罕向赫人以弗仑买来为业，作坟地的。 ###EN### In the cave that is in the field of Machpelah, which is before Mamre in the land of Canaan, which Abraham bought along with the field from Ephron the Hittite for
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: the possession of a burial place -
Verse_Ch: 49:31 他们在那里葬了亚伯拉罕和他的妻子撒拉，又在那里葬了以撒和他的妻子利百加；我也在那里葬了利亚。 ###EN### There they buried Abraham and Sarah his wife, there they buried Isaac and Rebekah his wife, and there I buried Leah -
Verse_Ch: 49:32 那块田和田间的洞，原是向赫人买的。 ###EN### The field and the cave that is in it, purchased from the children of Heth.
Verse_Ch: 49:33 雅各嘱咐众子完毕，就把脚收在床上，气绝而死，归到他本民那里去了。 ###EN### And when Jacob had finished charging his sons, he gathered up his feet into the bed and expired, and he was gathered to his people.
Chapter_Header: 50
Verse_Ch: 50:1 约瑟伏在他父亲的面上，为他哀哭，与他亲嘴。 ###EN### Then Joseph fell upon his father's face and wept over him and kissed him.
Verse_Ch: 50:2 约瑟吩咐伺候他的医生，用香料薰殓他父亲，医生就用香料薰殓了以色列。 ###EN### And Joseph commanded his servants the physicians to embalm his father. So the physicians embalmed Israel.
Verse_Ch: 50:3 用香料薰殓的时间是四十天；那四十天满了，埃及人为他哀哭了七十天。 ###EN### And forty days were spent for this, for this is the time to be spent for embalming. And the Egyptians wept for him seventy days.
Verse_Ch: 50:4 为他哀哭的日子过了，约瑟对法老家中的人说，我若在你们眼前蒙恩，请你们报告法老说， ###EN### And when the days of weeping for him had passed, Joseph spoke to the house of Pharaoh, saying, If I have found favor in your eyes, please speak in the hearing
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: of Pharaoh, saying,
Verse_Ch: 50:5 我父亲快要死的时候，叫我起誓说，你要将我葬在迦南地，在我为自己所掘的坟墓里。现在求你让我上去葬我父亲，以后我必回来。 ###EN### My father made me swear, saying, Now I am about to die; in my grave which I dug for myself in the land of Canaan, there shall you bury me. Now therefore
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: please let me go up and bury my father; then I will return.
Verse_Ch: 50:6 法老说，你可以上去，照着你父亲叫你起的誓，将他葬埋。 ###EN### And Pharaoh said, Go up, and bury your father, as he made you swear.
Verse_Ch: 50:7 于是约瑟上去葬他父亲；与他一同上去的，有法老的众臣仆，和法老家中的长老，并埃及地的众长老， ###EN### And Joseph went up to bury his father; and all the servants of Pharaoh went up with him, the elders of his house and all the elders of the land of Egypt,
Verse_Ch: 50:8 还有约瑟的全家，和他的弟兄们，并他父亲的眷属；只有他们的妇人孩子，和羊群牛群，都留在歌珊地。 ###EN### And all the house of Joseph and his brothers and his father's household; they left only their little ones and their flocks and their herds in the land of Goshen.
Verse_Ch: 50:9 又有车辆马兵，和他一同上去；那一帮人甚多， ###EN### And chariots also went up with him, as well as horsemen; and it was a very great company.
Verse_Ch: 50:10 他们到了约但河外亚达的禾场，就在那里大大的号啕痛哭；约瑟为他父亲哀哭了七天。 ###EN### And they came to the threshing floor of Atad, which is beyond the Jordan, and they lamented there with a very great and grievous lamentation; and he observed
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: seven days of mourning for his father.
Verse_Ch: 50:11 住在那地的迦南人，看见亚达禾场上的哀悼，就说，这是埃及人一场大的哀悼。因此那地方名叫亚伯麦西，是在约但河外。 ###EN### And when the inhabitants of the land, the Canaanites, saw the mourning at the threshing floor of Atad, they said, This is a grievous mourning for the Egyptians.
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: Therefore the name of it was called Abel-mizraim, which is beyond the Jordan.
Verse_Ch: 50:12 雅各的儿子们，就遵着他们父亲所吩咐的，给他办了， ###EN### And thus his sons did to him as he commanded them;
Verse_Ch: 50:13 把他搬到迦南地，葬在幔利前、麦比拉田间的洞里；那洞和田是亚伯拉罕向赫人以弗仑买来为业，作坟地的。 ###EN### And his sons carried him into the land of Canaan and buried him in the cave of the field of Machpelah before Mamre, which Abraham had bought with the field
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: for a possession of a burial place from Ephron the Hittite.
Verse_Ch: 50:14 约瑟葬了他父亲以后，就和众弟兄，并一切同他上去葬他父亲的人，都回埃及去了。 ###EN### And after he had buried his father, Joseph returned into Egypt, he and his brothers and all who went up with him to bury his father.
Verse_Ch: 50:15 约瑟的哥哥们见父亲死了，就说，或者约瑟会怀恨我们，照着我们从前待他一切的恶，足足的报复我们。 ###EN### And when Joseph's brothers saw that their father was dead, they said, What if Joseph bears a grudge against us and pays us back in full for all the evil which we
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: did to him?
Verse_Ch: 50:16 他们就打发人去见约瑟，说，你父亲未死以前吩咐说， ###EN### And they sent a message to Joseph, saying, Your father charged before he died, saying,
Verse_Ch: 50:17 你们要对约瑟这样说：从前你哥哥们恶待你，求你饶恕他们的过犯和罪。如今求你饶恕你父亲的神之仆人的过犯。他们对约瑟说这话，约瑟就哭了。 ###EN### Thus shall you say to Joseph, Please forgive the transgression of your brothers and their sin, for they did you wrong. So now please forgive the transgression of
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: the servants of the God of your father. And Joseph wept when they spoke to him.
Verse_Ch: 50:18 他的哥哥们又来俯伏在他面前，说，我们是你的仆人。 ###EN### And his brothers also went and fell down before him and said, We are here as your servants.
Verse_Ch: 50:19 约瑟对他们说，不要害怕，我岂能代替神呢？ ###EN### And Joseph said to them, Do not be afraid, for am I in the place of God?
Verse_Ch: 50:20 从前你们的意思是要害我，但神的意思原是好的，要使许多人存活，成就今日的光景。 ###EN### Even though you intended evil against me, God intended it for good, to do as it is this day, to preserve alive a numerous people.
Verse_Ch: 50:21 所以现在你们不要害怕，我必养活你们，和你们的妇人孩子。于是约瑟用亲切的话安慰他们。 ###EN### Now therefore do not be afraid; I will sustain you and your little ones. And he comforted them and spoke kindly to them.
Verse_Ch: 50:22 约瑟和他父亲的眷属，都住在埃及；约瑟活了一百一十岁。 ###EN### And Joseph dwelt in Egypt, he and his father's household; and Joseph lived one hundred ten years.
Verse_Ch: 50:23 约瑟得见以法莲第三代的子孙。玛拿西之子玛吉的众子，也养在约瑟的膝上。 ###EN### And Joseph saw Ephraim's children of the third generation; the children of Machir the son of Manasseh were also born on Joseph's knees.
Verse_Ch: 50:24 约瑟对他弟兄们说，我快要死了，但神必眷顾你们，领你们出这地，上到祂起誓要赐给亚伯拉罕、以撒、雅各之地。 ###EN### And Joseph said to his brothers, I am about to die, but God will surely visit you and bring you up out of this land to the land which He swore to Abraham, to Isaac,
UNCLASSIFIED_GENERAL: and to Jacob.
Verse_Ch: 50:25 约瑟叫以色列的子孙起誓，说，神必定看顾你们；你们要把我的骸骨从这里带上去。 ###EN### And Joseph made the children of Israel swear, saying, God will surely visit you, and you shall bring my bones up from here.
Verse_Ch: 50:26 约瑟死了，正一百一十岁。人用香料将他薰殓了，把他放在棺材里，停在埃及。 ###EN### And Joseph died, being one hundred ten years old; and they embalmed him, and he was put in a coffin in Egypt.
